NSV_1.1.1	viśva vyāpī viśva śaktiḥ pinākī ciśva īśānaḥ viśva kṛt viśva mūrtiḥ viśvajñātā viśva saṃhāra kārī viśvārādhyaḥ rādhayatvīptsitam naḥ yat akṣapādaḥ pravaraḥ munīnām śamāya śāstram jagataḥ jagāda ku tārkikā jñāna nirāsa hetuḥ kariṣyate tasya mayā prabandhaḥ puṇya kara pura ślādhyaḥ veda śāstra artha kovidaḥ gambhīra vaṃśa jaḥ cakre nyāya vārtika saṃgraham 
NSV_1.1.2^1	 tat khalu prameya tattva jñāna anantaram utpadyate na vā iti ākāṃākṣāyām āha tattva jñānāt iti duḥkha janma pravṛtti doṣa mithyā jñānānām uttarottara apāye tad anantara abhāvāt niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ iti sūtreṇa gatena sambandhaḥ atra ātma ādi apavarga paryantam prameyam jñeyam tat mithyā jñānam aneka prakāram vidyate sa ātmani śarīre tāvat ātmā na asti iti anātmani ātmā iti evam manaḥ paryanteṣu pañcasu prameyeṣu mithyājñāna bhedāḥ ūhyāḥ duḥkhe sukham iti atrāṇe trāṇam iti sa bhaye nirbhayam iti jugutsite hitam iti hātavye apratihātavyam iti atha pravṛti ādi apavarga anteṣu prameyeṣu mithyājñāna nivṛttau na asti karma na asti karma phalam iti doṣeṣu na ayam doṣa nimittaḥ saṃsāraḥ iti pretyabhāve na asti jantuḥ jīvaḥ satvaḥ ātmā vā yaḥ preyāt pretya ca bhavet iti apavargaḥ bhīṣaṇaḥ khalu ayam sarva upaśamaḥ sarva viprayoge apavarge bahu ca bhadrakam lupyate iti etasmāt mithyājñānāt anukūleṣu rāgaḥ pratikūleṣu ca dveṣaḥ ityādayaḥ doṣāḥ bhavanti 
NSV_1.1.2^2	 doṣa prayukta śarīra vāc manobhiḥ hiṃsā steya pratiṣiddha maithuna ādikam ācaran dharme adharmān sañcinoti pravṛtti sādhana tvāt tau= imau dharma adharmau pravṛtti śabdena ucyete seya pravṛttiḥ kutsitasya abhisūcitasya janmanaḥ kāraṇam bhavati janma punar ca indriya viṣaya buddhīnām nikāya viśiṣṭaḥ prādurbhāvaḥ tasmin sati duḥkham mithyājñāna ādayaḥ duḥkhāntāḥ dharmāḥ avicchedena eva pravartamānā saṃsāra hetavaḥ yadā ātma ādi prameya tattva jñānāt mithyājñānam apaiti mithyājñāna apāye doṣāḥ apayānti doṣa apāye pravṛttiḥ apaiti pravṛtti apāye janma apaiti janma apāye duḥkham apaiti duḥkha abhāve ātyantika apavargaḥ mahā parama ānanda parama śiva bhāvaḥ niḥśreyasam iti tattva jñānam tu mithyājñāna viparyayeṇa vyākhyeyam 
NSV_1.1.3–1.1.4	 trividhā ca asya śāstrasya pravṛttiḥ uddeśaḥ lakṣaṇam parīkṣā ca iti tatra nāmadheyena padārthānām abhidhānam uddeśaḥ uddiṣṭasya tattva vyavasthāpakaḥ dharmaḥ lakṣaṇam lakṣitasya ca lakṣaṇam upapadyate na vā iti pramāṇaiḥ avadhāraṇam parīkṣā atha uddiṣṭasya vibhāga vacanam avāntara uddeśaḥ pratyakṣa anumāna upamāna śabdāḥ pramāṇāni akṣasya akṣasya prativiṣayam vṛttiḥ pratyakṣam vṛttiḥ sannikarṣaḥ jñānam vā yadā sannikarṣaḥ tadā jñānam pramitiḥ phalam yadā jñānam tadā hāna upādāna upekṣā buddhayaḥ phalam iti mitena liṅgena liṅginaḥ arthasya paścāt jñānam anumānam upamānam sāmīpya jñānam yathā gauḥ evam gavayaḥ iti sāmīpyam tu avayava sāmānya yogaḥ śabdaḥ śabdyate anena arthaḥ abhidhīyate jñāpyate pramīyate anena iti karaṇa artha abhidhānaḥ pramāṇa śabdaḥ ihi vibhaktānām pramāṇānām pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam āha indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam jñānam avyapadeśyam avyabhicāri vyavasāya ātmakam pratyakṣam indriyasya artha sannikarṣāt yad artha viṣayam jñānam utpadyate tad pratyakṣam indriyāṇi vakṣyamāṇāni arthāḥ ca ghaṭa ādayaḥ 
NSV_1.1.5^1	 atha tad pūrvakam trividham anumānam pūrvavat śeṣavat sāmānyatodṛṣṭam ca atha iti ānantarye anumāna viśeśṇa artham sūtram anumānam tat pūrvakam iti anena samāna asamāna jātīyebhyaḥ vyavacchidyate tat ca te ca tāni ca tat tat pūrvam yasya tat idam tat pūrvakam yadā tāni pūrvam yasya iti vigrahaḥ tadā samasta pramāṇa abhisambandhāt sarva pramāṇa pūrvaka tvam anumānasya varṇitam bhavati pāramparyeṇa punar tad pratyakṣaḥ eva avatiṣṭhate iti tad pūrvaka tvam anumānasya uktam bhavati yadā ca te pūrve yasya iti vigrahaḥ tadā liṅga liṅginoḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhūtayoḥ liṅga darśanam ekam pratyakṣam liṅgi darśanam dvitīyam te dve pratyakṣe pūrvam yasya anumānasya tat idam tat pūrvakam kaḥ punar anumāna arthaḥ anumīyate anena iti karaṇa arthaḥ kim punar anumānasya phalam anumeya viṣayā pratipattiḥ yadi pratyakṣa pūrvakam anumānam bhavati tahri smṛti hetau bhāvanā ākhye saṃskāre nirṇaye vā anumānam prasajyeta 
NSV_1.1.5^2	 tayoḥ api pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvāt iti na eṣa doṣaḥ vijñānasya adhikṛta tvāt tat ca anumānam pūrvavat śeṣavat sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam ca iti trividham tatra pūrvavat iti yatra kāraṇena kāryam anumīyate yathā medhā unnatyā vṛṣṭiḥ bhaviṣyati iti atra pūrva śabdena kāraṇam abhidhīyate tat atiriktam kāryam śeṣavat iti kārya mātram atra śeṣa śabdena abhidhīyate tatas ca śeṣavat nāma kāryeṇa liṅgena kāraṇam anumīyate tat yathā nadī pūreṇa vṛṣṭi anumānam iti sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam nāma akārya kāraṇībhūtena yatra avinābhāvinā liṅgena dharmī gamyate yathā balākayā salila anumānam iti pūrvavat śeṣavat sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam iti padatra yoktyā eva traividhye trividham iti upādānam niyama artham anekadhā bhinnasya trividhena eva pūrva pada ādinā saṅgrahaḥ iti sat viṣayam ca pratyakṣam sat asat viṣayam anumānam kasmātttraikālya grahaṇāt 
NSV_1.1.6	 atha upamānam prasiddha sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam upamānam prajñātena sāmānyāt prajñāpanīyasya jñāpanam upamānam iti yathā gauḥ evam gavayaḥ iti kim punar atra upamānena kriyate saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandha pratipattiḥ yathā gauḥ evam gavayaḥ iti upamāna vākye prayukte gavā samāna artham indriya sannikarṣāt upalabhamānaḥ asya ayam gavaya śabdaḥ saṃjñā iti saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandham pratipadyate 
NSV_1.1.7	 atha śabdaḥ āpta upadeśaḥ śabdaḥ na śabda mātram iti sūtra arthaḥ āptaḥ khalu sākṣātkṛta dharmāḥ sākṣātkaraṇam arthasya āptiḥ tayā saha vartate iti āptaḥ nanu evam sati svarga apavarga devatā ādīni na kaścid paśyati iti tad pratipādakaḥ vyavahāraḥ na syāt iti ced na svarga apavarga ādīnām api kasyacid pratyakṣa tvāt svarga ādayaḥ kasyacid pratyakṣāḥ eva bhavanti sāmānya viśeṣava tvāt āśrita tvāt paramārtha tvāt vastu tvāt āgama viṣaya tvāt ca evam ca yasya pratyakṣāḥ svarga ādayaḥ tasya āptasya upadeśaḥ śabdaḥ iti lakṣaṇam yuktam eva 
NSV_1.1.8	 sa dvividhaḥ dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa artha tvāt yasya iha dṛśyate arthaḥ sa dṛṣṭaḥ yasya amutra pratīyate arthaḥ saḥ adṛṣṭaḥ evam ṛṣi laukika vākyānām vibhāgaḥ iti kimartham punar idam ucyate anena pramāṇena artha jātam yathāvat parijñāyamānam apavargāya bhavati anavagamyamānam tu saṃsārāya iti etad artha prakāśana artham idam sūtram 
NSV_1.1.9^1	 atha prameyam ātma śarīra indriya artha buddhi manaḥ pravṛtti doṣa pretya bhāva phala duḥkha apavargāḥ tu prameyam yathāvacanam vigrahaḥ anyat api prameyam asti yasya tatu ajñānāt niḥśreyasam bhavati tat idam prameyam iti tuśabdena jñāpayati atra ātmā sarvasya draṣṭā sarvasya bhoktā tasya bhoga āyatanam śarīram bhoga sādhanāni indriyāṇi bhoktavyāḥ arthāḥ bhogaḥ buddhiḥ sarva viṣayam antaḥkaraṇam manaḥ śarīra indriya artha buddhi sukha duḥkha vedanānām nivṛtti kāraṇam pravṛttiḥ doṣāḥ rāga ādayaḥ ātmanaḥ pūrva pūrva śarīrāt viyuktasya yāvat apavarga śarīram uttarottara sambandhaḥ pretyabhāvaḥ 
NSV_1.1.9^2	 sa sādhana sukha duḥkha upabhogaḥ phalam vādhana alakṣaṇam duḥkham janma maraṇa prabandha ucchedanāt sarva duḥkha prahāṇam apavargaḥ sukham punar kasmāt asminna uktam vairāgya jñāpana artham katham mokṣamāṇaḥ sarvam duḥkham bhāvayet iti tasya duḥkha bhāvanā arthaḥ sukhasya anapadeśaḥ iti duḥkha paribhāvanayā anāsaktiḥ viṣayeṣu jāyate anāsaktyā punarbhava prārthanā lakṣaṇā tṛṣṇā vicchidyate tṛṣṇā vicchedāt punarbhava sādhana anupādānam tad anupādānāt kevalam utpannānām upabhogena kṣayaḥ tatas ca apavargaḥ iti etāvat artha pratipādana artha m anamidhānam sukhasya iti 
NSV_1.1.10	 tatra ātmā pratyakṣataḥ na gṛhyate kim āpta upadeśa mātrāt pratipattavyaḥ iti kim vā anumānāt pratipattavyaḥ iti icchā dveṣa prayatna sukha duḥkha jñānāni ātmanaḥ liṅgam iti yat jātīya arthasya sannikarṣāt sukham ātma upalabdhavān tat jātīyam artham punar punar paśyan= upādātum icchati sā iyam ādātum icchā ekasya aneka artha darśinaḥ darśana pratisandhānāt bhavati liṅgam ātmanaḥ yathā yat jātīyaḥ arthaḥ sukha hetuḥ prasiddhaḥ tat jātīyam artham prāptum prayatate tathā saḥ ayam prayatna upi ekam aneka artha darśinam anumāpayati etena duḥkha hetau= api prayatnaḥ vyākhyātaḥ sukha duḥkha smṛtyā ca ayam tad sādhanam ādadhānaḥ sukha duḥkhe upalabhate iti atas sukha duḥkhe api tad tādhana smartuḥ ātmanaḥ liṅgam paratantram aguṇa tvāt rūpa ādi vat iti ātma siddhiḥ 
NSV_1.1.11–1.1.12	 atha ātmanaḥ bhoga āyatanam ceṣṭa indriya artha āśrayaḥ śarīram kā punar iyam ceṣṭā hita ahita prāpti parihāra arthaḥ parispandaḥ tasya āśrayaḥ śarīram katham indriyāṇām śarīram āśrayaḥ śarīra anugraha upaghāta anuvidhāyit tvāt teṣām katham artha āśrayaḥ artha nimitta sukha saṃvedana āyatana tvāt śarīrasya kāni punar bhoga sādhanāni ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuḥ tvac śrotrāṇi indriyāṇi bhūtebhyaḥ nanu na idam indriyāṇāḥ lakṣaṇa sūtram indriya uddeśa mātra avagamāt sva viṣaya grahaṇe kāraṇāni tāni indriyāṇi iti ghrāṇa ādīnām upadeśena eva lakṣaṇasya ukta tvāt katham jidhrati anena iti ghrāṇam rasayati anena iti rasanam caṣṭe anena iti cakṣuḥ tvac sthānam indriyam tvac tvac saṃvaraṇaḥ iti dhātuḥ saṃvrīyate anena iti tvac śrotram śṛṇoti anena iti kṛtvā śrotram iti bhūtebhyaḥ iti nānā prakṛtīnām eṣām satām viṣaya niyamaḥ bhavet na eka prakṛtīnām iti darśayati 
NSV_1.1.13–1.1.14	 kāni punar indriya kāraṇāni āha pṛthivī āpaḥ tejaḥ vāyuḥ ākāśam iti bhūtāni indriya prakṛti tvam bhūta lakṣaṇam ime khalu gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabdāḥ pṛthivī ādi guṇāḥ tad arthāḥ atra pṛthivī ādīni guṇāḥ ca iti ca arthe dvandvaḥ pṛthivī ādi grahaṇena pṛthivī ap tejāṃsi bāhya karaṇa grāhyāṇi vyapadiśyante guṇa grahaṇena ca sarve āśritaḥ guṇaḥ iti saṃkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāga paratva aparatva sneha drava tva vega saṃskāra karma sāmānya viśeṣāḥ upādīyante anāśritaḥ ca samavāyaḥ tad dharma tvāt guṇaḥ iti gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabdāḥ tarhi pṛthak na vaktavyāḥ guṇa grahaṇena grahaṇāt iti na anya artha tvāt gandha ādīnām pṛthak abhidhānam indriya viśeṣa niyama khyāpana artham ghrāṇa ādīni hi indriyāṇi gandha ādiṣu niyatāni anyatra ca aniyatāni tatra pṛthivī ap tejāṃsi cakṣu spārśanayoḥ grāhyāṇi śeṣaḥ ca guṇa rāśiḥ sattā guṇa tve tu sarva indriya grāhye samavāya abhāvau ca 
NSV_1.1.15	 atha buddheḥ avasara prāptāyāḥ lakṣaṇam āha buddhiḥ upalabdhiḥ jñānam iti anarthāntaram etaiḥ paryāya śabdaiḥ yaḥ abhidhīyate padārthaḥ sā buddhiḥ iti paryāya śabdāḥ katham lakṣaṇam vyavaccheda hetu tvāt yat āhuḥ buddheḥ jñānam vṛttiḥ ātmanaḥ upalabdhiḥ iti tad nirākaraṇa artham ca idam sūtram samāna arthāḥ ete śabdāḥ na ca samāna arthaiḥ śabdaiḥ artha bhedaḥ kathayitum yuktaḥ iti 
NSV_1.1.16	 atha manasaḥ lakṣaṇam āha yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ liṅgam yugapad khalu ghrāṇa ādīnām ca sannikarṣeṣu satsu yadi ugapad jñānam na utpadyate tena anumīyate asti tad indriya saṃyoga sahakāri nimitta antaram avyāpi yasya sannidhānā asannidhāna anuvidhānāt jñānasya utpati anutpattī bhavataḥ iti kutas kāraṇa vaikalye kārya pratibandha darśanāt iti manasaḥ siddhiḥ nanu yugapad anutpattiḥ jñāna dharmaḥ tat katham manasaḥ liṅgam  na jñānānām eva pakṣīkaraṇāt katham rūpa ādi jñānāni cakṣuḥ ādi vyatirekaṇa adhiṣṭhāyaka antara apekṣāṇi ayugapad utpadyamāna tvāt śilpa hasta ādi adhiṣṭhāyaka antara apekṣa vāsya ādi janya kriyā vat yat adhiṣṭhāyaka antaram tat manaḥ iti 
NSV_1.1.17	 atha pravṛtti lakṣaṇam pravṛttiḥ vāc buddhi śarīra ārambhaḥ manaḥ atra buddhiḥ iti abhipretam budhyate anena iti buddhiḥ śarīreṇa vācā manasā ca ārambhaḥ audāsīnyapracyutiḥ pravṛttiḥ sā punar puṇyā ca apuṇyā ca pratyekam daśavidhāḥ puṇyā kāyena paritrāṇam dānam paricaraṇam iti vācā satyam hitam priyam svādhyāyaḥ iti manasā dayā dhanāspṛhā śraddhā ca iti viparyayeṇa pāpāḥ daśavidhā eva sā iyam pravṛttiḥ kṣaṇikā ca satī na janma hetuḥ iti yuktam tatas ca dvitīya sūtra vyādhātaḥ na pravṛtti phale pravṛtti upacārāt pravṛtti sādhana tvāt dharma adharmau= atra pravṛttiḥ iti ucyete janya puṇyā puṇya dvārāḥ janma hetuḥ iti 
NSV_1.1.18–1.1.21	 atha doṣān āha pravartanā lakṣaṇāḥ doṣāḥ kā punar iyam pravartanā yathā avaśaḥ pravartate tam pravartamānam gaga ādayaḥ pravartayanti iti sā iyam pravṛtti hetu tvāt pravartanā iti ucyate atha pretyabhāvam lakṣayati punar utpattiḥ pretyabhāvaḥ pūrva upatta śarīra ādi parityāgāt anya śarīra ādi upasampattiḥ pretyabhāvaḥ punar grahaṇam saṃsāra an ādi tva jñāpana artham saḥ ayam saṃsāraḥ kasya kimātmanaḥ manasaḥ vā iti yadā kriyām adhikṛtya ucyate tadā manasaḥ tat hi saṃsarati atha upabhogam adhikṛtya ucyate tadā tmanaḥ sa hi sukha duḥkhe upabhuṃkte pravṛtti doṣa janitaḥ arthaḥ phalam śarīra ādi janyam sarvam phalam dharma adharma pravartaka tvāt iti bādhanā lakṣaṇam duḥkham etat eva śarīra ādīnām bādhana anuṣaṅgāt duḥkham iti ucyate 
NSV_1.1.22	 tad atyanta vimokṣaḥ apavargaḥ tena śarīra ādinā duḥkhena atyanta vimuktiḥ apavargaḥ upāttasya janmanaḥ upabhogāt hānam anyasya ca dharma adharma ākhya kāraṇa abhāvāt anupādānam etām ātmanaḥ avasthām aparyantām apavargam vedayaṃte tad abhayam ajaram amṛtyu padam brahma kṣema prāptiḥ iti kecid ātyantika sukha abhivyaktim apavargam manvate tat na pramāṇa abhāvāt nanu āgamāt etat gamyate muktaḥ sukhī bhavati iti tarhi saḥ āgamaḥ vicāraṇīyaḥ kim ayam nityena sukhena yogam āha uta ātyantikena duḥkhena viyogamāhā iti dṛṣṭaḥ ca duḥkha abhāvepi sukha śabda prayogaḥ bahudhā tatas eva hi jvara ādibhiḥ viyuktā laukikāḥ ācakṣate sukhinaḥ saṃvṛttāḥ smaḥ iti tadvat āgamaḥ api duḥkha abhāve sukha śabdam prayuṅkte iti yuktam eva 
NSV_1.1.23^1	 samāna aneka dharma upapatteḥ vipratipatteḥ upalabdhi anupalabdhi avyavasthātaḥ ca viśeṣa apekṣaḥ vimarśaḥ saṃśayaḥ atra samāna dharma upapatteḥ aneka dharma upapatteḥ vipratipatteḥ ca trividhaḥ eva saṃśayaḥ iti itara pada viśeṣaṇāt bhavati sūtra arthaḥ atra samāna dharma ādibhyaḥ hi utpannaḥ viṣaya viśeṣam na avadhārayati yaḥ pratyayaḥ sa saṃśayaḥ iti saṃśaya lakṣaṇam atra samāna śabdaḥ sādṛśya vacanaḥ yathā yāvat aham arthau pūrvam adrākṣam tayoḥ yaḥ dharmaḥ ūrdhva tva ādi lakṣaṇaḥ vartete tena dharmeṇa sadṛśaḥ ayam dharmaḥ upalabhyate iti 
NSV_1.1.23^2	 tasya upapattiḥ adhyavasāyaḥ upalabdhiḥ iti arthaḥ saḥ ayam sādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ upalabhyamānaḥ nirṇāyakam ajānataḥ saṃśaya hetuḥ kim kevalaḥ iti na kim tarhi upalabdhi anupalabdhi avyavasthātaḥ ca kim etāvat mātram kāraṇam iti na iti āha viśeṣa apekṣaḥ iti samānam tu artham upalabhate upalabdhi anupalabdhī na vyavatiṣṭhete idam tathā na idam tathā iti vā viśeṣa ākāṅkṣā ca yadi bhavati atha sandehaḥ bhavati kim idam samastam kāraṇa mutā asamastam kāraṇam iti samastam iti brūmaḥ anyatama apāye saṃśaya adarśanāt 
NSV_1.1.23^3	 nānā artha avamarśanam vimarśanam saṃśītiḥ saṃśayaḥ bhāva sādhanam karaṇa sādhanam vā saṃśayyate anena ātmā iti etena aneka dharma upapatteḥ vipratipatteḥ ca iti vyākhyātam asādhāraṇa dharmaḥ aneka dharmaḥ iti anena samāsapadena abhidhīyate samāna asamāna ja tīya viśeṣa vyavacchedaka tvāt samāna jātīyam ca asamāna jātīyam ca anekam tasmāt anekasmāt viśeṣaḥ aneka dharmaḥ yathā śabde vibhāga ja tvāt dravyam guṇaḥ karma vā iti saṃśayaḥ na hi dravya guṇa karmaṇām anyatamam vibhāgāt jāyamānam dṛṣṭam vibhāga ja tvam śabdasya asādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ atas sarvatas vyāvṛtteḥ ayam saṃśaya hetuḥ vipratipatteḥ iti vyāhatam eka artha darśanam vipratipattiḥ vyāghātaḥ virodhaḥ asahabhāvaḥ iti yathā asatya ātmā iti ekam darśanam satyā tmā iti aparam darśanam na ca sadbhāva asadbhāvau saha ekatra bhavataḥ iti saṃśayaḥ iti saḥ ayam evaṃbhūtaḥ saṃśayaḥ vicāra aṅgatayā upādīyate saṃśaya vat viparyayaḥ api na vicāra aṅgam yathā sandigdhaḥ tad viśeṣa pratipattaye prayatate na evam viparyastaḥ iti atas vidyā anaṅga tvāt viparyayaḥ na abhidhīyate iti 
NSV_1.1.24	 yam artham adhikṛtya pravartate tad prayojanam vyavasāyaḥ adhikāraḥ kasya vyavasāyaḥ sukha duḥkha tad sādhanānām idam sukha sādhanam iti budhvā sukha āptaye prayatate idam duḥkha sādhanam iti vā adhigamya duḥkha hānāya iti sukha duḥkha āptihānābhyām ayam lokaḥ prasajyate iti sukha duḥkha apti hānī prayojanam iti anena sarva arthāḥ saṃgṛhyante 
NSV_1.1.25	 laukika parīkṣakāṇām yasmin= arthe buddhi sāmyam sa dṛṣṭāntaḥ buddhi sāmya viṣayaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ evam ca na ākāśa ādi avarodhaḥ yadi punar avadhāryate laukikānām parīkṣakāṇām ca yaḥ viṣayaḥ sa dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti alaukikaḥ arthaḥ na dṛṣṭānta ssyāt ākāśa ādiḥ iti udāharaṇa tvena tu laukika parīkṣaka buddhi viṣayasya abhidhānam iti 
NSV_1.1.26–1.1.27	 atha siddhāntaḥ tantra adhikaraṇa abhyupagama saṃsthitiḥ siddhāntaḥ idam itthaṃbhūtam ca iti anujñātam artha jātam siddham siddhasya saṃsthitiḥ itthaṃbhāva vyavasthā dharma niyamaḥ tantram itaretara abhisambaddhasya artha samūhasya upadeśa śa stram tantram adhikaraṇam eṣām arthānām te tantra adhikaraṇāḥ yaḥ arthaḥ na śāstrataḥ tasyāḥ abhyupapagamaḥ na siddhānte iti tantra bhedāt tu sa caturvidhaḥ sarva tantra pratitantra adhikaraṇa abhyupagama saṃsthiti artha antara bhāvāt etāḥ catasraḥ saṃsthitayaḥ artha antara bhūtāḥ 
NSV_1.1.28	 tāsām sarva tantra aviruddhaḥ tantre adhikṛtaḥ arthaḥ sarva tantra siddhāntaḥ sarveṣām sampratipatti viṣayaḥ sarva tantra siddhāntaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ yathā pramāṇāni prameya sādhanāni nanu dṛṣṭāntāt sarva tantra siddhāntaḥ na bhidyate apratipatti viṣayaḥ sādharmyāt iti bhidyate eva vādi prativādinoḥ eva prasiddhaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ na ca evam sarva tantra siddhāntaḥ iti 
NSV_1.1.29–1.1.30	 samāna tantra siddhaḥ paratantrā asiddhaḥ prati tantra siddhāntaḥ sāmānya viśeṣavatām niyamena abhyupagamaḥ siddhānte iti yathā bhautikāni indriyāṇi iti yogānām evam abhautikāni iti sāṃkhyānām eva bhavati yat siddhau= anya prakaraṇa siddhiḥ saḥ adhikaraṇa siddhāntaḥ vākya artha siddhau tad anuṣaṅgī yaḥ arthaḥ saḥ adhikaraṇa siddhāntaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ indriya vyatiriktaḥ jñātā darśana sparśanābhyām eka artha grahaṇāt iti atra anuṣaṅgiṇaḥ arthāḥ indriya nānā tvam niyata viṣayāṇi indriyāṇi jñātuḥ jñāna sādhanāni ityādayaḥ 
NSV_1.1.31–1.1.32	 aparīkṣita abhyupagamāt tad viśeṣa parīkṣaṇam abhyupagama siddhāntaḥ asūtritaḥ yaḥ arthaḥ śāstre ca abhyupagataḥ saḥ abhyupagama siddhāntaḥ yathā naiyāyikānām manaḥ indriyam iti vaiśeṣikāṇām naiyāyikānām ca śrotram ākāśam iti pratijñā hetu udāharaṇa upanaya nigamanāni avayavāḥ avayavānām vibhāga uddeśa artham sūtram anumāna vākyasya ca ete avayavāḥ bhavanti 
NSV_1.1.33–1.1.34	 teṣām sādhya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā prajñāpanīya dharma viśiṣṭaḥ dharmī sādhyaḥ tasya nirdeśaḥ parigraha vacanam asya udāharaṇam anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti udāharaṇa sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam hetuḥ udāharaṇena sādharmyam udāharaṇa sādharmyam yaḥ dharmaḥ sādhye bhavati tathābhūtaḥ eva udāharaṇe api iti na punar saḥ eva anya dharmasya anyatra aprasaṅgāt evaṃlakṣaṇāt udāharaṇa sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam sādhyasya prajñāpanam hetuḥ utpatti varmaka tvāt anityaḥ iti 
NSV_1.1.35	 kim tarhi tathā vaidharmyāt atra api udāharaṇa vaidharmyāt iti udāharaṇena eva vaidharmyam vācyam na anudāharaṇena iti vaidharmyam eva udāharaṇena na sādharmyam api iti udāharaṇam tu na idam nirātmakam jīvat śarīram nirātmaka tve ghaṭa ādi vat aprāṇa ādimattva prasaṅgāt tau= etau vītāvīta hetū lakṣaṇābhyām pṛthak abhihitau tatra sva rūpeṇa artha parīt cheka tvam vīta dharmaḥ avītaḥ punar para tattva pratiṣedhena eva pravartate iti ekasya vidhīyamānaḥ arthaḥ aparasya pratiṣidhyamānaḥ dvau= api vīta avītau= avyabhicārāt 
NSV_1.1.36–1.1.37	 sādhya sādharmyāt tad dharma bhāvī dṛṣṭāntaḥ udāharaṇam asya udāharaṇa upalakṣaṇam arthaḥ sādhya sādharmyam sādhyena samāna dharma tā tasmāt sādhya sādharmyāt tad dharma bhāvī bhavati tasya dharmaḥ tad dharmaḥ tasya sādhyasya dharmiṇaḥ yaḥ dharmaḥ sa sādhya dharmaḥ sa yasmin dṛṣṭānte bhavati sa dṛṣṭāntaḥ udāharaṇam yathā stha alpa ādi dravyam tad utpatti dharmakam ca anityam dṛṣṭam iti udāhriyate anena dharmayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ iti udāharaṇam tad viparyayāt viparītam sādhya vaidharmyāt atad dharma bhāvī dṛṣṭāntaḥ udāharaṇam iti avīta hetau draṣṭavyam yathā na idam nirātmakam iti atra yat nirātmakam tad prāṇādimat na bhavati iti 
NSV_1.1.38	 udāharaṇa apekṣaḥ tathā iti upasaṃhāraḥ na tathā iti vā sādhyasya upanayaḥ udāharaṇa apekṣaḥ udāharaṇa tantraḥ udāharaṇe hi sādhya sādhana yukte dṛṣṭe iti atas udāharaṇa apekṣaḥ tathā ca śabdaḥ utpatti dharmakaḥ iti sādhyasya dharmasya utpatti dharmaka tvam upasaṃhriyate asti ca śabde kṛtaka tvam iti sa yadā sādhya sādharmya udāharaṇam pratyeti tadā tathā iti yadā vaidharmya udāharaṇam tadā na tathā iti upanayaḥ yathā vat nirātmakam tad aprāṇa ādimat na tad jīvat śarīram 
NSV_1.1.39	 hetu apadeśāt pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam nigamanam sādharmya udāharaṇa upanaye tasmāt utpatti dharmaka tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti vaidharmya udāharaṇa upanaye tu tasmāt aprāṇa ādimatva abhāvāt na nirātmakam jīvat śarīram iti nigamyante anena pratijñā hetu udāharaṇa upanaya nigamanāni ekatra iti nigamanam nigamyante samarthyante sambadhyante iti arthaḥ 
NSV_1.1.40	 atha tarkaḥ avijñāta tattve arthe kāraṇa upapattitaḥ tattva jñāna artham ūhaḥ tarkaḥ asya arthaḥ pūrvavat avijñāta tattve arthe iti yathā saḥ arthaḥ bhavati saḥ asya tathā bhāvaḥ tatvam tat avijñātam yasya arthasya tasmin= avijñāta tattve arthe ṣaṣṭhī sthāne eṣām saptamī draṣṭavyā avijñāta tattva arthasya tattva jñāna artham iti sambandhāt kāraṇa upapattitaḥ pramāṇa upapattitaḥ upapattiḥ sambhavaḥ bhavatu etasmin= arthe pramāṇam iti bhavet ayam arthaḥ iti udāharaṇa yaḥ ayam jñātā jñātavyam artham jānāti tam tattvataḥ jānīyām iti kim ayam utpatti dharmakaḥ atha anutpatti dharmakaḥ iti atra pramāṇa dharmaka tayā anutpatti dharmakeṇa anena bhavitavyam iti yaḥ ūhaḥ sa tarkaḥ nanu etat tattvataḥ jñānam eva kim ucyate tattva jñāna artham iti na idam tattva jñānam anavadhāraṇa ātmaka tvāt 
NSV_1.1.41	 etasmin= ca tarka viṣaye vimṛśya pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ sambandhaḥ arthaḥ ca pūrvavat vimṛśya vimarśanam kṛtvā pakṣāt ca pratipakṣāt ca pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām pakṣa śabdena pakṣa viṣayam sādhanam ucyate pratipakṣa śabdena pratipakṣa viṣayasya sādhanasya upalambhaḥ amūbhyām sādhana upalambhābhyām yad artha avadhāraṇam sa nirṇayaḥ pramāṇānām phalam iti mantavyam 
NSV_1.2.1^1	 atha tisraḥ kathāḥ bhavanti vādaḥ jalpaḥ vitaṇḍā ca iti tatra guru ādibhyaḥ saha vādaḥ vijigīṣuṇā jalpa vitaṇḍe bhavataḥ tatra yathoddeśam lakṣaṇa apadeśaḥ iti jñāpitam bhavati tatra vādasya lakṣaṇam ucyate pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ siddhānta aviruddhaḥ pañca avayava upapannaḥ pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahaḥ vādaḥ eka adhikaraṇa sthau viruddhau dharmau pakṣa pratipakṣau pratyanīka bhāvāt yathā asti ātmā na asti ātmā iti nānā adhikaraṇa sthau na viruddhau pakṣa pratipakṣau parigrahaḥ abhyupagama vyavasthā saḥ ayam pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahaḥ vādaḥ pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ iti pramāṇaiḥ tarkeṇa ca sādhanam upālambhaḥ ca asmin vicāre bhavati iti pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahasya mārga traye api samāna tvāt viśeṣaṇam bhavati 
NSV_1.2.1^2	 tarke api pramāṇa anugrāhaka tvāt pramāṇa sahitaḥ vāde praviṣṭaḥ na tu kevalam pramāṇānām eka artha vyavasthāpaka tvāt atha etau sādhana upālambhau kiṃviṣayau pakṣa pratipakṣa viṣayau pakṣa viṣayam sādhanam pratipakṣa viṣayaḥ upālambhaḥ atha pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ iti anena jalpa vitaṇḍābhyām katham vādaḥ viśiṣyate vādasya nityam eva pramāṇa tad sādhana upālambha ātmaka tvāt jalpa vitaṇḍayoḥ chala ja ati nigraha sthāna upālambha ātmaka tvasya vakṣyamāṇa tvāt jalpe nigraha sthāna viniyoga tvāt etat pratiṣedhaḥ siddhāntam abhyupetyāḥ aniyamāt yathā prasaṅgaḥ apasiddhāntaḥ iti evaṃlakṣaṇa apasiddhāntasya nigraha sthānasya avarodha artham siddhānta aviruddham iti vacanam vāde pañca avayava upapannaḥ iti hīnam anyatamena api avayavena nyūtam hetu udāharaṇa adhikam adhikam iti ca etayoḥ abhyanujñāna artham iti 
NSV_1.2.2^1	 yathā ukta upapannaḥ chala ja ati nigraha sthāna sādhana upālambhaḥ jalpaḥ atra yathā ukta upapannaḥ iti pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālmbhaḥ pakṣa pratipakṣa nigrahaḥ iti etāvat ādiśyate nanu siddhānta aviruddhaḥ pañca avayava upapannaḥ iti pada dvayam etasya pada dvayasya niyama artha tvāt na atideṣṭavye iti na yat atra sambadhyate tat atidiśyate sambadhyate ca pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ iti etat atidiśyate tathā ca yathā ukta upapannaḥ iti lakṣaṇa mātrasya atideśaḥ evam ca sāmarthya sadbhāvāt atidiśyate iti na niyama arthe pade niyantavyasya abhāvāt ca nanu chala jāti nigraha sthānaiḥ kasyacid sādhanam upālambhaḥ vā na bhavati ayukta uttara tvāt 
NSV_1.2.2^2	 atas kim artham chala jāti nigraha sthāna sādhana upālambha upādānam iti sādhana vighāta artham chala ja ati nigraha sthāneṣu punar sādhayitum samyak dūṣayitum vakṣyate atas na etat abhidhīyate chala jāti nigraha sthānāni sādhanam aṅgāni vā iti abādhita sādhana upādāne pareṇa ākulita buddhiḥ chala ādīni prayuṅkte kadācid chala ādibhiḥ ākulīkṛtasya parājayaḥ api syāt na punar etāni tattva bubhutsunā vaktavyāni kintu vijigīṣuṇā iti atas ayam pakṣa pratipakṣa nigrahāt chala ja ati nigraha sthāna prayoga aprayogābhyām bhidyamānaḥ vādaḥ jalpaḥ vitaṇḍā ca bhavati 
NSV_1.2.3–1.2.4	 sa pratipakṣa sthāpanā hīnaḥ vitaṇḍā pratipakṣa sthāpanā hīnaḥ dvitīya pakṣa sthāpanā hīnaḥ iti yāvat vaitaṇḍikaḥ hi para pakṣa pratikṣepeṇa pravartate iti savyabhicāra viruddha prakaraṇa sama sādhya sama atīta kālāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ hetu lakṣaṇa abhāvāt ahetavaḥ hetvābhāsāḥ ime tu savyabhicāra viruddha prakaraṇa sama sādhya sama atīta kālāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ kaḥ punar asya sūtrasya arthaḥ vibhāga uddeśaḥ 
NSV_1.2.5	 anaikāntika ssavi abhicāraḥ ekasmin= ante niścaye niyataḥ aikāntikaḥ tad viparītaḥ anaikantikaḥ vyabhicāraḥ sādhya tajjātīyayoḥ anyatra vṛtti tvam tena saha vartate iti savyabhicāraḥ asya udāharaṇam asparśa tvāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ sparśavān kumbhaḥ hi anityaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na ca tathā sparśavān śabdaḥ tasmāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ atra dṛṣṭānte sparśava tvam anitya tvam ca dvau= imau dharmau sadhya sādhana bhūtau na gṛhyete katham sparśavān= ca paramāṇuḥ nityaḥ ca iti asparśaḥ hi ātma ādiḥ nityaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti sādharmya dṛṣṭāntepya sparśa tva hetoḥ vyabhicāri tvam asparśā buddhiḥ anityā ca iti 
NSV_1.2.6–1.2.7	 siddhāntam abhyupetya tad virodhī viruddhaḥ kaḥ asya sūtrasya arthaḥ abhyupagata artha virodhī viruddhaḥ iti udāharaṇam tat etat trailokyam vyakteḥ apaiti nitya tva pratiṣedhāt apetam api asti vināśa pratiṣedhāt iti atra pūrva hetuta abhyupagatam artham uttara hetuḥ viruṇaddhi uttareṇa vā pūrvaḥ virudhyate yasmāt prakaraṇa cintā sa nirṇaya artham apadiṣṭaḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ vimarśa adhiṣṭhānau pakṣa pratipakṣau= anavasitau prakaraṇam tasya cintā vimarśāt prabhṛti prak nirṇayāt yat samīkṣaṇam sa hetuḥ nirṇaya artham prayuktaḥ ubhaya pakṣa sāmyāt prakaraṇa samaḥ prakaraṇam anatikamya vartamānaḥ udāharaṇam anityaḥ śabdaḥ nitya dharma anupalabdheḥ iti yathā śabde nitya dharmaḥ na upalabhyate evam anityavarmaḥ api iti saḥ ayam ubhaya pakṣa viśeṣa anupalabdhiḥ prakaraṇa cintām prayojayati na anyatarasya nirṇayāya kalpate iti prakaraṇa samaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ 
NSV_1.2.8	 sādhya aviśiṣṭaḥ sādhya tvāt sādhya samaḥ sādhyena aviśiṣṭaḥ yaḥ sādhana dharmaḥ sādhya vat prajñāpayitavyaḥ sa sādhya samaḥ saḥ eva ca asiddhaḥ iti ucyate udāhṛtiḥ dravyam chāyā gatimat tvāt iti atra ca yathā dravya tvam chāyāyāḥ sādhyam tathā eva gatimat tvam api iti gatima tvam deśāt deśa antara darśanāt iti ced na deśa antara darśanasya anyathā siddha tvāt katham anyathā āvaraṇa santānāt asannidhi santānaḥ tejasaḥ iti yathābhāṣyam āvarake dravye apasarpati gacchati tejasaḥ asannidhi viśiṣṭam dravyam yat upalabhyate tat tu chāyā iti ucyate iti 
NSV_1.2.9–1.2.10	 kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ kāla atītaḥ yasya apadiśyamānasya kāla atyayena eka deśaḥ yujyate saḥ eka deśa atyayāt kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ kāla atītaḥ udāharaṇam nityaḥ śabdaḥ saṃyoga vyaṅgya tvāt iti uplabdhi kāle saṃyogaḥ na asti saḥ ayam saṃyogaḥ hetu viśeṣaṇa tvena upāttaḥ upalabdhi kālam atyā iti iti hetuḥ kāla atītaḥ ucyate atha chalam āha vacana vidhātaḥ artha avikalpa upapatyā chalam sāmānya śabdasya viśeṣa aneka sambandhi tve sati avivakṣitā anya artha adhyāropaṇena vacana vidhātaḥ yaḥ kriyate tat chalam iti veditavyam 
NSV_1.2.11–1.2.12	 tat trividham vākchalam sāmānya chalam upacāra= chalam ca iti teṣām madhye abiśeṣa abhihite arthe vaktuḥ abhiprāyāt artha antara kalpanā vākchalam yathā nava kambalaḥ ayam māṇavakaḥ iti prayogaḥ atra navaḥ kambalaḥ asya iti vaktuḥ abhiprāyaḥ tatra chalavādi āha kutas asya nava kambalāḥ iti tat idam sāmānya śabdā iva aci chalam vākchalam iti 
NSV_1.2.13	 sambhavataḥ arthasya ati sāmānya yogāt asambhūta artha klpanā sāmānyacchalam sāmānyasya vivakṣita artha atikramaḥ atisāmānyam udāharaṇam vidyā caraṇa sampannaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ iti chala vāyadī brāhmaṇyam vidyā caraṇa sampadaḥ hetuḥ iti uktam iti kṛtvā pratyavatiṣṭhate yadi brāhmaṇe vidyā caraṇa sampad bhavati vrātye api sambhavet vrātyaḥ api brāhmaṇaḥ bhavitum arhati anena vacanena sambhavati brāhmaṇe vidyā caraṇa sampaditi asya vighātaḥ asambhava artha kalpanayā kriyate tat idam brāhmaṇa tva sāmānya nimitta tvāt sāmānya chalam 
NSV_1.2.14	 dharma vikalpa nirdeśe artha sadbhāva pratiṣedhaḥ upacāracchalam dharma vikalpa śabdena abhidhāna dharmaḥ dvedhā abhidhīyate pradhānam bhāktaḥ ca yathā mañcāḥ krośanti iti kāṣṭha saṃghāteṣu pradhānaḥ mañca śabdaḥ krośana kriyāḥ yāḥ tatra asambhavam īkṣitvā sthāniṣu puruṣeṣu prayujyamānaḥ bhāktaḥ yaḥ ekasmin prayoge pradhāna buddhyā pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate na mañcāḥ krośanti iti tad upacāra prayoga nimita tvāt upacāra= chalam 
NSV_1.2.15–1.2.16	 vākchalam eva upacāra= chalam tad aviśeṣāt eka tvam anayoḥ aviśeṣāt kaḥ aviśeṣaḥ iha api artha antara kalpanā tathā tatra api iti tad aviśeṣāt na tad artha antara bhāvāt aviśeṣa ādityasva hetoḥ anena sūtreṇa asiddha tām udbhāvayati katham asiddhiḥ ekatra vastu sadbhāvaḥ pratiṣidhyate na eva kroṣṭāraḥ mañcāḥ iti ekatra vastu abhyanujñāya kambala yogam abhyupagamya kambalasya aneka tā dharmāḥ pratiṣidhyante iti ekatra dharmaḥ pratiṣidhyate ekatra dharmī saḥ ayam ati mahān viśeṣaḥ 
NSV_1.2.17	 atha manyase kim naḥ anena viśeṣeṇa iha api artha antara kalpanā tatra api iti aviśeṣe vā kiñcid sādharmyāt eka= chala prasaṅgaḥ chalasya dvi tvam abhyanujñāya tritvam pratiṣidhyate yathā ca ayam hetuḥ tritvam pratiṣedhati tathā dvi tvam api abhyanujñātam pratiṣedhati vidyate hi kiñcid sādharmyam dvayoḥ api iti atha dvi tvam kiñcid sādharmyāt na nivartate tathā tri tvam api na nivartsyati ihi 
NSV_1.2.18–1.2.19	 atha jātayaḥ sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratyavasthānam jātiḥ saṃsthāpanāyām hetoḥ satyām sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa vā pratīpam avasthānam pratipakṣa vat iti pratyanīka vat jāyamāne arthaḥ jātiḥ vipratipattiḥ apratipattiḥ ca iti nigraha sthānam anyathā abhihitasya sthitasya vā anyathā pratipattiḥ vipratipattiḥ tathā vipratipadyamānaḥ parājayam prāpnoti nigraha sthānam khalu parājaya prāptiḥ apratipattiḥ tu ārambha viṣaye anārambhaḥ pareṇa sthāpitam vā na pratiṣedhati pratiṣiddham vā na uddharati asamāsāt ca na ete eva nigraha sthāne iti 
NSV_1.2.20	 kim punar dṛṣṭānta vat jāteḥ nigraha sthānasya ca abhedaḥ āhosvit siddhānta vat bhedaḥ iti atas āha tad vikalpāt jāti nigraha sthāna bahu tvam tasya sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratyavasthānasya vikalpāt hetoḥ jāti bahutvam tayoḥ ca vipratipatti apratipattyoḥ vikalpāt nigraha sthāna bahutvam iti te ete pramāṇa ādayaḥ padārthāḥ uddiṣṭāḥ lakṣitāḥ ca atas param yathoddeśam yathālakṣaṇam ca parīkṣiṣyante iti trividhā asya śāstrasya pravṛttiḥ veditavyā iti tantra pratijñā saṃsāraḥ tad nivṛttiḥ ca saṃvidā uddeśaḥ lakṣaṇam ca eva tattvānām iha kīrtitam 
NSV_2.1.1	 trividhā ca asya śāstrasya pravṛttiḥ uddeśaḥ lakṣaṇam parīkṣā ca iti kathitam tatra uddeśa lakṣaṇe vyākhyāte pūrva adhyāye idānīm parīkṣā vatiṣyate tatra yathoddeśaḥ tathā lakṣaṇam tathā parīkṣā iti pūrvam uddiṣṭāni lakṣitāni ca pramāṇāni prameyāṇi ca vilaṃdhya saṃśayaḥ pūrvam parīkṣyate kimartham krama bhedaḥ kriyate parīkṣā aṅga tvāt saṃśayasya saḥ ayam saṃśayaḥ samāna dharma upapatteḥ iti evam ādiḥ yaḥ tasya ākṣepaḥ samāna aneka dharma adhyavasāyāt anyatara dharma adhyavasāyāt vā na saṃśayaḥ samāna dharma adhyavasāyaḥ saṃśayasya na kāraṇam bhavati anyatara dharma adhyavasāyāt ca na saṃśayaḥ bhavati atas anyatara avadhāraṇam eva etat iti 
NSV_2.1.2–2.1.5	 vipratipatti avyavasthā adhyavasāyāt ca na saṃśayaḥ iti vartate vipratipatti avyavasthā adhyavasāyāt ca na saṃśayaḥ na vipratipatti mātrāt avyavasthā mātrāt vā iti sūtra arthaḥ vipratipattau ca sampratipatteḥ na vipratipattiḥ asti iti na saṃśayaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ avyavasthā ātmani vyavasthita tvāt ca avyavasthāyāḥ avyavasthā ātmani vyavasthita tvāt ca avyavasthāyāḥ na avyavasthā vidyate iti sūtra arthaḥ tathā atyanta saṃśayaḥ tad dharma sātatya upapatteḥ samāna dharma ādīnām dharmāṇām sātatyāt atyanta saṃśayaḥ syāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NSV_2.1.6^1	 asya uttaram āha yathā ukta adhyavasāyāt eva tad viśeṣa apekṣāt saṃśaye na asaṃśayaḥ na atyanta saṃśayaḥ vā ayam pratipakṣasya saṅkṣepeṇa uddhāraḥ na ayam samāna dharma ādibhyaḥ eva saṃśayaḥ kintu tad viṣaya adhyavasāyāt upalabdhi anupalaṣdhya vyavasthāne sati viśeṣa smṛti sahitāt evam ca na asaṃśayaḥ na atyanta saṃśayaḥ vā anyatara dharma adhyavasāyāt vā iti na yuktam na ekasmāt saṃśayaḥ iti na hi kadācid anyatara dharma adhyavasāye sati saṃśayaḥ anyatara dharma adhyavasāyasya nirṇaya hetu tvāt iti yat punar etat vipratipattau ca sampratipatteḥ iti na saṃjñā an yathā tvāt arthasya anyathātvam 
NSV_2.1.6^2–2.1.7	 yasmāt vipratipatti śabda arthasya nimitta antara sannipāte sampratipattiḥ iti nāma kṛtam na tāvatā vipratipattiḥ na asti vipratipatteḥ tu tathā abhāvāt saṃśaya hetu tvam iti yat punar etat avyavasthā ātmani vyavasthita tvāt ca avyavasthāyāḥ na avyavasthā asti iti tat api na vyadhātāta avyavasthā na asti iti sā ca avyavasthā ātmani vyavasthitā iti vyādhātaḥ na ca nimitta antara sannipātena arthasya saṃjñā antara karaṇam artha tathā bhāvam bādhate yathābhūtaḥ eva arthaḥ saṃjñā antara karaṇe tathābhūtaḥ eva akaraṇe api iti yatra saṃśayaḥ tatra evam uttarottara prasaṅgaḥ yatra yatra saṃśaya pūrvikā parīkṣā śāstre kathāyām vā tatra tatra eva saṃśaye pareṇa pratiṣiddhe evam samādhiḥ vācyaḥ iti śiṣyān śikṣayati ācāryaḥ atas ca sarva parīkṣā vyāpi tvāt prathamam saṃśayaḥ parīkṣitaḥ 
NSV_2.1.8–2.1.10	 atha idānīm pramāṇāni parīkṣyante tatra paraḥ pratyavatiṣṭhate pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam traikālya asiddheḥ pūrva apara sadbhāva lakṣaṇeṣu triṣu api kāleṣu na pratyakṣa ādīni artham sādhayiṣyanti iti asya sāmānya vacanasya artha vibhāgaḥ pūrva hi pramāṇa siddhau na indriya artha sannikarṣāt pratyakṣa upapattiḥ gandha ādi viṣayam jñānam pratyakṣam pramāṇam tat yadi pūrvam paścāt gandha ādīnām siddhiḥ tadā indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ tasya kāraṇam iti indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam jñānam iti asya vyāghātaḥ atha paścāt evam ca na vyādhātaḥ iti atas āha paścāt siddhau na pramāṇebhyaḥ prameya siddhiḥ pramāṇam antareṇa prameyam ātmānam na labhate iti na pramāṇa āyattā prameya siddhiḥ iti vyāghātaḥ 
NSV_2.1.11^1	 yugapad siddhau pratyartha niyata tvāt krama vṛtti tva abhāvaḥ buddhīnām indriya arthānām buddhīnām ca sannipāte sati buddhīnām krama vṛtti tvam yat dṛṣṭam tat na syāt iti vyāghātaḥ doṣaḥ atra samādhiḥ upalabdhi hetoḥ upalabdhi viṣayasya ca arthasya pūrva apara sahabhāva aniyamāt yathādarśanam vibhāga vacanam kvacid upalabdhi hetuḥ pūrvam paścāt upalabdhi viṣayaḥ yathā ādityasya prakāśaḥ utpadyamānānām kvacid pūrvam upalabdhi viṣayaḥ paścāt upalabdhi hetuḥ yathā avasthitānām pradīpaḥ kvacid upalabdhi hetu viṣayau saha bhavataḥ 
NSV_2.1.11^2	 yathā dhūmena agni grahaṇam iti upalabdhi hetuḥ pramāṇam upalabdhi viṣayaḥ prameyam evam pramāṇa prameyayoḥ pūrva apara sadbhāva aniyamāt yathā arthaḥ dṛśyate tathā vibhajya vaktavyaḥ iti tatra ekāntena pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ samākhyā hetoḥ traikālya yogāt ca apratiṣedhaḥ pramāṇam prameyam iti ca asyāḥ samākhyāyāḥ nimittam tri kāla yogi pramāsyate pramīyate prāmāyi vā anena iti pramāṇam pramāsyate pramīyate prāmāyi vā iti ca prameyam evañca sati pramāsyate ayam arthaḥ bhaviṣyati asmin hetutaḥ upalabdheḥ iti prameyam idam iti siddhyati 
NSV_2.1.12	 evañca traikālya asiddheḥ pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ ayam api pratiṣedhaḥ triṣu api kāleṣu na upapadyate iti sūtra arthaḥ asya vibhāgaḥ pūrvam hi pratiṣedha siddhau= asati pratiṣedhye kim anena pratiṣidhyate paścāt siddhau pratiṣedhyasya asiddhiḥ pratiṣedhāḥ abhāvāt iti yugapad siddhau pratiṣedhya siddhi abhyanujñānāt anarthakaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ pratiṣedha lakṣaṇe ca vākye anupapadyamāne siddham pratyakṣa ādīnām pramāṇa tvam iti 
NSV_2.1.13	 sarva pramāṇa pratiṣedhāt ca pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ traikālya asiddha iti asya hetoḥ udāharaṇam upādīyate na vā yadi upādīyate vyāghātaḥ bhavati pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇya abhyupagamāt upādīyamānam api na artham sādhayati iti vyartham atha sādhayati vyāghātaḥ atha na upādīyate apradarśitam hetu arthasya sādhaka tvam iti apradarśita dṛṣṭāntaḥ hetuḥ na sādhakaḥ iti saḥ ayam hetuḥ sarva pramāṇa evi pratiṣiddhaḥ viruddhaḥ bhavati siddhāntam abhyupetya tad virodhī viruddhaḥ iti vākya āryaḥ asya siddhāntaḥ sa ca vākya arthaḥ pramāṇāni na artham sādhayanti iti idam ca pramāṇānām upādānam artha sādhanāya pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam traikālya asiddheḥ iti buddhi spanda ādīni avarjayan buddhyā vākyam uccārayasi sthāṇu ādīn pariharan pāda viharaṇa ādīni karoṣi te ete vākya pravṛttī pramāṇa pratiṣedhāt na sambhavataḥ iti 
NSV_2.1.14	 tad prāmāṇye vā na sarva pramāṇa vipratiṣedhaḥ atha sva vākya āśrita pramāṇa vyatirekeṇa pramāṇāni pratiṣidhyante evam sati na sarvam pramāṇam pratiṣiddham bhavati iti vipratiṣedhaḥ iti vi iti ayam upasargaḥ viśeṣa pratiṣedhe na vyāghāte iti kim uktam bhavati kānicid pramāṇāni pratiṣidhyante kānicid abhyanujñāyante iti yāni sva vākya āśritāni tāni abhyanujñāyante yāni para vākya āśritāni tāni pratiṣidhyante iti yat ca idam vākyam pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam traikālya asiddheḥ iti kim idam pramāṇa svarūpam atha na iti yadi pramāṇa svarūpam tadā vyāghātaḥ atha na tathā api na anena kaścid arthaḥ siddhyati iti vyartham 
NSV_2.1.15	 traikālya apratiṣedhaḥ ca śabdāt ātodya siddhi vat tad siddheḥ ukteḥ pūrvam upalabdhi hetoḥ upalabdhi viṣayasya ca pūrva apara sadbhāvāḥ iti tatra ekām vidhām udāharati śabdāt ātodya siddhi vat iti yathā pūrva siddham ātodyam paścāt siddhena śabdena anumīyate sādhyam ātodyam sādhanam ca śabdaḥ antarhite hi ātodye svanataḥ anumānam bhavati iti vīṇā vādyate veṇuḥ pūryate iti sthāna viśeṣeṇa ātodya viśeṣam pratipadyate pūrva siddham paścāt siddhena upalabdhi hetunā pratipadyate nidarśana artha tvāt ca śeṣayoḥ vidhayoḥ yathā ukte udāharaṇe veditavye 
NSV_2.1.16	 pramāṇam prameyam iti ca samākhyā samāveśena vartate samākhyā nimitta vaśāt samākhya nimittam tu upalabdhi sādhanam pramāṇam upalabdhi viṣayaḥ ca prameyam yadā ca upalabdhi viṣayaḥ kasyacid upalabdhi sādhanam bhavati tadā pramāṇam iti prameyam iti ca eka arthaḥ vidhīyate iti asya arthasya jñāpana artham sūtram prameyā ca tulā prāmāṇya vat kim uktam bhavati yathā guru tva parimāṇa jñāna sādhanam tulā dravyam samāhāra guru tvasya iyat ta apariccheda nimitta tvāt pramāṇam suvarṇa ādinā paricchidyamāneyattā eṣā tulā iti pariccheda viṣaya tvena vyavatiṣṭhamānā prameyam upalabdhau svātantryāt pramātā buddhiḥ upalabdhi sādhana tvāt pramāṇam upalabdhi viṣaya tvāt tu prameyam ubhaya abhāvāt pramitiḥ iti evam artha viśeṣe api samākhyā samāveśaḥ yojyaḥ 
NSV_2.1.17–2.1.18	 atra idam cintyate kim etāni pramāṇāni pratyakṣa ādīni sva upalabdhau pratyakṣa ādi vyatiriktam pramāṇa antaram prayojayanti atha niḥsādhana eva pramāṇeṣu upalabdhiḥ iti kiñca atas pramāṇatassiddheḥ pramāṇānām pramāṇa antara siddhi prasaṅgaḥ pramāṇa viṣayāyāḥ siddheḥ yadi pramāṇam sādhanam pramāṇa antaram prāpnoti pratyakṣa ādīnām sādhya tvāt na sādhyam sādhanam bhavati iti atha pramāṇa antaram antareṇa nissādhana eva pramāṇeṣu upalabdhiḥ iti āśaṅkya āha tad vinivṛtteḥ vā pramāṇa antara siddhi vat prameya siddhiḥ yatra pratyakṣa ādi upalabdhau pramāṇa antaram nivartate ātma ādi upalabdhau= api pramāṇa antaram nivartsyati 
NSV_2.1.19	 evam ca sarva pramāṇa vilopaḥ iti atas āha na pradīpa prakāśa vat tad siddheḥ pradīpa prakāśaḥ hī ghaṭa ādi upalabdhi sādhana aṅga tvāt pramāṇam sa ca pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ eva upalabhyate iti tathā pramāṇa ādīni api pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ eva upalapsyante iti dṛṣṭānta mātram etat atra nyāyaḥ ucyate pati akṣa ādīni sva upalabdhau pramāṇa antara aprayojakāni pariccheda sādhana tvāt pradīpa vat iti tena eva tasya agrahaṇam iti ced na eṣa doṣaḥ pramāṇa lakṣaṇe na hi etāni saṅgṛhītāni lakṣaṇāni tatra kasyacid kenacid grahaṇam iti adoṣaḥ 
NSV_2.1.20	 pare tu hetu parigraham antareṇa dṛṣṭānta mātram pradīpa prakāśa sūtreṇa upādadate iti tān pratīdam ucyate kvacid nivṛtti darśanāt anivṛtti darśanāt ca kvacid ana ekāntaḥ vathā pradīpa prakāśaḥ tathā pramāṇāni na punar sthālī ādi rūpam tathā pramāṇāni iti kaḥ atra niyama hetuḥ pradīpa prakāśa dṛṣṭāntaḥ bhavatu mā abhūt sthālī ādi dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti atra api niyama hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ saḥ ayam ubhayathā anekāntar viśeṣa hetu parigraham antareṇa prasaktaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ viśeṣa hetu parigrahe sati upasaṃhāra abhyanujñānāt apratiṣedhaḥ yadi punar ayam pradīpa prakāśa dṛṣṭāntaḥ viśeṣa hetunā prakāśaka tva ādinā saṅgṛhītaḥ tata ekasmin pakṣe ayam anujñāyamānaḥ na śakyaḥ pratiṣedhdu iti anekantaḥ iti ayam doṣaḥ na bhavati iti pratyakṣa ādīnām pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ eva upalabdhau anavasthā iti ced na pratyakṣeṇa artham upalabhe iti saṃvitti viṣayam saṃvitti nimittam ca upalabhamānasya sarvaḥ vyavahāraḥ upapadyate saḥ ayam tāvatī eva nivartate iti 
NSV_2.1.21–2.1.22^1	 sāmānyena pramāṇāni parīkṣya viśeṣeṇa parīkṣyate tatra pratyakṣam ādau= uktam iti tat parīkṣyate pratyakṣa lakṣaṇa anupapattiḥ asamagra vacanāt yat idam bhavatā pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam ucyate indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam ityādi etat asamagram anyāni api pratyakṣasya kāraṇāni santi tāni na uktāni yathā atma manaḥ saṃyoga ādi tathā lakṣaṇam api etat na bhavati kasmāt utpatti kāraṇa apadeśāt na hi kāraṇa apadeśaḥ vastunaḥ lakṣaṇam na hi ghaṭa ādeḥ kāryasya mṛd piṇḍa ādi kama utpattiḥ lakṣaṇam na ubhayathā api adoṣāt yadi kāraṇam tadā api na doṣaḥ 
NSV_2.1.21–2.1.22^2	 yadi lakṣaṇam tathā api na doṣaḥ katham kāraṇa pakṣe tāvat uktam na idam kāraṇa avadhāraṇa artham sūtram api tu pratyakṣasya yat asādhāraṇam kāraṇam anumāna ādi vyavacchedakam tat vacana artham iti na ātma manaḥ saṃyoga ādeḥ anumāna sādhāraṇasya atra prasaṅgaḥ lakṣaṇa pakṣe api na doṣaḥ asādhāraṇa tvāt indriya artha sannikarṣasya iti na ātma manasoḥ sannikarṣa abhāve pratyakṣa utpattiḥ ātma manaḥ sannikarṣa abhāve api na utpadyate buddhiḥ indriya artha sannikarṣa abhāvāt iti na ukta uttara tvāt na idam kāraṇa sāmānya avadhāraṇa artham sūtram api tu viśiṣṭa kāraṇa avadhāraṇa artham iti 
NSV_2.1.23	 ye tu sati bhāvāt asati ca abhāvāt kāraṇa bhāvam varṇayanti teṣām diś deśa kāla ākāśeṣu api evam prasaṅgaḥ diś deśa kāla ākāśeṣu asatsu jñāna abhāvāt tāni api jñāna kāraṇāni iti prāptam iti kena punar nyāyena diś ādya kāraṇam sāmarthya anupalabdheḥ na hi jñāna utpattau diś ādeḥ sāmarthyam upalabhyate atha manyase diś ādiḥ sannidhi mātreṇa jñāna utpattau kāraṇam iti tat ayuktam sannidhera varjanīya tvāt kāraṇa bhāve hetuḥ vaktaṣyaḥ 
NSV_2.1.24–2.1.25	 yadi evam ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ tarhi upasaṃkhyeyaḥ na upasaṅkhyeyaḥ gamyamāna tvāt iti āha jñāna liṅga tvāt ātmanaḥ na anavarodhaḥ prāk abhihitam jñānam ātma liaṅgam iti tena ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ anukta upyanumeyaḥ tad ayaugapadya liṅga tvāt ca na manasaḥ anavarodhaḥ iti vartate yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ liṅgam ipi ucyamāne siddhi ati eva manaḥ sannikarṣa apekṣaḥ indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ jñāna sādhanam iti 
NSV_2.1.16	 atha kasmāt indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ abhidhīyate na ātma manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ indriya manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ vā iti pratyakṣa nimitta tvāt ca indriya arthayoḥ sannikarṣasya sva śabdena vacanam indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ pratyakṣasya eva nimittam ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ pratyakṣasya ca anyasya ca iti nanu indriya artha sannikarṣeṇa samāna tvāt indriya manaḥ saṃyogaḥ vaktavyaḥ na idam kāraṇa avadhāraṇa artham sūtram iti ukta tvāt 
NSV_2.1.27	 supta vyāsakta manasām ca indriya arthayoḥ sannikarṣa nimitta tvāt indriya artha sannikarṣasya prādhānya darśana param idam sūtram yadā tu tīvrau dhvani sparśau suptasya prabodha kāraṇam bhavataḥ tadā indriya artha sannikarṣa nimittam eva prabodha jñānam utpadyate viṣaya antara vyāsakta manasaḥ saṅkalpa vaśāt viṣaya antaram jijñāsamānasya bāhya viṣaya upanipātāt jñānam utpadyate tatra api indriya artha sannikarṣasya eva prādhānyam na ātma ādi sannikarṣasya iti 
NSV_2.1.28	 prādhānye hetu antaram taiḥ ca apadeśaḥ jñāna viśeṣāṇām taiḥ indriyaiḥ arthaiḥ ca jñāna viśeṣāḥ vyapadiśyante ghrāṇa vijñānam cakṣuḥ vijñānam rasana vijñānam iti gandha jñānam rūpa jñānam rasa jñānam iti ca indriya viṣaya viśeṣāt ca pañcadhā buddhiḥ bhavati atas prādhānyam indriya artha sannikarṣasya iti asādhāraṇena ca vyapadeśaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā śāli aṅkuraḥ iti 
NSV_2.1.29–2.1.30	 vyāhata tvāt ahetuḥ anena tri sūtrīm pratyācaṣṭe pratyakṣa nimitta tvāt ca indriya artha sannikarṣasya iti supta vyāsakta manasā ca indriya arthayoḥ sannikarṣa nimitta tvāt taiḥ ca apadeśaḥ jñāna viśeṣāṇām iti iyam kila trisūtrī ātma manasoḥ saṃyogasya jñāna kāraṇa tvam pratiṣedhati iti vyāghātaḥ pūrvam ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya jñāna kāraṇa tva abhyanujñānāt atha mābhūt vyāghātaḥ iti sarvam jñānam ātma manaḥ saṃyoga jam iṣyate deśya avasthāyām etat krasmāt ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ na abhidhīyate iti ukta uttaram etat kim iti na idam kāraṇa avadhāraṇa artham sūtram api tu viśiṣṭa kāraṇa vacanam iti na artha viśeṣa prābalyāt na anayā tri sūtryā ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ pratiṣidhyate api tu prādhānyam indriya artha sannikarṣasya upapādyate iti na vyāghātaḥ 
NSV_2.1.31	 evam tāvat samadhigatam pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam atas param idānīm pratyakṣasya anumāne antarbhāvam kurvāṇaḥ idam āha pratyakṣam anumānam eka deśa grahaṇāt upalabdheḥ yat idam indriya artha sannikarṣāt utpadyate ayam vṛkṣaḥ iti etat kila pratyakṣam tat ca anumānam eva kasmāt eka deśa grahaṇāt vṛkṣa upalabdheḥ arvāc bhāga lakṣaṇam eka deśa mayam gṛhītvā hi vṛkṣam upalabhate tatra yathā dhūmam gṛhītvā vahnim anuminoti tādṛś eva tat bhavati kim punar atra eka deśa grahaṇāt ayam pratipadyate avayava samūha avayavi pakṣe avayava antarāṇi dravya antara utpatti pakṣe tāni ca avayavī ca iti avayava samūha pakṣe tāvat vṛkṣa buddheḥ abhāvaḥ eka deśa grahaṇāt dravya antara utpatti pakṣe asya eka deśa sambaddhasyāḥ agrahaṇāt na avaya vi anumeyaḥ grahaṇe ca aviśeṣāt anumeya tva abhāvaḥ tasmāt na anumā vṛkṣa buddhiḥ 
NSV_2.1.32	 viruddhaḥ ca ayam hetuḥ eka deśa grahaṇāt vṛkṣa upalabdhiḥ iti katham iti pratyakṣeṇa yāvat tāvat api upalambhāt pratyakṣam anumānam iti eva bruvatā pratyakṣam apahnūyate tad apahnavāt ca yat eka deśa grahaṇam pratyakṣam āśrīyate tad vyāhatam bhavati iti viruddha tvam ca eka deśa grahaṇa mātreṇa pratyakṣasya lakṣaṇam siddhyati iti na pratyakṣasya hāniḥ itthaṃsūtra yojanā na pratyakṣam anumānam kasmat pratyakṣeṇa eva eka deśasya upalambhāt yāvat ca artha jātam tasya viṣayaḥ tāvat abhyanujñāyamānam pratyakṣasya vyavasthāpakam bhavati iti itas ca pratyakṣasya na anumāna tva prasaṅgaḥ tad pūrvaka tvāt pratyakṣa pūrvakam anumānam na tu pratyakṣa pūrvakam pratyakṣam iti ayam ca anayoḥ viśeṣaḥ iti na ca eka deśa upalabdhiḥ avayavi sadbhāvāt na ca eka deśa upalabdhi mātram kim tarhi tad saṃhita avaya vī upalabdhiḥ ca kasmāt avayavi sadbhāvāt asti hi ayam eka deśa vyatiriktaḥ avayavī tasya avayava sthānasya upalabdhi kāraṇa prāptasya eka deśa upalabdhau= anupalabdhiḥ anupapanna iti 
NSV_2.1.33–2.1.34	 sādhya tvāt avayavini sandehaḥ yat uktam avayavi sadbhāvāt iti ayam ahetuḥ sādhya tvāt sādhyam tāvat anupapāditam etat kāraṇebhyaḥ dravya antaram utpadyate iti anupapattiḥ evam ca vipratipatti mātram bhavati vipratipatteḥ ca avayavini sandehaḥ iti sarva agrahaṇam avayavi a siddheḥ saṃśaya pākaraṇa artham sūtram sarveṣām arthānām agrahaṇam prasajyeta yadi avayavi artha antara bhūtaḥ avayebhyaḥ na asti katham iti paramāṇavaḥ atīndriyāḥ avayavi dravyāṇi ca bhavadbhiḥ na pratipadyante tad anabhyupagame ca yaḥ ayam dravya pratyayaḥ kumbhaḥ iti guṇa pratyayaḥ śyāmaḥ iti kriyā pratyayaḥ calati iti sāmānya pratyayaḥ asti iti viśeṣa pratyayaḥ kalaśaḥ iti samavāya pratyayaḥ iha ghaṭe rūpa ādayaḥ iti tathā anye api pratyayāḥ ekaḥ mahān ityādayaḥ na syuḥ asti ca sarvasya dravya guṇa karma ādi prapañcasya tena sarvasya grahaṇāt paśyāmaḥ asti avayava tiriktaḥ avayavi iti 
NSV_2.1.35	 dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇa upapatteḥ ca avayavi artha antara bhūtaḥ iti ca arthaḥ kim idam dhāraṇam nāma ucyate yadā ayam avayavinaḥ eka deśam gṛhnāti tadā tena eka deśa grahaṇena saha avayavinam api gṛhṇāti tadā tena eka deśa grahaṇena saha avayavinam api gṛhṇāti tena ca grahaṇena yat avayavinaḥ deśa antara prāpti nivāraṇam tat dhāraṇam ākarṣaṇam nāma yadā eka deśena saha avayavinaḥ deśa antara prāpaṇam te ete dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇe avayavinam sādhayataḥ 
NSV_2.1.36	 avayavi apala apavādī ca evam paryanuyojyaḥ yā iyam ekam idam dravyam iti buddhiḥ sā kim nānā viṣayāḥ abhinna artha viṣaya iti yadi nānā viṣayā bahuṣu adarśanāt ayuktāḥ atha abhinna artha viṣayāḥ yaḥ asau= ekabuddheḥ viṣayaḥ saḥ avayavi iti senā vat grahaṇam iti ced na atīndriya tvāt aṇūnām yathā senā aṅgeṣu vana aṅgeṣu ca dūgada gṛhyamāṇa pṛthaktveṣu ekam idam iti utpadyate buddhiḥ evam aṇuṣu samucciteṣu agṛhyamāṇa pṛthaktveṣu ekam idam iti utpadyate buddhiḥ iti na atīndriya tvāt aṇūnām samuccayaḥ nāma saṃyogaḥ na ca atīndriyāṇām saṃyogaḥ pratyakṣaḥ bhavitum arhati yaḥ ca ayam anekasmin eka pratyayaḥ sa mithyā pratyayaḥ mithyā pratyaya nimittam sāmānya darśanam viśeṣa anupalabdhiḥ avidyamāna viśeṣa darśana dvāreṇa adhyāropita tvāt tad viparīta dharmatā na ca atīndriya tvāt aṇūnām sāmānya darśanam asti tad abhāve kutas viśeṣa adarśanam tad abhāve ca na tad viparīta dharma adhyāropaḥ na ca nimittam antareṇa naimittikasya mithyā pratyayasya prādurbhāvaḥ yuktaḥ 
NSV_2.1.37	 atha idānīm anumānam parīkṣyate kim idam anumānam uktam ca tad pūrvakam anumānam iti tatra ca pūrvavat udāharaṇāni nadīpūraḥ pipīlikā aṇḍa sañcaraṇam mayūra vāśitam iti etat udāharaṇa vyabhicāra dvārakam sūtram rodha upadhāta sādṛśyebhyaḥ vyabhicārāt anumānam apramāṇam rodhāt api nadī pūrṇā gṛhyate tadā ca upariṣṭāt vṛṣṭaḥ devaḥ iti mithyā anumānam nīḍa upaghātāt api pipīlikā aṇḍa sañcaraṇam bhavati tadā bhaviṣyati vṛṣṭiḥ iti mithyā anumānam puruṣaḥ api mayūra vāśitam anukaroti tat api śabda sādṛśyāt mithyā anumāna bhavati iti 
NSV_2.1.38	 atha rodha uda ghāta sādṛśyebhyaḥ vyabhicāra ādityasya hetoḥ asiddha tā udbhāva dvārakam sūtram na eka deśa trāsa sādṛśyebhyaḥ artha antara bhāvāt yat tāvat rodhāt api nadī pūraḥ bhavati tatra nadī pūra mātreṇa na upari vṛṣṭimat deśa saṃbandhi tvam nadyāḥ sādhyate api tu pūra viśeṣeṇa tasya vyabhicārāt asiddhaḥ hetuḥ evam upaghātāt pipīlikā aṇḍa sañcaraṇa mātrasya vyabhicāraḥ na avitraḥ tānām bhūyasīnām pipīlikānām sañcaraṇa viśeṣa vyabhicāraḥ śabda avi abhicāraḥ api na asti yasmāt na śabda mātram anumānam mayūra astitve na ca atra mayūraḥ sādhyate api tu śabda gata viśeṣaḥ tatas na anumānāḥ apāmāṇyam iti 
NSV_2.1.39	 tri kāla viṣayam anumānam traikālya grahaṇāt iti uktam tatra vartamāna kāla pratiṣedha artham sūtram vartamāna abhāvaḥ patataḥ patita patitavya kāla upapatteḥ vṛntāt pracyutasya bhūmim pratyāsīdataḥ yat ūrdhvam phalam avadhim kṛtvā ayāvat vṛntam iti saḥ patitaḥ adhvā tad saṃyuktaḥ kālaḥ patita kālaḥ patantam avadhim kṛtvā yāvat bhūmiḥ iti sa patitavyaḥ adhvā tad saṃyuktaḥ kālaḥ patitavya kālaḥ na idānīm tṛtīyodhvā vidyate iti 
NSV_2.1.40	 na virodhāt vartamānaḥ kālaḥ na amti iti bruvan= abhyupagatau kālau bādhate iti etat jñāpana artham sūtram tayoḥ api abhāvaḥ vartamāna abhāve tad apekṣa tvāt vartamāna apekṣau= itara kālau yasya vartamāna kālaḥ na asti tasya vartamāna anabhyupagamena abhyupagatayoḥ api abhāvaḥ iti na ca ayam kālaḥ adhva vyaṅgayaḥ patati iti yā patana kriyā sā yadā uparatā sa patita kālaḥ yadā utpatsyate sa patitavya kālaḥ yadā dravye vartamāne kriyā gṛhyate sa vartamāna kālaḥ iti 
NSV_2.1.41	 atha manyase vartamāna kāla anabhyupagame api atīta anāgatau= itaretara sa apekṣau setsyete iti etat pratiṣedha artham sūtram na atīta anāgatayoḥ itaretara apekṣā siddhiḥ na hi atīta anāgatau itaretara sā apekṣau siddhi atas katham iti vartamāna abhāve kim atītam kim anāgatam katham ca iti na śakyate vaktum na ca itara itara apekṣayā kasyacid siddhiḥ asti yasmāt eka abhāve anyatara abhāvāt dvaya abhāvaḥ tasmāt asti vartamānaḥ kālaḥ 
NSV_2.1.42	 artha sadbhāva vyaṅgyaḥ ca ayam vartamānaḥ kālaḥ vidyate dravyam vidyate guṇaḥ vidyate karma iti yasya ca ayam na asti tasya vartamāna abhāve sarva agrahaṇam pratyakṣa anupapatteḥ pratyakṣam indriya artha sannikarṣeṇa bhavati na ca avidyamānam asat indriyeṇa sat nikṛṣyate tatas ca pratyakṣa anupapattau tad pūrvaka tvāt anumāna āgamayoḥ api anupapattiḥ tatas ca sarva agrahaṇam iti 
NSV_2.1.43	 kiñca kriyamāṇa tā kṛta tā kartavyatā upapatteḥ tu ubhayathā grahaṇam atra yā uparatā kriyā sā kṛta tā vā cikīrṣitā sā kartavyatā yā vidyamānā sā kriyamāṇa tā tat evam kriyā santāna sthaḥ traikālya samāhāraḥ pacati iti vartamāna grahaṇena gṛhyate kriyā santānā vicchedaḥ dṛśyate na ārambhaḥ na uparamaḥ ca saḥ ayam ubhayathā vartamāna kālaḥ siddhaḥ 
NSV_2.1.44	 atha upamānam parīkṣyate kim punar upamānam prasiddha sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam upamānam iti uktam tasya ākṣepaḥ atyanta prāya eka deśa sādharmyāt upamāna asiddhiḥ na atyanta sādharmyāt upamānam bhavati yathā gauḥ evam gauḥ iti prāyas sādharmyāt upamānam na siddhayati yathā anaḍvān evam mahiṣaḥ iti eka deśa sādharmyāt upamānam na siddhyati na hi sarveṇa sarvam upamīyate 
NSV_2.1.45	 prasiddha sādharmyāt upamāna siddheḥ yathā ukta doṣa anupapattiḥ na sādharmyasya kṛtsna māyā alpa bhāgam āśritya upamānam pravartate kim tarhi prasiddha sādharmyāt sādhya sādhana bhāvam āśritya pravartate yatra etat asti tatra upamānam na śakyate pratiṣeddhum iti prāya śabdaḥ kiñcid nyūna tām abhidhatte atyanta sādharmyāt upamānam asti yatra tad kriyayā eva tat kriyā upamīyate yathā rāma rāvaṇayoḥ yuddham rāma rāvaṇayoḥ iva yatra anaḍuhaḥ bala prakarṣa jijñāsā bhavati tatra prāyas sādharmyeṇa yathā mahiṣaḥ tathā anaḍvān iti yadā tu sat mātram jijñāsitam bhavati tadā sarveṇa sarvasya upamānam bhavati yathā meroḥ sattā tathā sarṣapasya iti tasmāt apratiṣedhaḥ 
NSV_2.1.46–2.1.48	 astu tarhi upamānam anumānam pratyakṣeṇa apratyakṣa siddheḥ yathā dhūmena pratyakṣeṇa apratyakṣasya agneḥ grahaṇam anumānam eva gavā pratyakṣeṇā apratyakṣasya gavayasya pratipattiḥ iti na idam anumānāt viśiṣyate iti tasya aparijñānāt na bhavatā upamāna lakṣaṇam vyajñāyi na apratyakṣe gavaye pramāṇa artham upamānasya paśyāmaḥ kaḥ upamāna arthaḥ apratyakṣe api gavaye yā saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandha pratipattiḥ iti proktam eva na evam anumānam iti pūrva pakṣyāha para artham upamānam iti ced na svayam api adhyavasāyāt anumānam sva artham para artham ca upamānam para artham eva atas anumāna bhinnam upamānam iti ced manyase tat na asti kutas svayam api adhyavasāyam janayet yāvatā eva tat vākyam uccārayituḥ adhyavasāyam janayati tasmāt svārtham api iti anumānam eva iti tathā iti upasaṃhārāt upamāna siddheḥ na aviśeṣaḥ pratipatti bhedāt ca na anumānam evam bhavati yathā dhūmaḥ tatha agniḥ iti asti tu upamāne yathā gauḥ evam gavayaḥ iti 
NSV_2.1.49	 śabdaḥ anumānam arthasya anupalabdheḥ anumeya tvāt śabdaḥ anumānam anumānam eva na pramāṇa antaram iti arthaḥ kutas pratyakṣataḥ anupalabdheḥ śabda arthasya anumeya tvāt yathā ca anupalabhyamānaḥ liṅgī mitena liṅgena paścāt mīyate iti anumānam tathā eva mitena śabdena arthaḥ anupalabhyamānaḥ paścāt mīyate iti anumānam śabdaḥ iti arthaḥ 
NSV_2.1.50–2.1.51	 upalabdheḥ advi pravṛtti tvāt pramāṇa antara bhāve dvi pravṛttiḥ upalabdhiḥ anyathā hi ulabdhiḥ anumāne anyathā upamāne iti tat vyākhyātam śabda anumānayoḥ upalabdhiḥ at vipravṛttiḥ yathā anumāne pravartate tathā śabde api iti śabdaḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt anumānam eva sambandhāt ca śabdaḥ anumānam iti vartate liṅga liṅgi vat śabda arthayoḥ saṃbandhāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NSV_2.1.52	 yat tāvat arthasya anumeya tvāt iti tat na āpta upadeśa sāmarthyāt śabdāt artha sampratyayaḥ svarga ādeḥ apratyakṣasya na śabda mātrāt sampratyayaḥ kim tarhi āptaiḥ ayam prayuktaḥ iti atas sampratyayaḥ viparyaye sampratyayasya abhāvāt na tu evam anumānam iti yat punar etat upalabdheḥ advi pravṛtti tvāt iti ayam eva śabda anumānayoḥ upalabdheḥ pravṛtti bhedaḥ tatra viśeṣe satya hetuḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt iti yat punar idam sambandhāt ca iti asti śabda arthayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ anujñātaḥ asti ca pratiṣiddhaḥ asya śabdasya idam vācyam iti vākyasya artha viśeṣaḥ anujñātaḥ prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ ca pratiṣiddhaḥ kasmāt pramāṇataḥ anupalabdheḥ pratyakṣataḥ tāvat śabda artha prāpteḥ na upalabdhiḥ atīndriya tvāt yena indriyeṇa śabdaḥ gṛhyate na tena tasya arthaḥ gṛhyate atas tad prāptiḥ api tasya āviṣaya iti 
NSV_2.1.53–2.1.54	 atha khalu ayam pūraṇa pradāha pāṭana anupalabdheḥ ca sambandha abhāvaḥ sthāna kāraṇa tā bhāvāt iti ca arthaḥ āsya eka deśe sthāna karaṇa uccāraṇīyaḥ śabdaḥ tad antike arthaḥ iti anna agni asi śabda uccāraṇe pūraṇa pradāha pāṭanāni prasajyeran na ca pragṛhyate tad agrahaṇāt na anumeyaḥ prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥ iti pūrva pakṣa vādī āha śabda artha vyavasthānāt apratiṣedhaḥ śabda artha pratyayasya vyavasthā darśanāt anumīyate asti śabda artha saṃbandhaḥ vyavasthā kāraṇam asaṃbandhe hi śabda mātrāt artha mātre pratyaya prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt apratiṣedhaḥ saṃbandhasya iti 
NSV_2.1.55	 atra ayam samādhiḥ na sāmayika tvāt śabda artha sampratyayasya na saṃbandha kāritam śabda artha vyavasthānam kim tarhi samaya kāritam kaḥ punar ayam samayaḥ asya śabdasya idam abhidheyam iti abhidhāna abhidheya niyamaḥ tasmin= upayukte śabda artha saṃpratyayaḥ vyavatiṣṭhate saṃbandha vādinām api ca ayam avarjanīyaḥ iti 
NSV_2.1.56	 jāti viśeṣe ca aniyamāt sāmayikaḥ śabdāt artha sampratyayaḥ na svābhāvikaḥ ṛṣi āri amlecchānām yathākāmam śabda viniyogaḥ artha pratyāyanāya bhavati svābhāvike hi śabdasya artha pratyāyaka tve yathākāmam na syāt yathā āditya prakāśasya rūpa pratyaya hetu tvam jāti viśeṣam na vyabhicarati jāti viśeṣa śabdena punar deśa viśeṣaḥ abhidhīyate 
NSV_2.1.57	 tad aprāmāṇyam anṛta vyāghāta punarukta doṣebhyaḥ tad iti adhikṛta śabda abhidhānāt śabda viśeṣa adhikāraḥ yasmāt prakaraṇena prāptam api śabdam tat śabdena abhidhatte punar tat jñāpayati śabda viśeṣam pratīyam cintā na tu śabda mātram tad aprāmāṇyam arthasya apratyāyaka tvam anṛta tvam anyathārtha abhidhānam vyādhātaḥ padayoḥ vākyayoḥ vā saha asaṃbhavaḥ punaruktam pūrva abhihita abhidhānam putra kāmena iṣṭau saṃsthitāyām na putra janma dṛśyate dṛṣṭa arthasya vākyasya anṛta tvāt adṛṣṭa artham api agnihotram juhuyāta svarga kāmaḥ ityādi vākyam anṛtam iti jñāyate vihita vyāghāta doṣāt ca havane udite hotavyam anudite hotavya samaya adhyuṣite hotavyam iti vidhāya vihitam vyāhanti śyavaḥ asya āhutim abhyavaharati yaḥ udite juhoti śabalaḥ asvāhutim abhyavaharati yaḥ anudite juhoti śyāma śabalau= asya āhutim abhyavaharataḥ yaḥ samaya adhyuṣite juhoti vyāghātāt ca anyatarat mithyā iti punarukti doṣāt ca abhyāse codyamāne triḥprathamām anvāha tris uttamām iti punarukta doṣaḥ pramatta vākya vat idam api na mānam 
NSV_2.1.58	 karma kartṛ sādhana vaiguṇyāt yat tāvat amṛta tvāt apramāṇam vedaḥ iti tat atra vicāraṇīyam kim phala adarśanam vākyānām apramāṇa tvāt āhosvit karma kartṛ sādhana vaiguṇyāt iti vayam tu brūmaḥ karma kartṛ sādhana vaiguṇyāt iti phala adarśanāt tu kāraṇānām asāmarthyam gamyate tatra karma vaiguṇyam samīha abhreṣaḥ kartṛ vaiguṇyam avidvān prayoktā kapūyā caraṇaḥ ca sādhana vaiguṇyam haviḥ asaṃskṛtam upahatam iti guṇa yogena phala niṣpatti darśanāt na ca idam laukikāt bhidyate putra iṣṭyā putra kāmaḥ yajeta iti 
NSV_2.1.59–2.1.60	 atha na vyāghātaḥ iti āha abhyupetya kāla bhede doṣa vacanāt yaḥ abhyupagatam havana kālam bhinatti tatonyatra juhoti tatra ayam abhyupagata kāla bhede doṣaḥ ucyate śyāvaḥ asya āhutim abhyavaharati yaḥ udite juhoti iti idam vākyam vidhi bhreṣe nindā vacanam anuvāda upapatteḥ ca na punarukta doṣaḥ abhyāsaḥ iti prakṛtam anarthakaḥ abhyāsaḥ punarukta doṣam āvahati arthavān eva abhyāsaḥ anuvādaḥ saḥ ayam abhyāsaḥ triḥprathamām anvāha tris uttamām iti anuvādaḥ upapadyate arthava tvāt tris vacanena hi prathama uttamayoḥ pañcadaśa tvam sāmidhenīnām bhavati 
NSV_2.1.61–2.1.63	 vākya vibhāgasya ca artha grahaṇāt manu ādi vākya vat samastāni veda vākyāni artha vibhāgavanti tasmāt pramāṇam vibhāgaḥ ca brāhmaṇa vākyānām trividhaḥ vidhi artha vāda anuvāda vacana viniyogāt vidhivacanāni arthavāda vacanāni anuvāda vacanāni iti tridhā khalu veda vākyāni tatra tāvat vidhiḥ vidha yakaḥ yat vākyam vidhāyakam deśakam sa vidhiḥ vidhiḥ tu niyogaḥ anujñā vā yat vākyam vidhatte idam kuryāt iti sa niyogaḥ yatra kartāram anujānāti tad anujñā vākyam tat yathā agnihotra vākyam eva etat sādhana avāpti pūrvaka tvam anujānāti 
NSV_2.1.64	 stutiḥ nindā para kṛtiḥ purākalpaḥ iti artha vādaḥ vidheḥ phala vāda lakṣaṇā yā praśaṃsā sā stutiḥ sarva jitā vai devāḥ sarvam ayajan ityādi aniṣṭa phala vādaḥ nindā saḥ eṣa vāva prathamaḥ yajñaḥ yajñānām yat jyotiṣṭomaḥ yaḥ etena yajñenā aniṣṭvā anyena yajate gartapatyam eva etat jīryate vā ityādi anya kartṛkasya vyāhatasya vidheḥ vādaḥ parakṛtiḥ hutvā vapām eva agre abhidhārayati atha pṛṣadājyam tat uha carakādhvaryavaḥ pṛṣadājyam eva agre abhivārayati agneḥ prāṇāḥ pṛṣadājya stomam iti evam abhidadhati iti evamādi aitihya samācaritaḥ vidhiḥ purākalpaḥ tasmāt vā etena brāhmaṇāḥ bahiṣpavamānam samastam astauṣan katham para kṛti puga kalpau= artha vādau= iti stuti nindā vākyena abhisaṃbandhāt vidhi āśrayasya kasyacid arthasya dyotanāt artha vādaḥ iti 
NSV_2.1.65–2.1.67	 vidhi vihitasya anuvacanam anuvādaḥ vidhi anuvacanam ca anuvādaḥ vihita anuvacanam ca pūrvaḥ śabda anuvādaḥ aparaḥ artha anuvādaḥ yathā punar uktam dvividham evam anuvādaḥ api śabda punaruktam artha punaruktam ca iti tatra ādyaḥ yathā anityaḥ anityaḥ iti artha punaruktam anityaḥ nirodha dharmakaḥ iti na anuvāda punaruktayoḥ viśeṣaḥ śabda abhyāsa upapatteḥ punaruktam asādhu sādhuḥ anuvādaḥ iti ayam viśeṣaḥ na upapadyate kasmāt ubhayatra api pratīta arthaḥ śabdaḥ abhyasyate iti ubhayam asādhu iti śīghratara gamana upadeśa vat abhyāsāt na aviśeṣaḥ śīghratara gamana upadeśa vat śīghram śīghram gamyatām śīghrataram gamyatām iti kriyā atiśayaḥ abhyāsena eva ucyate evam anuvādaḥ artha viśeṣeṇa asti punar ukte tu na kvaścid viśeṣaḥ gamyate iti mahān viśeṣaḥ punar ukta anuvādayoḥ 
NSV_2.1.68	 kim punar pratiṣedha hetutva uddhārāt eva pramāṇa tā veda vākyānām siddhāḥ na kintarhi mantra āyurveda prāmāṇya vat ca tad prāmāṇyam āpta prāmāṇyāt caśabdaḥ pūrva hetu anukarṣaṇa arthaḥ yathā mantra āyurveda vākyāni puruṣa viśeṣa abhihita tvāt pramāṇam tathā veda vākyāni iti kim punar āptānām pramāṇa tvam sākṣātkṛta dharmatā bhūta dayā yathābhūta artha cikhyā payiṣā ca iti prayogaḥ tu pramāṇam veda vākyāni vaktṛ viśeṣa abhihita tvāt mantra āyurveda vākya vat iti na vā asiddhaḥ hetuḥ iti vaktavyam veda vākyāni api pauruṣeyāṇi vākya tvāt laukika vākya vat iti anumānena hetoḥ siddha tvāt 
NSV_2.2.1	 pratyakṣa anumāna upamāna śabdāḥ pamāṇāni iti sūtram tasya ākṣepaḥ na catuṣṭvam aitihya arthāpatti sambhava abhāva prāmāṇyāt ayathārthaḥ ayam pramāṇa uddeśaḥ na hi catvāri eva pramāṇāni aitihya ādīni api pramāṇāni iti anirdiṣṭa vaktṛkam pravāda pāramparyam aitihyam yasmin vākye abhidhīyamānāt arthāt anya ūrthaḥ pratipādyate saḥ arthāpattiḥ yathā asatsu megheṣu vṛrṣṭina bhavati kim atra āpādyate satsu bhavati iti saṃbhavaḥ nāma avinābhāvinaḥ arthasya sattā grahaṇāt anyasya sattā grahaṇam yathā droṇasya sattā grahaṇāt āḍhakasya satā grahaṇam tasmāt prasthasya iti abhāvaḥ pratyanīkasya grahaṇāt virodhinaḥ grahaṇam yathā vidhārake vāyu abhra saṃyoge sati guru tva pratibandhāt apām pātaḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ tad apāma pātena viroghinam vāyu abhra saṃyogam pratipadyate iti 
NSV_2.2.2	 satyam etāni pramāṇāni na pramāṇa antarāṇi iti āha śabdaḥ aitihya anartha antara bhāvāt anumāne arthāpatti sambhava abhāva anartha antara bhāvāt ca apratiṣedhaḥ anupapannaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ arthāpatti sambhava abhāvānām anumāne antar bhābaḥ saṃbhavati tathā hi pratyakṣeṇa hi apratyakṣasya saṃbandhasya pratipattiḥ anumānam tathā ca arthāpatti saṃbhava abhāvāḥ iti eteṣām udāharaṇeṣu śabdaḥ aitihyam antar bhavati tat evam antar bhāvāt na pṛthak upadeśaḥ 
NSV_2.2.3	 nanu arthāpatteḥ pramāṇa tvena abhyanujñā na upapadyate tathā hi iyam arthāpattiḥ apramāṇam anaikāntika tvāt asatsu megheṣu vṛṣṭiḥ na bhavati iti arthāpattiḥ sā ca anaikāntikī satsu api megheṣu ekadā vṛṣṭiḥ na bhavati iti arthāpatti mātrasya pakṣīkaraṇe tāvat anaikāntika tvam avyāpakam atha anaikāntikī yā sā pakṣīkriyate abhyupagacchāmaḥ vayam api anaikāntikya pramāṇam iti na hi asau sākṣāt arthāpattiḥ iti 
NSV_2.2.4–2.2.5	 anartha āpatta vartha apati abhimānāt satsu megheṣu vṛṣṭiḥ tu bhavati iti kāraṇa pratibandhaḥ asau na tad arthāpatteḥ prameyam kintu asyāḥ prameyam sati kāraṇe kāryam bhavati iti sā iyam katham anaikāntikī yadi asati api kāraṇe kāryam utpadyate tat tu na dṛṣṭam iti na kvacid api anaikāntika tvam pratiṣedha aprāmāṇyam ca anaikāntika tvāt yaḥ ayam bhavatā pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate artha aparttina pramāṇam anaikāntika tvāt iti ayam api anaikāntikaḥ sattā apratiṣedhāt na anena pratiṣedhena arthāpatteḥ sattā pratiṣidhyate katham na sattā pratiṣedhaḥ arthāpatti viśeṣaḥ hi atra pratiṣidhyate na arthāpatti mātram tena sattā pratiṣedhāt anekāntika tā bhavati 
NSV_2.2.6–2.2.7	 atha manyase na pratiṣedhasya satvam viṣayaḥ kim tarhi pramāṇa tvam saḥ ayam pratiṣedhaḥ sva viṣaye pravartamānaḥ na anaikāntikaḥ bhavitum arhati iti tad prāmāṇye vā na artha apatya prāmāṇyam arthāpattiḥ api sva viṣaye vartamānā pramāṇam bhavitum arhati iti na abhāva prāmāṇyam prameyāḥ asiddheḥ yat aviṣayam tad apramāṇam yathā go śabgaḥ aśva pratipādane tathā ca abhāvaḥ tasmāt apramāṇam iti kaḥ ca eva māhābhāvaḥ pramāṇam iti api tu abhāva viṣayā pratipattiḥ pramāṇam 
NSV_2.2.8	 tatra anekadhā minnasya bhāva prapañcasya udāharaṇa artham sūtram lakṣiteṣu alakṣaṇa lakṣita tvāt alakṣitānām tat prameya siddheḥ alakṣitāni vāsāṃsi ānayā iti prayuktaḥ puruṣaḥ ubhaya sannidhau yeṣu vā satsu lakṣaṇāni na paśyati tāni lakṣaṇa abhāvena pratipadyate preṣaṇa sampratipatyoḥ eka viṣaya tvāt pratipadya ca ānayati pratipatti hetuḥ ca pramāṇam tatas ca tasya abhāvasya sidhyati prameyam 
NSV_2.2.9	 asati arthe na abhāvaḥ iti ced na anya lakṣaṇa upapatteḥ yatra bhūtvā kiñcid na bhavati tatra tasya abhāvaḥ upapadyate alakṣiteṣu vāsassu na lakṣaṇāni bhūtvā bhavanti tena teṣu lakṣaṇa abhāvaḥ anupapannaḥ iti na anya lakṣaṇa upapatteḥ yathā ayam anyeṣu vāsassu lakṣaṇa upapattim paśyati na evam alakṣiteṣu saḥ ayam lakṣaṇānām abhāvam paśyan= abhāvena artham pratipadyate iti 
NSV_2.2.10–2.2.12	 atra pūrva pakṣa vādyāha tad siddheḥ alakṣiteṣu ahetuḥ lakṣiteṣu yāni ca vidyante lakṣaṇāni tāni na kasyacid na santi iti yāni khalu bhavanti teṣām abhāvaḥ vyāhate iti atra samādhiḥ na lakṣaṇa vā āsthita apekṣa siddheḥ na brūmaḥ yāni yatra bhavanti teṣām tatra eva abhāvaḥ iti kintu keṣucid lakṣāṇāni avasthitāni apekṣya yeṣu tāni na bhavanti tāni lakṣaṇa abhāvena pratipadyante iti prāk utpatteḥ abhāva upapatteḥ ca abhāvat vaividhyam khalu bhavati prāk utpatteḥ avidyamāna tā ūrdhvam ca vināśāt avidyamāna tā iti tatra yaḥ ayam vināśāt abhāvaḥ lakṣaṇānām alakṣiteṣu vāsassu vā 
NSV_2.2.13^1	 āpta upadeśaḥ śabdaḥ iti śabdasya pramāṇa bhāve viśeṣaṇam bruvatā nānā prakārḥ prakāraḥ śabdaḥ iti jñāpyate tad sāmānyena vicāraḥ kim nityaḥ atha anityaḥ iti vimarśa hetu anuyoge ca vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ ākāśa guṇaḥ śabdaḥ tad gata mahatva vat nityaḥ abhivyakti dharmakaḥ iti eke gandha ādi saha varti dravyeṣu sanniviṣṭaḥ gandha ādi vat avasthitaḥ abhivyakti dharmaḥ iti apare ākāśa guṇaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti nirodha dharmakaḥ buddhi vat iti apare mahābhūta saṅkṣobha jaḥ śabdaḥ anāśritaḥ utpatti dharmakaḥ nirodha dharmakaḥ iti antye atas saṃśayaḥ kim atra tattvam iti anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti uttaram ādima tvāt aindriyaka tvāt kṛtaka vat upacārāt ca saṃyoga vibhāga kāraṇakaḥ hi śabdaḥ iti sāṃśayikam etat kim utpatti kāraṇam saṃyoga vibhāgau śabdasya āhosvit abhivyakti kāraṇam iti atas āha aindriyaka tvāt iti sāmānyavat tve sati bahis indriya janu alaukika pratyakṣa viṣaya tvāt iti arthaḥ tatas kim yat indriya pratyāsatti grāhya aindriyakaḥ tatas na vyajyate na vyajyamānasya indriyeṇa pratyāsattiḥ yuktā katham iti 
NSV_2.2.13^2	 śrotram tāvat śabda deśam na gacchati tasya ākāśa prakṛtika tvāt ākāśasya ca amūrta tvāt gamana anupapatteḥ śabdaḥ api na gacchati niṣkriya tvāt eva na ca aprāptasya grahaṇam asti sarva śabda upalabdhi prasaṅgāt pāriśeṣyāt śabda santāna siddhiḥ evam santānena aindriyaka tvāt anityaḥ iti atha manyase ekaḥ eva ayam śabdaḥ vitati a ākāśam avatiṣṭhate sa vyavasthita saṃyoga vibhāgābhyām vyaktaḥ san upalabhyate iti tat ca na sarva upalabdhi prasaṅgāt itas ca utpadyate kṛtaka vat upacārāt kṛtaka vat upacaryate tīvram mandram iti tīvra sukham mandram duḥkham iti ca upacaryate 
NSV_2.2.13^3	 tīvraḥ śabdaḥ mandraḥ śabdaḥ iti asya prayogaḥ anitya ṣabdaḥ tīvra mandra viṣaya tvāt sukha duḥkha vat iti atha manyase prayogasya vyañjakasya tīvra mandra tayā śabda grahaṇasya tīvra mandra tā bhavati na śabdaḥ bhidyate yathā prakāśasya tīvra mandra tayā rūpa grahaṇasya iti tat ca na evam abhibhava upapatteḥ tīvraḥ bherī śabdaḥ mandram tantrī svanam abhibhavati na tandaḥ na ca śabda grahaṇayoḥ abhibhāvya abhibhāvaka bhāvaḥ tayoḥ yugapad a sammavāt tasmāt utpadyate śabdaḥ na abhivyajyate iti 
NSV_2.2.14	 na ghaṭa abhāva sāmānya nitya tvāt nityeṣu api anitya vat upacārāt ca asya sūtrasya pūrva hetūnām anaikāntika tva jñāpanam arthaḥ na khalu ādimat tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ vyabhicārāt ādimataḥ khalu ghaṭa pradhvaṃsa abhāvasya nitya tvam dṛṣṭam aindriyaka tvāt iti etat api vyabhicarasi aindriyakam sāmānyam nityam ca iti yat api kṛtaka vat upacārāt iti tat api vyabhicarati nityeṣu api anitya vat upacāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ ākāśasya pradeśaḥ ātmanaḥ pradeśaḥ iti 
NSV_2.2.15	 tattva bhāktayoḥ nānātvasya vibhāgāt avyabhicāraḥ nityam iti atra kim tāvat tattvam ubhaya anta aparicchinna vastu sattā saṃbandhaḥ nitya tā tad viparyayāt anitya tā etat ca abhāve na asti tena bhāktam tu nitya tvam tatra bhavitum arhati kā punar iyam bhaktiḥ prāgabhāvamya kāraṇāḥ abhāvaḥ pradhvaṃsa abhāvasya vināśa abhāvaḥ sāmānyam nityaḥ iva nityaḥ ghaṭa abhāvaḥ iti na punar nityaḥ eva iti 
NSV_2.2.16	 yat api sāmānya nitya tvāt iti indriya pratyāsatti grāhya tvāt iti santāna anumānā viśeṣaṇāt avyabhicāraḥ iti prakṛtam na vayam aindriya katyāt iti anena śabda anitya tvam sādhayāmaḥ api tu nitya tve śabdasya abhivyaktim pratiṣedhāmaḥ na hi vyajyamānasya śabdasya aindriyaka tvam yuktam iti uktam purastāt tena indriya pratyāsatti grāhya tvāt santāna anumānam tena anitya tvam iti 
NSV_2.2.17–2.2.18	 yat api manyeta nityeṣu api anitya vat upacārāt iti tat api kāraṇa dravyasya pradeśa śabdena abhidhānāt nityeṣu api avyabhicāraḥ iti na hi nityānām dravyāṇām ākāśa ātma ādīnām pradeśa śabdena kāraṇam ucyate yathā kṛtakasya kim iti na ucyate avidyamāna tvāt avidyamāna tvam ca pramāṇataḥ anupalabdheḥ yadi ākāśam niṣpradeśam pratipadyase nanu lokaḥ virudhyate pūrva bhāgena vyāptaḥ ādityaḥ iti na anyathā tad upapatteḥ saṃyogasya avyāpya vṛtti tve pradeśa śabdena abhidhīyamāne na loka virodhaḥ paricchinnayoḥ hi pradeśayoḥ āmalakayoḥ saṃyogaḥ na vyāpya vartate ākāśa saṃyogaḥ hi na ākāśam vyāpnoti kasmāt pradeśa vat dravya sāmānyāt pradeśa vat ākāśam iti bhāktaḥ pratyayaḥ etena ātma pradeśaḥ vyākhyātaḥ parīkṣitā ca tīvra manda tā śabdasya tattvam na bhakti kṛtā iti ye tu śabdam nityam kalpayanti te idam paryanuyojyāḥ idam asti idam na asti iti etat bhavantaḥ katham pratipadyante iti te evam uktāḥ pratibruvate pramāṇataḥ upalabdheḥ anupalabdheḥ ca iti avidyamānaḥ tarhi śabdaḥ 
NSV_2.2.19	 evam tattvaḥ ukte jātyā pratyavatiṣṭhate sā ca jātiḥ tad anupalabdheḥ anupalambhāt āvaraṇa upapattiḥ yadi anupalambhāt āvaraṇam na asti āvaraṇa anupalabdhiḥ api tarhi anupalambhāt na asti tasyāḥ abhāvāt apratiṣiddham āvaraṇam iti katham bhavān jānīte nā aavaraṇa anupalabdhiḥ upalabhyate iti ayam khalu loke āvaraṇam anupalabhamānaḥ pratyātmam vedayate sā iyam āvaraṇa upalabdhi vat āvaraṇāḥ anupalabdhiḥ api saṃvedya eva iti evam ca sati apahata viṣayam uttara vākyam asti iti 
NSV_2.2.20	 abhyanujñā vādena tu ucyate jātivādimāḥ anupalambhāt api anupalabdhi sadbhāvāt nāḥ aavaraṇa anupapattiḥ anupalambhāt yathā anupalabhyamānā api a āvaraṇa anupalabdhiḥ asti evam anupalabhyamānam api āvaraṇam asti iti yadi abhyanujānāti bhavān anupalabhyamāna āvaraṇa anupalabdhiḥ asti iti abhyanujñāya ca vadati na asti āvaraṇam anupalambhāt iti etasmin= abhyanujñā vāde pratipatti niyamaḥ na upapadyate iti 
NSV_2.2.21	 anupalambha ātmaka tvāt anupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ yat upalabhyate tat asti yat na upalabhyate tat na asti iti anupalambha ātmakaḥ asat iti vyavasthitam upalabdhi abhāvaḥ ca anupalabdhiḥ sā iyam abhāvāt na upalabhyate sat ca khalu āvaraṇam tasya upalabdhyā bhavitavyam na ca upalabhyate tasmāt na asti iti tatra yat uktam nā avaraṇa anupapattiḥ anupalambhāt iti etat ayuktam iti arthaḥ evam tāvat svasa dhana sthityā vyavasthitam anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti 
NSV_2.2.22–2.2.24	 atha śabdasya nitya tvam pratijānānāḥ kasmāt hetoḥ pratijānate asparśa tvāt atra prayogaḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśa tvāt ākāśa ādi vat iti asya vyabhicāra pradarśana artham sūtram na karmā anitya tvāt sādhya vaidharmya udāharaṇam na aṇu nitya tvāt ittham tu sādharmya vaidharmya udāharaṇam ubhayasmin= udāharaṇe vyabhicārāt ahetuḥ 
NSV_2.2.25–2.2.26	 ayam tarhi nitya tve hetuḥ sampradānāt saṃpradīyamānam avatthitam eva dṛṣṭam sampradīyate śabdaḥ ācāryeṇa antevāsine tasmāt avasthitaḥ iti tad antarāa anupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ atra nirākurvat sūtram tad antarāā iti gurūṇām upadeśaḥ hi tadā bhavati yadā śiṣyaḥ upasannaḥ bhavati yadi tatas praṅnityaḥ eva śabdaḥ tiṣṭhet tadā upalabhyeta na ca tathā tasmāt na asti iti anityaḥ eva iti arthaḥ 
NSV_2.2.27–2.2.28	 adhyāpanāt apratiṣedhaḥ na virādhaḥ anumānataḥ upalabdheḥ kim anumānam adhyāpanam adhyāpanam nāma dīyamānasya saṃpradāna prāptiḥ dātṛ pratigṛhītroḥ antarāle śabdaḥ asti adhyāpanāt ubhayoḥ pakṣayoḥ anyatarasya adhyāpanāt apratiṣedhaḥ na śabdasyadhyāpanam pratiṣidhyate api tu nṛtya upadeśana vat anityasya adhyāpanam iti ucyate iti 
NSV_2.2.29–2.2.30	 ayam tarhi śabdasya avasthāne hetuḥ abhyāsāt abhyasyamānam avasthitam dṛṣṭam pañca kṛtvas rūpam paśyati iti rūpam avasthitam punar dṛśyate daśa kṛtvas adhītaḥ anuvākaḥ iti atra śabde bhavati abhyāsaḥ tasmāt avasthitasya śabdasya punar punar uccāraṇam abhyāsaḥ iti asya anaikāntika tva pradarśana artham sūtram na anya tvepi abhyāsa upacārāt anavasthānepyasya ca abhyāsa abhidhānam bhavati dvis nṛtyatu bhavān tris nṛtyatu bhavān iti atas vyabhicāra āt ayam ahetuḥ iti 
NSV_2.2.31–2.2.32	 anyat anyasmāt ananya tvāt ananyat iti anya tā abhāvaḥ yat idam anyat iti manyase tad sva rtthena ananya tvāt anyat na bhavati evam anyatāyāḥ abhāvaḥ tatra yat uktam anya tvepi abhyāsa upacārāt iti tat etat ayuktam iti atha siddhānta vādinā anya śabda prayogaḥ pratīṣidhyate tad abhāve na asti ananya tā tayoḥ itaretara apekṣa siddheḥ ayam tarhi hetuḥ pratyabhijñānāt tad abhāve pratyabhijñānam na dṛṣṭam maṇi ādiṣu asti ca pratyabhijñānam śabde saḥ eva ayam go śabdaḥ iti tasmāt avatiṣṭhate śabdaḥ iti 
NSV_2.2.33–2.2.34	 vināśa kāraṇāḥ anupalabdheḥ yadi anityam tasya tasya vināśaḥ kāraṇāt bhavati yathā loṣṭhasya kāraṇa dravya vibhāgāt śabdaḥ ced anityaḥ tasya vināśa kāraṇam upalabhyeta na ca upalabhyate tasmāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti aśravaṇa kāraṇāḥ anupalabdhesantata śravaṇa prasaṅgaḥ yathā vināśa kāraṇāḥ anupalabdheḥ avināśa prasaṅgaḥ tathā aśravaṇa kāraṇāḥ anupalabdheḥ satatam śravaṇa prasaṅgaḥ vyañjaka abhāvāt agrahaṇam iti ced pratiṣiddham vyañjakam atha vidyamānasya nirnimittam śravaṇam evam yadi vidyamānasya nirnimittaḥ vināśaḥ iti 
NSV_2.2.35	 upalabhyamāne ca anupalabdheḥ asattvāt anapadeśaḥ anumānāt upalabhyamāne śabdasya vināśa kāraṇe vināśa kāraṇā anupalabdheḥ asattvāt iti anapadeśaḥ kim idam anumānam iti ced santāna upapattiḥ ghaṇṭāyām abhihanyamānāyām tāraḥ tārataraḥ mandraḥ mandataraḥ iti śruteḥ bhedāt nānā śabda santānaḥ avicchedena śrūyate tatra nitye śabde ghaṇṭā stham anya gatam vā avasthitam santāna vṛtti vā abhivyakti kāraṇam vācyam yena śruti santānaḥ bhavati iti śabda bhede ca asati śruti bhedaḥ upapādayitavyaḥ anitye ca śabde ghaṇṭā santāna vṛtti saṃyoga sahakāri nimitta antaram saṃskāra bhūtam paṭu mandam anuvartat te tasya anuvṛtyā śabda santāna anuvṛttiḥ tatas paṭu manda bhāvāt ca tīvra manda tā śabdasya iti bhavati tad kṛtaḥ śruti bhedaḥ 
NSV_2.2.36	 nanu ayam saṃskāraḥ na asti anupalabdheḥ iti āha pāṇi nimitta praśleṣāt śabda abhāve na anupalabdhiḥ pāṇi karmaṇā pāṇi ghaṇṭā praśleṣaḥ bhavati tasmin= ca sati saṃskāraḥ nirudhyate tatas ca śabda santānaḥ na utpadyate anutpattau śruti vicchedaḥ yadi saṃskāram śabda utpatti nimittam na pratipadyase pāṇi ghaṇṭā saṃśleṣāt śabda santāna ucchedaḥ na prāpnoti tasmāt nimitta antarasya saṃskāra bhūtasya na anupalabdhiḥ iti 
NSV_2.2.37–2.2.38	 vināśa kāraṇāḥ anupalabdheḥ ca avasthāne tad nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ yāni khalu imāni śabda śravaṇāni na teṣām vināśa kāraṇam bhavatā upapādyate anupapādanāt avasthānam avasthānāt teṣām nitya tvam prasajyate atha na evam tarhi vināśa kāraṇāḥ anupalabdheḥ śabdasya avasthānāt nitya tvam iti asparśa tvāt apratiṣedhaḥ yadi tat na ākāśa guṇaḥ śabdaḥ iti śabdasya ākāśa guṇa tvam pratiṣidhyate ayam anupapannaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kasmāt asparśa tvāt śabda āśrayasya rūpa ādi samāna deśasya agrahaṇe śabda santāna upalabdheḥ asparśa vyāpi dravya āśrayaḥ śabdaḥ iti na kampa samāna āśrayaḥ 
NSV_2.2.39	 pratidravyam rūpa ādi bhiḥ sannikṛṣṭaḥ taiḥ taiḥ samāna deśaḥ vyajyate iti na upapadyate vibhakti antara upapatteḥ ca samāse santāna upapatteḥ ca iti ca arthaḥ vibhāgaḥ ca vibhāga antaram ca vibhakti antaram vidharmāṇaḥ ca śabda svarūpāḥ ca eka dravya āśrayāḥ śrūyante yadi rūpa ādayaḥ śabdāḥ ca pratidravyam samuditāḥ samastāḥ tasmin samāse samudāye yaḥ yathāceti yat sannikṛṣṭaḥ tasya tathājātīyakasya eva śabdasya śravaṇena bhavitavyam rūpa ādi vat 
NSV_2.2.40	 dvividhaḥ ca ayam śabdaḥ varṇa ātmakaḥ dhvani mātraḥ ca tatra varṇa ātmani vikāra ādeśa upadeśāt saṃśayaḥ dadhi atra iti kecid ikāraḥ itvam hitvā yakāra tvam āpadyate iti vikāram manyante kecid tu saṃhitāyām viṣaye ikāraḥ na prayujyate tasya sthāne yakāraḥ prayujyate ādeśaḥ iti evam ubhayam upadiśyate tatra na jñāyate kim tatvam iti ādeśa upadeśaḥ tatvam na vikāra upadeśaḥ 
NSV_2.2.41–2.2.43	 prakṛti vivṛddhau vikāra vivṛddheḥ prakṛti anuvidhānam vikāreṣu dṛṣṭam yakāre tu hrasva dīrdha anuvidhānam na asti tena na vikāri tvam anumīyate iti nyūna samādhika upalabdheḥ vikārāṇām ahetuḥ dravya vikārāḥ nyūnāḥ samāḥ adhikāḥ ca gṛhyante tadvat ayam vikāraḥ nyūnaḥ syāt iti dvividhasya api hetoḥ abhāvāt asādhanam dṛṣṭāntaḥ atra na udāharaṇa sāmarthyāt hetuḥ asti na vaidharmyāt anupasaṃhṛtaḥ ca hetunā dṛṣṭāntaḥ na sādhakaḥ iti pati dṛṣṭānte ca aniyamaḥ prasajyeta yathā anaḍuha sthāne aśvaḥ voḍhum niyuktaḥ na tad vikāraḥ bhavati evam iva ṛṇasya sthāne yakāraḥ prayuktaḥ na tad vikāraḥ iti 
NSV_2.2.44	 dravya vikāra udāharaṇam ca na atulya prakṛtīnām vikāra vikalpāt atulyānām dravyāṇām prakṛti bhāvaḥ vikalpyate vikārāḥ ca prakṛtīḥ anu vidhīyante na tu ivarṇam anuvidhīyate yakāraḥ na jātu nyagrodha bījāt nārikea pādapaḥ bhavati bhavati vā nārikea bījāt nyagrodha pādapaḥ na tvivarṇa bhedam anuvidhīyate yakāraḥ tasmāt anudāharaṇam dravya vikāraḥ iti 
NSV_2.2.45	 asya ākṣepa sūtram dravya vikāra vaiṣamya vat varṇa vikāra vikalpaḥ na prakṛti bhedam avaśyam anuvidhīyante vikārāḥ dravya tvena tulya tvepi prakṛtīnām vikāra vaiṣamya darśanāt evam varṇa tvena tulya tve api vikāra vaiṣamyam tathā hrasva dīrdha tvābhyām vaiṣamye bhaviṣyati prakṛti sāmya iva vikāra vaiṣamyam iti bhāvaḥ 
NSV_2.2.46–2.2.47	 tad pratyākhyāna sūtram na vikāra dharmāḥ anupapatteḥ dravya vikāra tulya tā atra na śaṅkyā vikārāṇām hi ayam dharmaḥ prakṛti anuvidhānam tad bhede ca bhedaḥ prakṛte tad anupapattiḥ hrasva tva ādinā prakṛti bhede api kārya bhedāḥ abhāvāt itas ca na varṇa vikāraḥ vikāra prāptānām apunarāvṛtteḥ yadi vikriyante varṇāḥ punar āpatti na āpnuvanti no khalu kṣīra vikāre kṣīram dṛṣṭam iti 
NSV_2.2.48–2.2.49	 asya ākṣepaḥ suvarṇa ādīnām punar āpatteḥ ahetuḥ suvarṇa vikārāṇām rucaka ādīnā punar suvarṇa tva apatti darśanāt ahetuḥ vikāra prāptānām apunarāvṛtteḥ iti etat ayuktam iti yathā payaḥ dadhi bhāvam āpannam na punar payaḥ bhavati kim evam varṇānām api anāvṛttiḥ atha suvarṇa vat puta rāpattiḥ iti suvarṇa udāharaṇa upapattiḥ ca na tad vikārāṇām suvarṇa bhāvāḥ avyatirekāt avasthitam suvarṇam sarva avastham dṛśyate na evam kaścid śabda ātmā hīyamānena itvena upajāyamānena yatvena dharmaḥ gṛhyate tasmāt suvarṇa udāharaṇam na upapadyate iti 
NSV_2.2.50–2.2.52	 asya ākṣepaḥ varṇa tva avyatirekāt varṇa vikārāṇām apratiṣedhaḥ varṇa vikārāḥ api varṇa tvam na vyabhicaranti yathā suvarṇa vikāraḥ suvarṇa tvam iti sāmānyavataḥ dharma yogaḥ na sāmānyasya kuṇḍala rucakau suvarṇasya dharmau na suvarṇa tvasya iti itas ca varṇa vikāra anupapattiḥ nitya tve avikārāt anitya tve ca anavasthānāt nitya tve na yuktaḥ vikāraḥ vyāghātāt anityāḥ varṇāḥ iti etasmin pakṣe na yuktam avasthānam vikāraḥ punar anavasthitānām varṇānām na bhavati iti
