NSV_2.2.53	 nitya tva pakṣe tāvat samādhiḥ nityānām atīndriya tvāt tad dharma vikalpāt ca varṇa vikārāṇām apratiṣedhaḥ nityāḥ varṇāḥ na vikriyante iti vipratiṣedhaḥ yathā nitya tve sati kiñcid ati indriyam paramāṇu ādi indriya grāhyāḥ ca varṇāḥ evam nitya tve sati kiñcid na vikriyate varṇāḥ tu vikriyante iti dharma vikalpaḥ virodhāt ahetuḥ viruddham hi nitya tvam vikāri tvam ca iti atas iyam vikalpa samā jātiḥ 
NSV_2.2.54	 athā anitya pakṣe samādhiḥ anavasthāyi tve varṇa upalabdhi vat tat vikāra upapattiḥ yathā anavasthāyinām varṇānām śravaṇam bhavati evam eṣām vikāraḥ api bhavati iyam varṇa upalabdhiḥ asambandhāt ahetuḥ na hi varṇa upabdhiḥ varṇa vikāreṇa sambandhāt asamarthāḥ varṇa vikāram anumāpayet atas iyam sādharmya samā jātiḥ 
NSV_2.2.55	 ubhayoḥ api uttaram vikāra dharmi tve nitya tva abhāvāt kāla antare vikāra upapatteḥ ca apratiṣedhaḥ tad dharma vikārāt iti na yuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ na khalu vikāra dharmakam kiñcid nityam upalabhyate iti varṇa upalabdhi vat iti ca na yuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ avagrahe hi dadhi atra iti prayujya ciram sthitvā tatas saṃhitāyām prayuṅkta dadhi atra iti 
NSV_2.2.56–2.2.57	 itas ca varṇa vikāra anupapattiḥ prakṛti aniyamāt varṇa vikārāṇām ikāra sthāne yakāraḥ śrūyate dadhi atra iti yakāra sthāne khalu ikāraḥ sidhyati iti yadi syāt prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ varṇānām tadā prakṛti niyamaḥ syāt dṛṣṭaḥ hi vikārāṇām prakṛti niyamaḥ iti aniyame niyamānnāḥ aniyamaḥ yaḥ ayam prakṛteḥ aniyamaḥ iti uktaḥ aniyamaḥ sa viṣaye niyata tvāt niyamaḥ iti bhavati evañca satya niyamaḥ na asti tatra yat uktam prakṛti aniyamāt iti etat ayuktam iti 
NSV_2.2.58–2.2.59	 niyama aniyama virodhāt aniyame niyamāt ca apratiṣedhaḥ niyamaḥ iti atra artha abhyanujñā aniyamaḥ iti tasya pratiṣedhaḥ anujñā pratiṣedhayoḥ vyāghātāt anartha antara tvam na bhavati kiñca aniyame hi sva viṣaya niyata tvāt niyame sati niyama pratiṣedhaḥ na bhavati iti na varṇāḥ vikriyante guṇa antara āpatti upamarda hrāsa vṛddhi leśa śleṣebhyaḥ tu vikāra upapatteḥ varṇa vikārāḥ guṇa antara āpattiḥ udāt tasya anudātta tvam iti evamādiḥ upamardaḥ nāma eka rūpa nivṛttau rūpa antara upajaniḥ hrāsaḥ dīrghasya hrasvaḥ vṛddhiḥ hrasvasya dīrghaḥ tayoḥ vā plutaḥ leśaḥ lāghavam staḥ iti asteḥ vikāraḥ śleṣaḥ āgamaḥ prakṛteḥ pratyayasya vā ete vikārāḥ ete eva ādeśāḥ ete ced vikārāḥ tahari upapadyante varṇa vikārāḥ iti 
NSV_2.2.60–2.2.61	 te vibhakti antāḥ padam te varṇāḥ yathādarśanam vikṛtāḥ vibhakti antāḥ pada saṃjñakāḥ bhavanti vibhaktiḥ dvayī nāmikya ākhyātikī ca brāhmaṇāḥ paṭhanti iti udāharaṇam upasarga nipātāḥ tarhi vibhakti abhāvāt na pada saṃjñāḥ tatas ca lakṣaṇa antaram vācyam iti na śiṣyate khalu nāmikyāḥ vibhakteḥ avyayāt lopaḥ tayoḥ pada saṃjñā artham nanu śabda anitya tva pakṣe artha pratyayaḥ na prāpnoti antya varṇa kāle pūrva pūrva varṇāḥ anavasthānāt iti na antya varṇāt pūrva varṇa pratisandhāna apekṣāt artha pratyaya upapatteḥ atha nāma padam cintyate vyakti ākṛti jāti sannidhau= upacārāt saṃśayaḥ yasmāt ayam go śabdaḥ vyakti ākṛti jātiṣu avinā abhāvena vartamānāsu prayujyate avinā abhāva vṛttiḥ ca sannidhiḥ atas na jñāyate kim vyaktiḥ padārthaḥ uta ākṛtiḥ uta jātiḥ iti 
NSV_2.2.62	 śabdasya prayoga sāmarthyāt padārtha avadhāraṇam iti prayoga darśana artham sūtram yā śabda samūha tyāga parigraha saṅkhyā vṛddhi apacaya varṇa samāsa anubandhānām vyaktau= upacārāt vyaktiḥ vyaktiḥ padārthaḥ kasmāt yā śabda prabhṛtīnām vyaktau= upacārāt prayogaḥ upacāraḥ prayogaḥ yā gauḥ tiṣṭhati yā gauḥ niṣaṇṇa iti na idam vākyam jāteḥ abhidhāyakam tasyāḥ ekatvena viśeṣaṇam anarthakam gavām samūhaḥ iti bhedāt dravya abhidhānam na jāteḥ abhedāt gām dadāti iti dravyasya tyāgaḥ na jāteḥ amūrta tvāt parigrahaḥ sva tvena abhisambandhaḥ saḥ api mūrtāya avyakteḥ eva sambhavati na jāteḥ saṅkhyā daśa gāvaḥ viṃśatiḥ gāvaḥ iti bhinna dravyam saṅkhyāyate na jātiḥ abhedāt vṛddhiḥ kāraṇavataḥ dravyasya avayava upacayaḥ iti avardhatā aśvaḥ iti niravayavā jātiḥ iti etena apacayaḥ vyākhyātaḥ varṇaḥ kapilā gauḥ iti dravyasya guṇa yogaḥ na sāmānyasya samāsaḥ gohita go sukham ityādi dravyasya sukha yogaḥ na jāteḥ anubandhaḥ svarūpa prajanana santānaḥ gaugām janayati iti tad utpatti dharma tvāt dravye yuktam na jātau 
NSV_2.2.63–2.2.64^1	 asya ca pratiṣedha artham sūtram na tad anavasthānāt na vyaktiḥ padārthaḥ kasmāt anavasthānāt etat uktam bhavati yadi ayam go śabdaḥ vyakti mātra abhidhāyakaḥ abhaviṣyat tena yasyām kasyāṃcid vyaktau pratyayaḥ abhaviṣyat iti yadi vyaktiḥ na padārthaḥ katham yā gauḥ tiṣṭhati iti evamādiḥ nimittāt atat bhāve tad upacāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti tasya pradarśana artham sūtram sahacaraṇa sthāna tādarthya vṛtta māna dhāraṇa sāmīpya yoga sādhana ādhipatyebhyaḥ brāhmaṇa mañca kaṭa rāja saktu candana gaṅgā śā kaṭa anta puruṣeṣu atad bhāve api tad upacāraḥ atadbhāve api tad upacāraḥ iti atad śabda vācyasya arthasya tad śabdena abhidhānam upacāraḥ yathā sahacaraṇāt yaṣṭikām bhojaya iti yaṣṭikā sahacaritaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ abhidhīyate sthānāt mañcāḥ krośanti iti mañca sthāḥ puruṣāḥ abhidhīyante 
NSV_2.2.64^2	 tādarthyāt kaṭārtheṣu vīraṇeṣu vyūhyamāneṣu kaṭam karoti iti vṛttāt kuberaḥ rājā yamaḥ rājā yama vat vartate iti arthaḥ mānāt āḍhakena mitāḥ saktavaḥ āḍhaka saktavaḥ dhāraṇāt tulāyām dhṛtam candanam tulā candanam iti bhavati sāmīpyāt gaṅgāyām gāvaḥ caranti iti deśaḥ abhidhīyate yogāt kṛṣṇena rāgeṇa yuktaḥ śakaṭaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ iti abhidhīyate sādhanāt annam prāṇāḥ iti ādhipatyāt ayam puruṣaḥ kulam ayam gotram iti tatra ayam sahacaraṇāt yogāt vā jāti vācakaḥ śabdaḥ vyaktau prayujyate iti 
NSV_2.2.65	 yadi khalu gauḥ iti padasya na vyaktiḥ arthaḥ astu tarhi ākṛtiḥ tad apekṣa tvāt sattva vyavasthāna siddheḥ ākṛtiḥ padārthaḥ kutas tad apekṣa tvāt sattva vyavasthāna siddheḥ sattva avayavānām tad avayavānām ca niyataḥ vyūhaḥ ākṛtiḥ tasyām gṛhyamāṇāyām sattva vyavasthānam prāṇi vyavasthā sidhyati ayam gauḥ ayam aśvaḥ iti na agṛhyamāṇāyām yasya ca grahaṇāt sattva vyavasthānam sidhyati tam śabdaḥ abhidhātum arhati saḥ asya arthaḥ iti tat api upapadyate tatra jātyā yogaḥ yatra jāti viśiṣṭa dravyam abhidhīyate gauḥ iti na ca avayava vyūhasya jātyā yogaḥ asti tasmāt na ākṛtiḥ padārthaḥ 
NSV_2.2.66–2.2.68	 astu tarhi vyakti ākṛti yuktā ipya prasaṅgāt prokṣaṇa ādīnām mṛd gavake jātiḥ gām prokṣaya gām ānaya gām dehi iti na etāni mṛdgavake prayujyante kutas jāteḥ abhāvāt yat abhāvāt tatra asampratyayaḥ sa padārthaḥ iti na ākṛti vyakti apekṣa tvāt jāti abhivyakteḥ jāteḥ abhivyaktiḥ ākṛti vyaktī apekṣate na agṛhyamāṇayoḥ tayoḥ jāti mātram śuddham gṛhyate tasmāt na jātiḥ padārthaḥ iti kaḥ idānī padārthaḥ iti vyakti ākṛti jātayaḥ tu padārthaḥ tu śabdaḥ viśeṣaṇa arthaḥ kim viśiṣyate pradhāna upasarjana bhāvasya aniyamena padārtha tvam iti 
NSV_2.2.69	 katamā vyaktiḥ katamā ākṛtiḥ katamā jātiḥ iti apekṣāyām vyakti lakṣaṇa pratipādana artham sūtram vyaktiḥ guṇa viśeṣa āśrayaḥ mūrtiḥ yat dravyam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptānām rūpa ādīnām sparśa antānām guṇānām āśrayaḥ tat mūrcchita avayava tvāt mūrtiḥ iti ca ucyate vyakta tvāt avyaktiḥ iti ucyate iti dravyam vyakti lakṣaṇa lakṣitam guṇāḥ ca viśeṣāḥ ca tad āśrayaḥ ca atra tad śabda lopāt guṇa viśeṣa āśraya padena dravyam ucyate karma api guṇa viśeṣa śabda vallabhyate guṇebhyaḥ viśeṣāḥ iti atas tat api vyakta tvāt vyaktiḥ bhavati guṇa viśeṣa grahaṇam kim artham guṇa padena saṅgṛhītāyāḥ ākṛteḥ nirākaraṇa artham ākṛtiḥ saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ sa ca guṇaḥ iti tad nirākaraṇa artham guṇa viśeṣa grahaṇam 
NSV_2.2.70–2.2.71	 ākṛtiḥ jāti liṅga ākhyā yayā jātiḥ liṅgāni ca prakhyāyante tām ākṛtim vidyāt śiraḥ pāṇi pāda ādi mat a ākāra sāmānyena hi go tvam vyajyate atas tad jāti liṅgam tat api tad avayava sāmānyena vyajyate iti tat ubhayam ākṛtiḥ iti samāna prasava ātmikā jātiḥ yā samānām buddhim prasūte bhinneṣu adhikaraṇeṣu yathā bahūni itaretarataḥ na byāvartante yaḥ arthaḥ aneka pratyaya anuvṛtti nimittam tad sāmānyam tat yathā imāni kuṇḍāni iti anuvartate buddhiḥ atra samāna pratyaya utpatti kāraṇam eva jātiḥ iti jātau niyamaḥ na tu samāna pratyaya utpattau jātim antareṇa api samāna pratyaya darśanāt iti tasmāt vyavasthitam vyakti ākṛti jātayaḥ padārthaḥ iti 
NSV_3.1.1^1	 parīkṣitāni pramāṇāni prameyam idānīm parīkṣyate yat viṣayaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ saṃsāram pratanoti yat viṣayam ca samyak jñānam saṃsāram nivartayati tat ca ātma ādi iti ātmā vicāryate kim punar atra vicāryam śarīra indriya manaḥ buddhi prāṇa vṛtti vyatiriktaḥ āhosvit na iti kutas saṃśayaḥ vyapadeśasya ubhayatha asiddheḥ kriyā karaṇayoḥ kartrā saṃbandhasya abhidhānam vyapadeśaḥ sa dvividhaḥ avayavena samudāyasya mūlaiḥ vṛkṣaḥ tiṣṭhati iti anyena vā anyasya vyapadeśaḥ pāśunā vṛścati iti asti ca ayam vyapadeśaḥ cakṣuṣā paśyati iti tatra na avadhāryate kim avayavena samudāyasya deha ādi saṅghataiḥ asya vyapadeśaḥ atha anyena vā anyasya tad vyatiriktasya iti anyena ayam anyasya vyapadeśaḥ kasmāt 
NSV_3.1.1^2	 darśana sparśanābhyām ekārtha grahaṇāt dṛśyate anena iti darśanam cakṣuḥ spṛśyate anena iti sparśanam tvac darśanena dṛṣṭam artham sparśanena pratyabhijānāti yam aham adrākṣam tam aham spṛśāmi iti eka viṣayau= etau pratyayau pratisandhīyete pratisandha na nāma smṛtyā saha eka viṣaya tvam darśana sparśana pratyayayoḥ ghaṭa ādi viṣaya tvāt asambandhaḥ iti ced atha manyase yaḥ etau darśana sparśana pratyayau ghaṭa ādi viṣayau atas na dehāt avyatirekam ātmanaḥ gamayataḥ vyadhikaraṇa tvāt iti tat na sūtra artha aparijñānāt darśana sparśanau= eka kartṛkau iti sūtra arthaḥ saṅghāta kartṛkau darśana sparśana viṣayau pratyayau bhaviṣyate iti na yuktam saṅghātasya nānātva ābādhanāt 
NSV_3.1.2–3.1.3	 na viṣaya vyavasthānāt na deha ādi saṅkhātāt anyaḥ cetanaḥ kasmāt viṣaya vyavasthānāt vyavasthita viṣayāṇi indriyāṇi tāni sva viṣaya grahaṇāt cetanāni evañca sati kim anyena cetanena iti asya parihāraḥ sandigdha tvāt ahetuḥ kim indriyāṇām viṣaya niyamaḥ cetana tvāt āhosvit cetanā upakaraṇa tvāt iti sandihyate vayam tu brūmaḥ cetanā upakaraṇa tve api indriyāṇām grahaṇa nimitta tvāt bhavitum arhati tad vyavasthānāt eva ātma sadbhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ yasmāt eva etāni indriyāṇi vyavasthita viṣayāṇi atas eva anyena jñātrā bhavitavyam vyavasthita viṣayeṇa atha prayogaḥ ca bhavati na ācaitanyam ātmanaḥ svātantrye satya vyavasthānāt yatra caitanyam na asti tatra svātantrye sati api avasthānam na asti cakṣuḥ ādi vat 
NSV_3.1.4	 itas ca śarīra ādi vyatiriktaḥ ātmā śarīra dāhe pātaka abhāvāt śarīra grahṇena śarīra indriya buddhi saṅghātaḥ prāṇi bhūtaḥ gṛhyate prāṇi bhūtam śarīram dahataḥ prāṇi hiṃsā akṛtam pāpam pātakam ucyate tastha abhāvaḥ akartuḥ phalena sambandhaḥ kartuḥ ca anabhisaṃbandhaḥ iti kasmāt abhyupagata artha antarātmanaḥ anyaḥ śarīra indriya buddhi vedanā saṅghātaḥ kartā anyaḥ ca tad phalasya bhoktā iti tat evam akṛta āgama kṛta nāśa doṣa prasaṅgaḥ aniṣṭaḥ ca ayam mārgaḥ tasmāt yaḥ karmaṇām kartā bhoktā ca saḥ ātmā iti 
NSV_3.1.5–3.1.6	 evam ātmani nitye siddhe pūrva pakṣa vādyāha tad abhāvaḥ sa ātmaka pradāhe api tad nitya tvāt yasya api nityenā aatmanā sa ātmakam śarīram dahyate tasya api śarīra dāhe pātakam na bhavet dagdhuḥ kasmāt nitya tvāt ātmanaḥ hiṃsā narha tvāt iti siddhāntavādi āha na kārya āśraya kartṛ vadhāt na brūmaḥ nityasya ātmanaḥ vadhāḥ hiṃsā iti kim tarhi kāryasya sukha duḥkha upabhoga lakṣaṇasya tad āśrayasya śarīrasya kartṛṇām ca indriyāṇām vadhaḥ hiṃsā iti 
NSV_3.1.7–3.1.8	 itas ca deha ādi vyatiriktaḥ ātmā savya dṛṣṭasya itareṇa pratyabhijñānāt savyena cakṣuṣā dṛṣṭam artham itareṇa cakṣuṣā pratyabhijānāti tatas ca eka kartṛka tva siddhiḥ nanu darśana sparśanābhyām iti anena siddha tvāt anārabhyam na indriyavyati reka jñāpana artham atha dvi tvam ākṣipati na ekasminnāsa asthi vyavahite dvi tva abhimānāt na cakṣuḥ dvityam ekam cakṣuḥ madhye nāsā asthi vyavadhānāt dvi tva abhimānam yathā dīrghasya dravyasya madhye kena api vyavahitasya antau= upalabhyamānau dvi tva abhimānam prayojayate iti 
NSV_3.1.9–3.1.10	 atha pariharati eka vināśe dvitīya avināśa at na eka tvam ekasmin vinaṣṭe ca uddhṛte vā cakṣuṣi dvitīyam avatiṣṭhate viṣaya grahaṇa liṅgam tasmāt cakṣuḥ na ekam iti punar ākṣipati avayava nāśepya vaya vī upalabdheḥ ahetuḥ ekasya vṛkṣasya kāsucid śākhāsu bhagna asu upalabhyate vṛkṣaḥ evam ekasya avayasya vināśe sarva avayavi nāśa aniyamena cakṣuḥ upalabdhiḥ na virudhyate iti 
NSV_3.1.11	 dṛṣṭānta virodhāt apratiṣedhaḥ na kāraṇa dravya vibhāge kāryam avatiṣṭhate nitya tva prasaṅgāt yadi na avatiṣṭhate katham kāraṇa dravya vināśe kāryam upalabhyate iti kaḥ evam āha upalabhyate iti api tu bahuṣu avayaviṣu yasya kāraṇāni vibhaktāni tat vinaṣṭam yasyāḥ avibhaktāni tat upalabhyate iti dṛṣṭānta virodhaḥ tad virodhāt cakṣuḥ dvi tva stha na pratiṣedha 
NSV_3.1.12–3.1.13	 anumīyate ca ayam deha ādi vyatiriktaḥ cetanaḥ indriya antara vikārāt kasyacid āmra phalasya rūpe gṛhyamāṇe cakṣuṣā rasanā indriya vikāraḥ bhavati kaḥ punar vikāraḥ rasa anusmṛtau danta antara paristrutābhiḥ adbhiḥ rasanā indriyasya saṃplavaḥ sā ca smṛtiḥ indriya caitanye na prāpnoti na ca pratikṣaṇa vināśiṣu saṃskāreṣu anya anubhūtasya anyena anusmaraṇāt iti smṛtiḥ asati ātmani sarva indriya viṣaya vedini na bhavitum arhati iti ātma siddhiḥ etat ākṣipati na smṛteḥ smartavya viṣaya tvāt iyam smṛtiḥ smartavya artha sannidhānāt upajāyamānāḥ aparidṛṣṭa sāmarthyam na smartāram pratipādayiṣyati na hi sva kāraṇa sannidhānāt prādurbhavan= aṅkuraḥ aparidṛṣṭa sāmarthyam stambha ādikam pratipādayati iti 
NSV_3.1.14	 pariharati tad ātma guṇa sadbhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ tasyāḥ smṛteḥ ātma guṇa tve sadbhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ ātmanaḥ na hi iyam smṛtiḥ anādhārā yuktāḥ guṇa tvāt na ca iyam indriya ādhārāḥ ananubhūta tvāt na viṣaya ādhārāḥ tasyāḥ aasatvāt na api śarīra āśrayā śarīra guṇānām sva ātma parātma pratyakṣa tvāt pariśeṣa adyaḥ ādhāraḥ saḥ ātmā iti aparisaṅkha yānāt ca smṛti viṣayasya aparisaṅkhyānāt ānantyāt tathā ca lāghavāt atiriktaḥ ātma aṅgī kāryaḥ idam upalakṣaṇam smṛteḥ atīta viṣayaka tvāt śarīrasya ca anitya tayā pūrva śarīra anubhūtasya khaṇḍa śarīre smaraṇam na syāt anyathā smṛteḥ puruṣa viśeṣīyatva niyāmakāḥ alābhaḥ ca iti dhyeyam 
NSV_3.1.15–3.1.16	 na ātma pratipatti hetūnām manasi sambhavāt yaḥ ete bhavatā ātma vyatireka pratipādakāḥ hetavaḥ uddiṣṭāḥ sarve te manasi sambhavanti evam ca sati na manaḥ vyatiriktaḥ ātmā sidhyati iti pariharati jñātuḥ jñāna sādhana upapatteḥ saṃjñā bheda mātram yathā jñātāram abhyupagacchatā jñāna sādhanāni cakṣuḥ ādīn īṣyante tathā mantāram pratipadyamānena mati sādhanāni abhyupagantavyāni yat ca tat mati sādhanam tat manaḥ iti saṃjñā bheda mātram 
NSV_3.1.17	 niyamaḥ ca niranumānaḥ matiḥ asādhanā na punar jñaptiḥ iti yaḥ ayam niyamaḥ āśriyate saḥ ayam niranumānaḥ jñapti vat tu mateḥ sa sādhana tve anumāna bhāvāt evam tāvat ātmanaḥ astitva vyatirekau siddhau bahu tvam ca atas eva siddham darśana sparśanābhyām eka artha grahaṇāt itya ādyāḥ sarvāḥ vyavasthāḥ ca śarīra bhede sati bhavanti iti 
NSV_3.1.18^1	 kim punar ātmā deha ādi saṅghātāt anyaḥ nityaḥ anityaḥ vā iti saṃśayaḥ kutas saṃśayaḥ ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt vidyamānam ubhayathā bhavati nityam anityam ca iti ātmā api tāvat pūrva hetubhiḥ vidyamānaḥ bhavati atas saṃśayaḥ atra ātma sadbhāva hetubhiḥ eva asya prāc deha bhedāt avasthānam siddham bhavati ūrdhvam api deha bhedāt avatiṣṭhate kasmāt pūrva abhyasta smṛti anubandhāt jātasya harṣa bhaya śoka sampratipatteḥ jātaḥ khalu ayam kumārakaḥ asmin janmani indriya sāmarthyāt anubhūteṣu harṣa bhaya śoka hetuṣu harṣa bhaya śokān pratipadyamānaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ 
NSV_3.1.18^2	 smita cakita rudita anumeyān te ca smṛti anubandhāt utpadyante smṛti anubandhaḥ ca pūrva abhyāsam antareṇa na bhavati pūrva abhyāsaḥ ca pūrva janmani sati bhavati iti siddhati etat avatiṣṭhate ayam ūrdhvam dehāt iti evam nityasya ātmanaḥ jāta tvam nāma śarīra ādibhiḥ abhisambandhaḥ abhipreta viṣaya prāptyā sukha anubhavaḥ harṣaḥ aniṣṭa viṣaya upanipāte tad jihāsā aśakyatā jñānam bhayam iṣṭa viṣaya yoge sati tad prāptau= aśakya prārthanā śokaḥ tad anubhavaḥ sampratipattiḥ atra ayam prayogaḥ śoka ādi vat ātmavatī bālya avasthā smita rudita ādima tvāt yauvana avasthāvat iti 
NSV_3.1.19	 anityeṣu api vikāra darśanāt anaikāntikaḥ hetuḥ iti ākṣipati padma ādiṣu prabodha sammīlana vikāravat tat vikāraḥ kaḥ punar ayam prabodhaḥ padmasya kim vā sammīlanam iti padma patra avayava vibhāgaḥ avinaśyat kāryaḥ prabodhaḥ padma patra avayavānām ārabdha kāryāṇām yāḥ punar paraspareṇa prāptayaḥ tad sammīlanam iti yathā padma ādiṣu anityeṣu prabodha sammīlana vikārāḥ bhavanti evam anityasya ātmanaḥ harṣa bhaya śoka sampratipattaye vikārāḥ syuḥ iti syāt ātmanaḥ utpatti nirodha kāraṇa anumānam tat na yuktam dravyasya sataḥ sarvadā amūrta tvāt akāraṇaḥ ātmā ākāśa ādi vat iti anumāna siddham 
NSV_3.1.20	 atha padma ādi sūtreṇa padma ādiṣu prabodha sammilana vikārasya akasmika tvam ucyate iti ced na iti āha na uṣṇa śīta varṣā kāla nimitta tvāt pañca ātmaka vikārāṇām uṣṇa ādiṣu satsu bhāvāt asatsu ca abhāvāt tad nimittāḥ padma ādi vikārāḥ na akasmikāḥ evañca sati na kiñcid dṛṣṭāntena pratiṣidhyate iti pañca ātmaka vikārāṇām iti na pañca ātmakāni padma ādīni api tu pañcānām bhūtānām anugrahe sati bhavanti iti pañca ātmakāni iti ucyante vastutas tu na pañca ātmakam kiñcid asti iti upariṣṭa dvakṣyāmaḥ 
NSV_3.1.21	 itas ca nityaḥ ātmā pretyāḥ aahāra abhyāsa kṛtāt stanya abhilāṣāt ja tamātrasya vatsasya pravṛtyā stanya abhilāṣaḥ gamyate tatra pravṛti anumeyaḥ stanya abhilāṣaḥ tena smṛtiḥ tayā saṃskāraḥ tena anubhavaḥ tena pūrva śarīram iti atas eva ayam ātmā pūrva śarīrāt pretya śarīra antaram āpannaḥ kṣudh pīḍitaḥ pūrva abhyastam sva jāti anuguṇam āhāram anusmaran stanyam abhilaṣati tasmāt nityaḥ ātmā iti kimartham idam sūtram ārabhyate yadā ayam arthaḥ pūrva abhyasta sūtre avagataḥ sāmānyatas adhigatasya viśeṣa jñāpana artham iti adoṣaḥ 
NSV_3.1.22–3.1.23	 atha pravṛtti mātrasya anaikāntika tva jñāpana artham sūtram ayasaḥ ayaskānta abhigamana vat tad upasarpaṇam yathā khalvayaḥ abhyāsam antam antareṇa ayaskāntam upasarpati evam āhāra abhyāsam antareṇa api bālaḥ stanyam abhilaṣati iti kim idam ayasaḥ ayaskānta abhisarpaṇam nirnimittam iti na tāvat nirnimittam iti āha na anyatra pravṛti abhāvāt atha khalu na anyatra pravṛttiḥ bhavati na hi jātu ayaḥ loṣṭam upasarpati kim kṛtaḥ ayam niyamaḥ iti vicāre yadi ayam kāraṇa niyamāt tarhi sa ca kriyā niyama liṅgaḥ evañca bālasya api niyata viṣaya abhilāṣaḥ kāraṇa niyamāt bhavitum arhati tat ca kāraṇam abhyasta smaraṇāt āhāra abhilāṣaḥ iti 
NSV_3.1.24–3.1.26	 itas ca nityaḥ ātmā iti āha vīta rāga janma adarśanāt ayam khalu jāyamānaḥ rāga anubaddhaḥ jāyate rāgasya ca pūrva anubhūta viṣaya anucintanam yoniḥ pūrva anubhavaḥ ca śarīram antareṇa na upapadyate iti anādi cetanasya śarīra yogaḥ anādiḥ ca rāga anubandhaḥ iti siddham nitya tvam iti katham punar jñāyate pūrva anubhūta viṣaya anucintana janitaḥ jātasya rāgaḥ na punar sa guṇa dravya utpatti vadat tad utpattiḥ yathā utpatti dharmakasya dravyasya guṇāḥ kāraṇataḥ utpadyante tathā utpatti dharmakasya ātmanaḥ rāgaḥ kutaścid utpadyate iti tat na iti āha na saṅkalpa nimitta tvāt rāga ādīnām atra api pūrvavat saṃkalpa smṛti saṃskāra pūrva anubhava pūrva śarīra vat ātmava tvāni yojyāni evañcāna ādiḥ saṃsāraḥ apavarga antaḥ sidhyati iti tasmāt vyavasthitam etat asti ātmā deha ādi vyatiriktaḥ na ekaḥ nityaḥ ca iti 
NSV_3.1.27	 ātma anantaram avasara prāptam śarīram parīkṣyate kim punar atra parīkṣyam kim ghrāṇa ādi vat eka prakṛti atha nānā prakṛti iti kutas saṃśayaḥ vipratipatteḥ tat evam tatvam pārthivam guṇa antara upalabdheḥ mānuṣam śarīram pārthivam kasmāt guṇa antara upalabdheḥ atra ayam prayogaḥ idam śarīram eka ātmakam gandhava tvāt yaḥ gandhavān saḥ eka ātmakaḥ yathā pārthivaḥ paramāṇuḥ iti evam varuṇa ādi lokeṣu śarīrāṇi kevala jala ādi ārabdhāni draṣṭavyāni na tu etāni śarīrāṇi anyonyam asaṃpṛktaiḥ taiḥ taiḥ ārabdhāni ceṣṭa indriya artha āśraya bhāvena kalpyate iti pañcānām bhūtānām avipratiṣiddhaḥ saṃsargaḥ 
NSV_3.1.31	 pārthiva apya taijasam tad guṇa upalabdheḥ niśvāsa ucchvāsa upalabdheḥ cāturbhautikam gandha kleda pāka byūha avakāśa dānebhyaḥ pāñcabhautikam śruti prāmāṇyāt ca sūryam te cakṣuḥ gacchatāt iti mantre pṛthivīm te śarīram iti śrūyate tat idam prakṛtau vikārasya laya abhidhānam evam sūryam te cakṣuḥ spṛṇomī ati mantra antare pṛthivīm te śarīram smṛṇomi iti śrūyate sā iyam kāraṇāt vikārasya sṛṣṭiḥ abhidhīyate 
NSV_3.1.32	 atha indriyāṇi prameya krameṇa vicāryante kim āvyaktikāni āhosvit bhautikāni iti saṃśaya kāraṇa pratipādana artham sūtram kṛṣṇasāre sati upalambhāt vyatiricya ca upalambhāt saṃśayaḥ kṛṣṇasāram bhautikam tasmin= upahate viṣaya upalabdhiḥ kṛṣṇasāra vyatirekeṇa ca viprakṛṣṭa deśa avasthitasya viṣayasya upalabdhiḥ sā iyam vyatirekeṇa upalabdhiḥ abhautika dharmaḥ tat evam ubhaya dharma upalabdheḥ sandehaḥ iti 
NSV_3.1.33	 abhautikāni iti āha pūrva pakṣa vāde kasmāt mahat aṇu grahaṇāt mahat iti mahattaram mahattamam ca upalabhyate yathā nyagrodha parvata ādi aṇu iti aṇutaram aṇutamam ca gṛhyate yathā nyagrodha dhāna ādi tat ubhayam upalabhyamānam bhautika tvam cakṣuṣaḥ bādhate bhautikam hi yāvat bhavati tāvat eva vyāpnoti abhautikam tu vibhu tvāt sarva vyāpakam iti 
NSV_3.1.34	 na mahat aṇu grahaṇa mātra āt abhautika tvam vibhu tvam ca indriyāṇām śakyam pratipattum idam khalu raśmi artha sannikarṣa viśeṣāt tad grahaṇam tayoḥ mahadaṇvoḥ grahaṇam cakṣū raśmeḥ arthasya ca sannikarṣa viśeṣāt bhavati yathā pradīpa raśmeḥ arthasya ca iti raśmi artha sannikarṣaḥ ca āvaraṇa liṅgaḥ cākṣuṣaḥ hi raśmiḥ kuḍya ādibhiḥ āvṛtam artham na prakāśayati yathā pradīpa raśmiḥ iti tatra sannikarṣa mātrāt sāmānya grahaṇam sannikarṣa viśeṣāt viśeṣa grahaṇam kaḥ punar asya sannikarṣasya viśeṣaḥ bhūyas avayava sannikarṣa anugrahaḥ 
NSV_3.1.35–3.1.36	 āvaraṇa anumeya tve ca sati idam āha tad anupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ rūpa sparśa vat hi tejaḥ mahat tvāt aneka dravyava tvāt ca upalabdhiḥ iti pradīpa raśmi vat pratyakṣataḥ upalabhyeta cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ yadi syāt iti na anumīyamānasya pratyakṣataḥ anupalabdhiḥ abhāva hetuḥ sannikarṣa pratiṣedha arthena āvaraṇena anumīyamānasya raśmeḥ yā pratyakṣataḥ anupalabdhiḥ na asā a= abhāvam pratipādayati yathā candramasaḥ para bhāgasya pṛthivyāḥ ca adhas bhāgasya iti 
NSV_3.1.37–3.1.38	 dravya guṇa dharma bhedāt ca upalabdhi aniyamaḥ bhinnaḥ khalu ayam dravya dharmaḥ guṇa dharmaḥ ca mahat aneka dravya vat ca viṣakta a= ayavam āpyam dravyam pratyakṣataḥ na upalabhyate rūpam ca anudbhūtam spārśanena tu śaityam gṛhyate evam anudbhūta rūpa sparśaḥ na ayana raśmiḥ tasmāt na upalabhyate iti aneka dravya samavāyāt rūpa viśeṣāt ca rūpa upalabdhiḥ tatra rūpam ca dravyam ca tad āśrayaḥ pratyakṣataḥ upalabhyate rūpa viśeṣaḥ tu yad bhāvāt kvacid rūpa upalabdhiḥ yad abhāvāt ca dravyasya kvacid anupalabdhiḥ sa rūpa dharmaḥ ayam udbhava samākhyātaḥ iti anudbhūta rūpaḥ ca ayam nāyanaḥ raśmiḥ tasmāt pratyakṣataḥ na upalabhyate iti dṛṣṭaḥ ca tejasaḥ dharma bhedaḥ udbhūta rūpa sparśam pratyakṣam tejaḥ yathā ādityasya raśmayaḥ udbhūta rūpam anudbhūta sparśam ca pratyakṣam yathā pradīpa raśmayaḥ udbhūta sparśam anudbhūta rūpam apratyakṣam yathā abādi saṃyuktam tejaḥ anudbhūta rūpa sparśaḥ apratyakṣaḥ cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ iti 
NSV_3.1.39	 karma kāritaḥ ca indriyāṇām vyūhaḥ puruṣa artha tantraḥ yathā cetanasya arthaḥ viṣaya upalabdhi bhūtaḥ sukha duḥkha upalabdhi bhūtaḥ ca kalpyate tathā indriyāṇi vyūḍhāni viṣaya prāpti arthaḥ ca raśmeḥ cākṣuṣasya vyūhaḥ kalpyate sarva dravyāṇām ca viśvarūpaḥ vyūhaḥ indriya vartma kāritaḥ puruṣa artha tantra karma tu dharma adharma bhūtam cetanasya upabhoga artham iti avyabhicārāt tu pratīghātaḥ bhautika dharmaḥ yaḥ ca ayam āvaraṇa upalambhāt indriyasya dravya viśeṣe pratighātaḥ sa bhautika dharmaḥ na bhūtāni vyabhicarati nābhautikam kiñcid pratighāta dharmakam prayogaḥ ca bhavati cakṣuḥ bhautikam pratighātaka tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti 
NSV_3.1.40	 upapadyate ca na ayanasya raśmeḥ anupalabdhiḥ kāraṇa bhedāt iti āha madhyandina ulkā prakāśa anupalabdhi vat tad anupalabdhiḥ yathā aneka dravyeṇa samavāyāt rūpa viśeṣāt ca upalabdhiḥ iti sati upalabdhi kāraṇe madhyandina ulkā prakāśaḥ na upalabhyate ādityasya prakāśena abhibhūtaḥ evam cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ na upalabhyate nimitta antarataḥ tat ca nimittam abhibhūta rūpa sparśa tvam iti vyākhyātam 
NSV_3.1.41	 yat tu bruvate loṣṭasya api prakāśaḥ asti sa madhyandina āditya prakāśāt na upalabhyate iti tat uttara dvārakam sūtram na rātrau= api anupalabdheḥ anumānataḥ ca na upalabhyate loṣṭa raśmiḥ iti api śabdāt gamyate tat evam sarva pramāṇa vinivṛtteḥ na vidyate loṣṭa raśmiḥ na evam cakṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ niranumānaḥ kuḍya ādeḥ āvaraṇasya sāmarthyāt iti 
NSV_3.1.42	 bāhya prakāśa anugrahāt viṣaya upalabdheḥ anabhivyaktitaḥ anupalabdhiḥ dṛṣṭānta sthānaḥ eva etat sūtram yat khalu bāhya prakāśa anugraham apekṣate tad anupalabdhiḥ khalu rūpasya anabhivyaktitaḥ iti anudbhūteḥ yathā viṣaktau= ayavasya api adravyasya rūpān udbhūteḥ agrahaṇam tathā cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ bāhya prakāśa anugraham apekṣate tasmāt asya api rūpasya anudbhūteḥ agrahaṇam 
NSV_3.1.43	 kasmāt punar abhibhavaḥ anupalabdhi kāraṇam cākṣuṣasya raśmeḥ na ucyate iti ced abhivyaktau ca abhibhavāt bāhya prakāśa anugraha nirapekṣa tve ca iti ca arthaḥ yat udbhūta rūpam bāhya prakāśa anugraha anapekṣam ca tat abhibhūyate yathā madhyandine na ulkā prakāśaḥ anudbhūta rūpaḥ ca nāyanaḥ raśmiḥ bāhya prakāśa apekṣaḥ ca atas na abhibhūyate kintu anudbhūta rūpaḥ eva iti upapannam asti cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ iti 
NSV_3.1.44–3.1.45	 naktañcara nayana raśmi darśanāt ca cakṣuṣaḥ raśmima tve dṛṣṭāntam āha naktañcara iti vṛṣadaṃśa ādīnām naktañcarāṇām golake raśmiḥ vidyate tat dṛṣṭāntena anyatra api cakṣuṣi tat anumīyate anyathā naktañcarāṇām rātrau pratyakṣam na syāt raśmi artha sannikarṣa viśeṣāt tad grahaṇam iti ayuktam anyathā api tad grahaṇāt aprāpyagrahaṇam kāca abhra paṭala sphaṭika antarita upalabdheḥ tṛṇa ādi sarpat dravyam kāca dau pratihatam avyavahitena cakṣuṣā sat nikṛṣyate tathā api kāca ādi vyavahitam artham prakāśayati cakṣuḥ tasmāt na prāpya kārī iti atas eva ca abhautikam prāpya kāri tvam na bhautika dharmaḥ iti 
NSV_3.1.46–3.1.47	 kuḍya antarita anupalabdheḥ apratiṣedhaḥ aprāpya kāri tve sati indriyāṇām kuḍya ādibhiḥ antaritasya anupalabdhiḥ na syāt nanu prāpya kāri tve api ca kāca ādi antarita upalabdhiḥ na syāt apratighātāt sannikarṣa upapattiḥ na kāca ādi na ayana raśmi viṣṭabhnāti kāca ādinā su accha dravyeṇa apratighātāt apratibandhāt upapadyate sannikarṣaḥ 
NSV_3.1.48–3.1.49	 yat ca manyeta na bhautikasya asti apratighātaḥ sarvam hi bhautikam pratighāta dharmakam iti tat na iti āha āditya raśmeḥ sphaṭika antarite api dāhye avighātāt āditya raśmeḥ avighātāt sphaṭika antarite api avighātāt dāhye avighātāt avighāta pada abhisambandhāt vākya bhedaḥ prativākyam ca artha bhedaḥ āditya raśmiḥ kumbha stham udakam tapati prāptau hi dravya antara guṇasya uṣṇa sparśasya grahaṇam tena ca śīta sparśa abhibhavaḥ iti sphaṭika antarite ca prakāśanīye dīpa raśmī nām aprativātaḥ prāpta prakāśanam iti bharjana kapāla ādi stham ca dravyam āgneyena tejasā dahyate tasya apratidhātāt prāptiḥ iti kaḥ ayam apratighātā nāma avyūhyamāna avayavena vyavadhāyakena dravyeṇa sarvatas dravyasya avaṣṭambhaḥ iti atra pūrva ṣakṣa vādi āha na itara itara dharma prasaṅgāt itara dharmaḥ itaratra prasajyate itara dharmaḥ ca itaratra yadi avighātaḥ cakṣūraśmeḥ sphaṭika ādibhiḥ kuḍya ādibhiḥ api prāpnoti kuḍya ādibhiḥ vā pratighātaḥ sphaṭika ādibhiḥ api pratighātaḥ prāpnoti iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NSV_3.1.50	 na eṣa doṣaḥ iti āha ādarśa udakayoḥ prasāda svābhāvyāt rūpa upalabdhi vat tad upalabdhiḥ ādarśa udakayoḥ prasādaḥ rūpa viśeṣaḥ sa ca svaḥ bhavati niyamāt kaḥ punar ayam rūpasya viśeṣaḥ dravya antara sampṛkte dravye samavāyaḥ tad svābhāvyāt prasāda svabhāvaka tvāt ādarśa ādiṣu nayana raśmiḥ pratihanyate sa ca pratihataḥ pratinivṛtya sva mukhena eva sambadhyate sambandhāt sva mukha upalambhanam pratibimba grahaṇa ākhyam atra ādarśa grahaṇam ca krameṇa bhavat api āśu bhāvāt na vibhāvyate mukhasya ādarśa stha tayā grahaṇam śrānti nibandhana tad mukha upalambhanam ādarśa rūpa anugrahaṇāt tad nimittam bhavati ādarśa rūpa upaghāte tad abhāvāt kuḍya ādiṣu pratibiṃba grahaṇam na bhavati dravya svabhāva niyamāt evam kāca ādibhiḥ apratighātaḥ ca cakṣūraśmeḥ kuḍya ādibhiḥ ca pratighātaḥ iti 
NSV_3.1.51	 dṛṣṭa anumitānām hi niyoga pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ pramāṇasya tattva viṣaya tvāt dṛṣṭa anumitāḥ khalu ime dravya dharmāḥ tathābhūtāḥ bhavanti tathābhūtāḥ eva pramāṇena pratipadyante imau ca bhavatā niyoga pratiṣedhau deśitau kva viṣaye syātām na ca etat yuktam na hi yathā dhūmena agni pratipattiḥ tathā udaka pratipattiḥ api bhavatu iti na ca udaka pratipattiḥ dhūmena na bhavati iti agni pratipattiḥ api ayuktā arthān niyuñjānaḥ bhavān upekṣaṇīyaḥ pratighāta apratighātayoḥ khalu upalabdhi anupalabdhī vyavasthāpike vyavahita upalabdhyā a numīyate sphaṭika ādibhiḥ apratīghātaḥ vyavahita anupalabdhyā ca kuḍya ādibhiḥ pratīghātaḥ iti yadi prāpya kāri cakṣuḥ bhavati atha kasmāt añjana śalākā ādi na upa labhyate na indriyeṇa asambandhāt indriyeṇa saṃbaddhāḥ arthāḥ upalabhyante na ca añjana śalāka ādi indriyeṇa saṃbaddham adhiṣṭhānasya anindriya tvāt raśmiḥ indriyam na adhiṣṭhānam na raśminā añjana śalākā saṃbaddhā iti 
NSV_3.1.52	 evam tāvat bhautikāni indriyāṇi iti vyavasthitam kim punar ekam indriyam āhosvit na ekam iti saṃśayaḥ kutas sthāna anya tve nānā tvāt avayavi nānā sthāna tvāt ca saṃśayaḥ sthāna anya tve sthāna bhede sthāna bhede ghaṭa paṭa ādīnām nānātvam dṛśyate nānā avayava sthita sva avayavinaḥ eka tvam api dṛśyate atas saṃśayaḥ indriyāṇām nānātvam eka tvam vā iti 
NSV_3.1.53^1	 ekam indriyam kim punar tat tvac avyatirekāt kaḥ punar ayam avyatirekaḥ sarva adhiṣṭhāna saṃbandhaḥ na hi kiñcid indriyam na tvacā prāptam satibhāvaḥ vā na hi asatyām tvaci kiñcid artha grahaṇam bhavati tasmāt tvac ekam indriyam iti tvac abhāve viṣaya grahaṇa asaṃbhavena tdak ekam eva indriyam astu na loka virodhāt vidyamāne tvac indriye sparśa upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ indriya artha antarāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ na gṛhyante andha ādibhiḥ upalabhyeran na eva upalabhyante tasmāt na ekam eva indriyam tvac avayava viśeṣeṇa dhūma upalabdhi vat tat upalabdhiḥ 
NSV_3.1.53^2	 tvacaḥ avayava viśeṣaḥ kaścid cakṣuṣi sannikṛṣṭaḥ dhūva sparśam gṛhṇāti na anyaḥ evam tvacaḥ avayava viśeṣāḥ rūpa ādi grāhakāḥ teṣām upaghātāt andhādibhiḥ na gṛhyante rūpa ādayaḥ vyāghātāt ahetuḥ prāk ekam indriyam abhyupagamya idānīm tvac avayava viśeṣā rūpa ādi grāhakā iti bruvāṇaḥ pratiṣedhyam indriya bahu tvam abhyanujānāti iti vyāvātaḥ na hi avayavi anatiriktā tvac avayavāḥ rūpa ādi grāhakāḥ bhavitum arhanti iti sandigdhaḥ ca avyatirekaḥ pṛthivī ādibhiḥ api bhūtaiḥ indriya adhiṣṭhānāni vyāptāni na ca teṣu asatsu viṣaya grahaṇam sambhavati tasmāt na ttvac anyat vā sarva viṣayam ekam indriyam iti 
NSV_3.1.54–3.1.55	 pariharati na yugapad artha anupalabdheḥ yasya ekam indriyam tasya yugapad arthānām upalabdhiḥ prasajyate ātmā manasā sambadhyate manaḥ indriyeṇa indriyam sarva arthaiḥ iti yugapad eva sarvāḥ buddhayaḥ prādurbhaveyuḥ na ca etat asti tasmāt na ekam indriyam sarva viṣayakam iti vipratiṣedhāt ca na tyagekāḥ na tvac ekam indriyam vyāghatāt ca rūpa dīnya prāptāni gṛhyante iti ced sparśa ādiṣu api evam prasaṅgaḥ sparśa ādīnām ca prāptānām grahaṇe rūpa ādīnām api prāptānām grahaṇam iti 
NSV_3.1.56–3.1.57	 atha nānātva sthāpanā hetuḥ upādīyate indriya artha pañcatvāt arthaḥ prayojanam tad pañcavidham indriyāṇām sparśana indriyeṇa sparśa grahaṇena tena eva rūpam na gṛhyate iti rūpa grahaṇa prayojanam cakṣuḥ anumīyate evam anyeṣu api draṣṭavyam evam indriya prayojanasya pañcavidha tvāt pañca indriyāṇi iti na tad artha bahu tvāt nakhalu indriya artha pañcatvāt indriya pañcatvam siddhyati tad viṣayāṇām pratyekam bahu tvāt iti evañca sati bahūni indriyāṇi prasajyante iti 
NSV_3.1.58–3.1.59	 gandha tva ādi avyatirekāt gandha ādīnām apratiṣedhaḥ gandha tva ādibhiḥ sva sāmānyaiḥ kṛta vyasthānām gandha ādīnām yāni grahaṇāni tāni asamāna sādhana sādhya tvāt na grāhaka antarāṇi prayojayanti iti na yuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ iti sāmānyena saṅgrāhaka tve viṣaya tva avyatirekāt punar indriya eka tva śaṅkā āyadi sāmānyam saṅgrāhakam vimiśrāṇām gandha ādīnām prāptam indriyāṇām viṣaya tva avyatirekāt eka tvam viṣaya tvena hi sāmānyena gandha ādayaḥ saṅgṛhītāḥ 
NSV_3.1.60^1	 indriyāṇām na ekatvam yuktam iti pariharati na buddhi lakṣaṇa adhiṣṭhāna gati ākṛti jāti pañcatvebhyaḥ na khalu viṣaya tvena sāmānyena kṛta vyavasthāḥ viṣayāḥ grāhaka antara nirapekṣāḥ eka sādhana sādhyāḥ gṛhyante anubhūyante tu pañca gandha ādayaḥ gandha tva ādibhiḥ kṛta vyavasthāḥ indriya antara grāhyāḥ ayam eva arthaḥ anūdyate buddhi lakṣaṇa pañcatvāt iti buddhayaḥ eva lakṣaṇāni viṣaya grahaṇa liṅga tvāt indriyāṇām tasmāt buddhi pañcaka tvāt pañca indriyāṇi gati bhedāt api indriya bhedaḥ kṛṣṇasāra upanibaddham cakṣuḥ bahis nissṛtya rūpa adhikaraṇāni dravyāṇi prāpnoti spārśana ādīni tu indriyāṇi na gacchanti 
NSV_3.1.60^2	 viṣayāḥ eva āśraya upasarpaṇāt pratyāsīdanti santāna vṛtyā śabdasya śrotra pratyāsattiḥ iti ākṛtiḥ khalu parimāṇam iyattā sā pañcadhā sva sthāna mātrāṇi ghrāṇa rāsanaspārśanāni viṣaya grahaṇa anumeyāni cakṣuḥ kṛṣṇasāra āśritam bahis nisṛtam viṣaya vyāpi śrotram tu na anyat ākāśāt tat ca vibhu tad adhiṣṭhāna niyamena pravartate jātiḥ iti yonim pracakṣmahe pañca khalu imāḥ indriya yonayaḥ pṛthivī ādīni bhūtāni indriyāṇām yonayaḥ iti yoniḥ iti tādātmyam ucyate na punar tad kārya tvam ākāśe sambhavati nitya tvāt tasmāt ākṛti pañcatvāt api pañca indriyāṇi iti siddham 
NSV_3.1.61	 katham punar jñāyate bhūta prakṛtīni indriyāṇi iti na avyakta prakṛtīni iti atra uktam eva uttaram smārayati bhūta guṇa viśeṣa upalabdheḥ tādātmyam dṛṣṭaḥ hi bhūtānām vāyu ādīnām guṇa viśeṣa abhivyakti niyamaḥ vāyuḥ sparśa vyañjakaḥ āpaḥ rasa vyañjakāḥ tejaḥ rūpa vyañjakam pārthivam kiñcid dravyam nimba ādi kasyacid ravyasya candanasya vā gandha vyañjakam asti ca ayam indriyāṇām bhūta guṇa viśeṣa upalabdhi niyamaḥ tena bhūta guṇa viśeṣa upalabdheḥ manyāmahe bhūta prakṛtīni indriyāṇi na avyakta prakṛtīni iti atra prayogaḥ pārthivam ghrāṇam gandha vyakti hetu tvāt bāhya pārthiva dravya vat iti evam śeṣeṣu api 
NSV_3.1.62–3.1.64	 gandha ādayaḥ pṛthivī ādi guṇāḥ iti uddiṣṭam uddeśaḥ ca niyoga vikalpa samuccayaiḥ samānaḥ atra niyogaḥ ekaika guṇa tvam vikalpaḥ kasyacid ekaḥ kasyacid dvau iti evamādiḥ samuccayaḥ sarvaḥ sarvatra iti atas viśeṣaṇa artham ucyate gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabdānām sparśa paryantāḥ pṛthivyāḥ ap tejaḥ vāyūnām pūrvam pūrvam apohya ākāśasya uttaraḥ spaṣṭaḥ arthaḥ  uddeśa sūtre hi śabdaḥ paraḥ uddiṣṭaḥ iti paratvam eva uttara śabdena ucyate atra codayati na sarva guṇāḥ anupalabdheḥ na ayam guṇa viniyogaḥ sādhuḥ kutas pārthivena ghrāṇena pārthivānām gandha ādīnām caturṇām upalabdhi prasaṅgāt evam āpyena rasanena trayāṇām taijasena cakṣuṣā dvayoḥ iti 
NSV_3.1.65	 katham tarhi ime guṇāḥ viniyoktavyāḥ ekaika śyena uttara uttara guṇa sadbhāvāt uttara uttarāṇām tad anupalabdhiḥ gandha ādīnām ekaikaḥ yathākramam pṛthivī ādīnām ekaikasya guṇaḥ atas tad anupalabdhiḥ ekaikasya iti sautraḥ nirdeśaḥ katham tarhi aneka guṇāni bhūtāni gṛhyante iti atā āha saṃsargāt ca neka guṇa grahaṇam avādi saṃsargāt pṛthivyām rasa ādayaḥ gṛhyante evam śeṣeṣu api 
NSV_3.1.66–3.1.67	 niyamaḥ tarhi na upapadyate pṛthivyām catvāraḥ na itareṣu saṃsargasya aniyamāt iti prāpnoti katham yasmāt viṣṭam hi aparam pareṇa aparam pareṇa viṣṭama bādinā na apareṇa param atas saṃsarga viśeṣaṇāt niyamaḥ iti pariharati na pārthiva āpyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt na iti tri sūtrīm pratyācaṣṭe kasmāt pārthivasya ca pratyakṣa tvāt mahatvā aneka dravya tvāt rūpāt ca upalabdhiḥ iti taijasam eva dravyam pratyakṣam syāt na pārthivam āpyam vā rūpa ādi bhāvāt 
NSV_3.1.68	 tat evam nyāya viruddham pravādam pratiṣidhya na sarva guṇāḥ anupalabdhe iti yat ca uditam tat samādhatte pūrva pūrva guṇa utkarṣāt tat tat pradhānam tasmāt na sarva guṇa upalabdhiḥ ghrāṇa ādīnām indriyāṇām pūrvaṃpūrvam indriyam parasmāt pradhānam kā pradhāna tā catur guṇa tva ādiḥ kaḥ guṇa utkarṣaḥ sva guṇa abhivyakti sāmarthyam yena guṇena dravyam utkṛṣyate sa tad ja tīya abhivyañjaka tvāt utkṛṣṭaḥ bhavati yathā bāhyānām dravyāṇam pārthiva āpya taijasānām caturguṇa triguṇa dviguṇānām na sarva guṇa grāhaka tvam gandha rasa rūpa utkarṣānttu yathākramam gandha rasa rūpa grāhaka tvam ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuṣām tasmāt na ghrāṇa ādibhiḥ sarveṣām guṇa upalabdhiḥ iti 
NSV_3.1.69	 kim kṛtam punar vyavasthānam kiñcid pārthivam indriyam na sarvāṇi iti tad vyavasthānam tu bhūyastvāt artha nirvṛtti samarthasya pravibhaktasya dravyasya saṃsargaḥ puruṣa saṃskāra kāritaḥ bhūyatsvam prakṛṣṭaḥ hi loke bhūyān iti ucyate yathā pṛthak artha kriyā samarthāni puruṣa saṃskāra viṣa oṣadhi maṇi prabhṛtīni dravyāṇi nivartyante na sarvam sarva artham evam pṛthak viṣaya grahaṇa samarthāni ghrāṇa ādīni nivartyante iti 
NSV_3.1.70–3.1.71	 sva guṇān na upalabhante indriyāṇi kasmāt iti ced sa guṇānām indriya bhāvāt svena gandha ādinā samāna artha kāriṇā saha ghrāṇa ādīnām indriya tvāt ghrāṇa ādīni bāhyam gṛhṇanti sva gandha ādi grahaṇam ca saha kāri vaikalyāt na bhavati iti tena eva tasya agrahaṇāt ca na guṇa upalabdhiḥ indriyāṇām yaḥ hi bruvate yathā bāhyam dravyam cakṣuṣā gṛhyate tathā tena eva cakṣuṣā gṛhyatām tat eva cakṣuḥ iti tādṛś idam tulyaḥ hi ubhayatra pratipatti hetu abhāvaḥ iti 
NSV_3.1.72–3.1.73	 atra codayati na śabda guṇa upalabdheḥ sva guṇān na upalabhante indriyāṇi iti etat na bhavati upalabhyate hi sva guṇaḥ śabdaḥ śrotreṇa iti pariharati tad upalabdhiḥ itaretara dravya guṇa vaidharmyāt astha arthaḥ satyam upalabhyate śrotreṇa ākāśa guṇaḥ śabdaḥ na punar śrotram sa śabdam indriyam yathā itarāṇi sa guṇāni indriyāṇi na evam ākāśakam kasmāt śabdasya itara guṇa vaidharmyāt ākāśasya itara dravya vaidharmyāt na hi śabdaḥ eva śabdasya vyañjakaḥ na ākāśam sa guṇam indriyam iti 
NSV_3.2.1–3.2.2	 parīkṣitāni indriyāṇi tad arthāḥ ca buddheḥ idānīm parīkṣā sā kim nityā anityā vā iti kutas saṃśayaḥ karma ākāśa sādharmyāt saṃśayaḥ karma kriyā ākāśaḥ prasiddhaḥ asparśa tvam tayoḥ samāna dharmaḥ upalabhyate buddhau tatas saṃśayaḥ iti atra sāṅkhyā pravadanti nityā buddhiḥ iti sādhanam ca pracakṣate viṣaya pratyabhijñānāt yam aham pūrvam ajñāsiṣam tam aham idānīm jānāmi iti jñāna yoḥ samāne arthe pratisandhānam pratyabhijñānam avasthitāyāḥ buddheḥ upapannam liṅgam eka tve buddhi nānātve tu pratyabhijñā anupapattiḥ yathā puruṣa antara buddhiṣu 
NSV_3.2.3–3.2.5	 dūṣaṇam āha sādhya sama tvāda hetuḥ yathā khalu nitya tvam buddheḥ sādhyam evam pratyabhijñānam api kim kāraṇam puruṣa dharmaḥ khalu ayam jñānam darśanam upalabdhiḥ bodhaḥ cetanaḥ hi pūrva jñātam artham pratyabhijānāti na antaḥkaraṇam tatas cetanasya etat hetoḥ nitya tvam yuktam iti yat ca idam ucyate buddheḥ avasthitāyāḥ yathā viṣayam vṛttayaḥ prādurbhavanti jñāna śabda vācyāḥ vṛttiḥ ca vṛttimataḥ na anyā iti tat ca na na yugapada grahaṇāt vṛtti vṛttim atoḥ ananya tve tat abhinnānām vṛttīnām api avasthānam iti yāni imāni viṣaya grahaṇāni tāni avatiṣṭhante iti yugapad viṣayāṇām grahaṇam prasajyate na ca tat asti iti apratyabhijñāne ca vināśa prasaṅgaḥ vṛttīnām apagame vṛttimataḥ api apagamaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NSV_3.2.6–3.2.7	 avibhu ca ekam manaḥ paryāyeṇa indriyaiḥ sambadhyate iti krama vṛtti tvāt ayugapad grahaṇam indriya arthānām vṛtti vṛttim atoḥ nānātvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ eka tve tu prādurbhāva tirobhāvayoḥ abhāvaḥ iti apratyabhijñānam ca viṣaya anta khya āsaṅgāt viṣaya antara vyāsakte manasi kasyacid arthasya anupalabdhiḥ vṛtti vṛtti matoḥ bhede sati upapadyate iti sūtra arthaḥ eka tve tu anarthakaḥ vyāsaṅgaḥ iti 
NSV_3.2.8	 vibhu tve ca antaḥkaraṇasya paryāyeṇa indriyaiḥ saṃyogaḥ na gati abhāvāt prāptāni indriyāṇi antaḥkaraṇena iti prāpti arthasya gamanasya abhāvaḥ tatra ca yugapad grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ na ca yugapad pratyaya utpattau pramāṇam asti yena pramāṇena pratiṣiddham api pratyaya yauga payam pratipadyeta yadā kiñcid pratiṣiddham api pratipadyate yathā cakṣuṣaḥ gatiḥ sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭayoḥ tulya kāla grahaṇāt yasmāt sannikaṣṭam pāṇim viprakṛṣṭam candramasam ekasmin kāle cakṣuḥ pratipadyate tasmāt na gatimat cakṣuḥ iti pratiṣiddhā satī gatiḥ vyavadhāna pratighātena anumīyate na ca yugapad pratyaya utpattau pramāṇam asti etena viṣaya antara vyāsaṅgaḥ pratyuktaḥ kaḥ punar ayam vyāsaṅgaḥ abhīviṣaṣṭayaḥ aneka vijñāna utpādaḥ sa ca puruṣasya na antaḥkaraṇasya iti 
NSV_3.2.9–3.2.10	 ekam antaḥkaraṇam nānā vṛttayaḥ iti satyabhede vṛteḥ idam ucyate sphaṭika anyatva abhimāna vat tad anyatva abhimānaḥ japā kusuma sannidhāne tad gata dharmā sphaṭike pratibhāsante tadā sphaṭikaḥ eva tad anyatva āropaḥ sambhavati yathā tathā eva ekasyāḥ eva buddheḥ viṣaya indriya sannikarṣa vaśāt nānāvidha viṣaya sambandhāt nānātu a āropaḥ iti siddhāntayati na hetu abhāvāt iti ekasyām eva buddhau nānā tva āropaḥ iti na yuktam uktam buddheḥ eka tva sādhaka abhāvāt nānātvasya pratyakṣa siddha tvena anyathā kalpaka abhāvāt 
NSV_3.2.11	 sphaṭike nānātvam bhramaḥ iti uktam tat asahamānaḥ jñāna jñeyayoḥ kṣaṇika tva vādī pratyavatiṣṭhate sphaṭike api apara apara utpatteḥ kṣaṇika tvāt vyaktīnām ahetuḥ buddhi graha artham api iti uktam vyaktīnām kṣaṇika tvena pratikṣaṇam api apara apara utpatteḥ pūrva sphaṭika nāśena sphaṭika antaram eva utpadyate iti yāvat kṣaṇika tā ca bhāvānām sva utpatti dvitī ya kṣaṇa vṛtti dhvaṃsa pratiyogi tvam na ca satām kṣaṇika tvam aprāmāṇikam upacayā apacaya ādinā pratikṣaṇam śarīre tad anubhavāt 
NSV_3.2.12–3.2.13	 bauddha uktam dūṣayati niyama hetu abhāvāt yathādarśanam abhyanujñā saḥ eva ayam sphaṭikaḥ saḥ ayam devadattaḥ ityādi pratyabhijñā anurodhena vināśa hetu abhāvāt padārthānām sthairyam abhyupeyam satām akṣaṇika tve sthāyi tve ca upapati antaram na utpatti vināśa kāraṇa upapatteḥ na sphaṭika ādeḥ śakyam abhyupetum kṣaṇika tvam padārthānām utpatti vināśau utpatti vināśa kāraṇakau= iti sarva sammataḥ arthaḥ prakṛte ca sphaṭika ādīnām pratikṣaṇam utpatti vināśa abhāvāt eva akṣaṇika tvam siddhayati 
NSV_3.2.14	 punar ākṣipati kṣīra vināśa kāraṇā anupalabdhi vat dadhi utpatti vat ca tad utpattiḥ kṣīra vināśa kāraṇam na upalabhyate kṣīram ca vinaśyati evam dadhi utpatti kāraṇam na upalabhyate tathā api utpadyate dadhi tadvat pūrva sphaṭika nāśa kāraṇa uttara sphaṭika utpatti kāraṇā anupalabdhau= api pūrva vināśaḥ aparasya ca utpattiḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ 
NSV_3.2.15–3.2.16	 siddhāntam āha liṅgataḥ grahaṇa anna anupalabdhiḥ kṣīra vikāre dadhi bhāve ca vidyate hetuḥ pratyakṣa siddhaḥ tasmāt eva tatra kāraṇāḥ anupalabdhiḥ anupapannāḥ sphaṭikasya pratikṣaṇa utpatti vināśe tu na asti hetuḥ tasmāt ayam vādaḥ anupapannaḥ eva sāṅkhyam dūṣayitum āha na payasaḥ pariṇāma guṇa antara prādurbhāvāt na hi kṣīra nāśaḥ dadhi utpattiḥ iti anarthāntaram kintu kṣīrasya pariṇāmena pūrva guṇa nāśena guṇa antara rasa antara prādurbhāvaḥ eva dadhi evam ca etat dṛṣṭānta anuguṇyena sphaṭika ādeḥ utpatti vināśa kalpanam a yuktam 
NSV_3.2.17	 matam idam dūṣayati vyūha antarāt dravya antara utpattiḥ pūrva dravya nivṛtteḥ anumānam vyūha antarāt racanā antarāt dravya antara utpattau tasmin= eva kāle dravya antara sthiteḥ viruddha tvena pūrva nāśam vinā dravya antara utpattiḥ iti na sādhīyān pakṣaḥ tatas ca vidyamānā dravya antara utpattiḥ eva pūrva dravya nāśa jñāpikā 
NSV_3.2.18	 punar api saugata matam pratyākhyāti kvacid vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ kvacid ca upalabdheḥ anekāntar kvacid grīṣma ādau kṣīra vināśena dadhi utpāde vināśa kāraṇāḥ anirṇayāt kvacid ca amla dravya saṃyogena kṣīra ādi vināśena dadhi utpāde anekāntar sa kāraṇaka tvasya vyabhicāra saṃśayaḥ na ca sa kāraṇaka tva niścaya virodhī vyabhicāra nirṇayasya virodhi tvāt iti bhāvaḥ iti eke yat vā saugata ukta diśā kṣīra dadhi dṛṣṭāntena akāraṇakau= evātra utpāda vināśau= iti na yukam ghaṭa ādau sa kāraṇa ka tva upalabdheḥ vyabhicārāt iti 
NSV_3.2.19–3.2.20	 prāc buddheḥ ātma guṇa tvam pratyapādi idānīm śiṣya buddhi vaiśadyāya asya eva parīkṣā vartiṣyate iti na indriya arthayoḥ tad vināśe api jñāna avasthānāt na buddhiḥ indriyāṇām arthasya vā guṇaḥ tat tad indriya ādi nāśe api tat tad indriya āhita saṃskāreṇa jñāna sadbhāvena smaraṇa upapatteḥ anubhavituḥ abhāve tu na smaraṇa ādi upapadyate ati prasaṅgāt na api manaḥ guṇaḥ yugapad jñāna anupalabdha īśva manasaḥ na iti pūrva sūtrāt anuvartate tathā ca na manasaḥ api guṇaḥ iti sampannam tatra hetuḥ yugapad jñāna anupalabdheḥ iti kāya vyūha sthale yugapad eva nānā śarīra avacchedena jñāna anutpāda prasaṅgāt manasaḥ aṇu tvena nānā śarīra sambandhasya ekadā aasambhavāt 
NSV_3.2.21–3.2.22	 śaṅkate tad ātma guṇa tve api tulyam buddheḥ ātma guṇa tve jñāna yaugapadyam tulyam eva sarva indriya samprayogasya ātmanaḥ vidyamāna tvāt samādhatte sannikarṣa abhāvāt tad anutpattiḥ indriya artha sannikarṣasya jñāna kāraṇa tva vat ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya api tad kāraṇa tvam abyāhatam tasya ca ayaugapadyam aṇu tvāt manasaḥ ayaugapadyāt anutpattiḥ yugapad jñānānām ātma guṇa tve api iti 
NSV_3.2.23–3.2.24	 ākṣipati na utpatti kāraṇāḥ anupadeśāt buddhiḥ na ātma guṇaḥ utpatti kāraṇāḥ anupadeśāt budhi utpattau kāraṇasya anukta tvāt iti arthaḥ ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya kāraṇa tve jñānasya sārvadika tva prasaṅgaḥ buddheḥ ātma guṇa tve doṣam āha vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ ca avasthāne tad nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ yadi ātma guṇaḥ buddhiḥ bhaviṣyati tadā vināśa kāraṇa abhāvāt asyāḥ nitya tvam syāt vināśaḥ ca buddheḥ tadā bhavet yadā aśrayasya aatmanaḥ vināśaḥ syāt na ca etat vidyate na api virodhi guṇa antara utpādena tasyāḥ abhāvāt tasmāt buddhiḥ nityā syāt 
NSV_3.2.25	 uttamāha anitya tva grahaṇāt buddheḥ budhi antarāt vināśaḥ śabda vat buddheḥ utpāda vināśayoḥ ānubhavika tvāt sva uttara utpanna budhyā pūrva buddheḥ vināśa aṅgīkārāt nanu evam carama buddheḥ vināśaḥ katham svasmāt eva iti brūmaḥ yathā sva uttara utpanna śabdasya pūrva pūrva nāśaka tvam carama śabdasya svasmāt eva vināśaḥ evam eva prakṛte api iti dhyeyam yat vā adṛṣṭa nāśāt kālāt vā śabda nāśaḥ sambhavati yathā tathā eva nimitta nāśāt buddheḥ api vināśa sambhavāt 
NSV_3.2.26	 buddheḥ ātma guṇa tve saṃskāra manaḥ yogayoḥ vidyamāna tvena smṛtīnām pūrva anubhūta yāvat vastu viṣayaka tvam syāt iti atra kasyacid samādhānam dūṣayitum anuvadati jñāna samaveta ātma pradeśa sannikarṣāt manasaḥ smṛti utpatteḥ na yugapad utpattiḥ jñāyate anena iti vyutpatyāḥ jñāna padam saṃskāra param tad samavetaḥ tad sambaddhaḥ iti yāvat tad ātmakaḥ yaḥ ātma pradeśaḥ ātma sambandhī tad avacchedena sannikarṣāt iti arthaḥ tathā ca yat viṣaya avacchedena ātma manaḥ yogaḥ vartate tad viṣayasya eva smaraṇam na sarvasya iti bhāvaḥ 
NSV_3.2.27–3.2.29	 dūṣayati na antar śarīra vṛtti tvāt manasaḥ manasaḥ antar śarīra vṛtti tvena śarīra atirikta avacchedena ātma manaḥ yogasya jñānāḥ ajanaka tvena ca prāc ukta doṣa tādavasthyam śaṅkate sādhya tvāt ahetuḥ śarīra avacchinna ātma manaḥ yogaḥ na hetuḥ sādhya tvāt asiddha tvāt māna abhāvāt ca iti yāvat śaṅkām nirasyati smarataḥ śarīra dhāraṇa upapatteḥ apratiṣedhaḥ uktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ na yuktaḥ susmūrṣoḥ śarīra dhāraṇa sadbhāvāt manasaḥ bahirbhāve dhārakasya prayatnasya abhāvāt guru tvāt ca śarīrasya patanam syāt 
NSV_3.2.30–3.2.31	 punar api śaṅkate na tad āśu gati tvāt manasaḥ śarīra dhāraṇam manasaḥ upapadyate śīdhra gatima tvāt tasya śarīrāt bahis nirsṛtam manaḥ punar śīghram eva pratyāvartate atas smaraṇam dhāraṇam ca iti ubhayam api sidhyati dūṣayati na smaraṇa kālāḥ aniyamāt na śarīra dhāraṇam yujyate manasaḥ smaraṇa kālāḥ aniyamāt yadā kadācid smaraṇa dhārā asagbhavena tadā śarīre manasaḥ aparāvṛtta tvena śarīra dhāraṇam na syāt 
NSV_3.2.32–3.2.33	 atra kasyacid dūṣaṇam āha ātma preraṇa yadṛcchā jña tābhiḥ ca na saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ manasaḥ hi bahis pradeśe viṣayeṇa saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ tredhā syāt ātma preraṇena yadṛcchayā jñatayā vā na ādyaḥ tasya smaraṇīya jñāna pūrvaka tayā prāk eva smaraṇa āpatteḥ na dvitīyaḥ ākasmika tve manaḥ gamanasya jagataḥ api tathātvam syāt na tṛtīyaḥ jñātṛ tvam na manasaḥ dharmaḥ iti prāk eva upāditam dūṣaṇam pariharati vyāsakta manasaḥ pāda vyathanena saṃyoga viśeṣeṇa samānam nṛtya ādikam paśyataḥ kaṇṭaka ādinā pāda vyathanena manaḥ saṃyogaḥ yathā jāyate tathā eva atra api iti bhāvaḥ anyathā manaḥ saṃyoge api ukta doṣāḥ syuḥ adṛṣṭa viśeṣa kalpanena doṣa uddhāre atra api samam 
NSV_3.2.34	 smaraṇā ayaugapadyam upapādayati praṇidhāna liṅga ādi jñānānām ayugapad bhāvāt yugapad a smaraṇam praṇidhānam citta aikāgryam suṣmūrṣā iti yāvat jñāna pada uttaram ādi padam yojyam tena liṅga jñāna ādīnām iti arthaḥ sampannaḥ liṅga jñānam udbodhakam ādi padam icchā saṃskāra ādi grāhakam ayugapad bhāvāt krameṇa utpādanāt tathā ca yadi yugapad udbodhakāni bhavanti tadā tāvat viṣayakam api smaraṇam iṣyate eva yathā pada jñāna ādau 
NSV_3.2.35	 jñānam puruṣa dharmaḥ icchā dayaḥ tu antaḥkaraṇa dharmāḥ yathā ca sāṅkhyānām gītiḥ puruṣa caitanyam ekam eva kūṭastha nityam sat tad tad artha ākāra pariṇata buddhi tatva pratibiṃba vibhrama vaśāt bhinnam iva upajana apāya dharmakam vijñānam iti vṛttiḥ iti ca ākhyāyate icchā dveṣa ādayaḥ tu vastutas upajana apāya dharmāṇaḥ antaḥkaraṇasya iti darśanam tat etam matam nirākartum āha jñasya icchā dveṣa nimitta tvāt ārambha nivṛtyoḥ jñasya jñātuḥ ātmanaḥ ārambha nivṛtyoḥ pravṛtti nivṛtyoḥ icchā dveṣa nimitta tvam vidyate iti bhāvaḥ prāpti icchā prayuktasya ātmanaḥ sukha sādhana avāptaye yaḥ samīhā viśeṣaḥ prārabhyate sa ārambhaḥ jihāsā prayuktasya duḥkha sādhana parityāgaḥ nivṛttiḥ tathā ca pravṛttim pratīcchāyāḥ nivṛttim prati dveṣasya ca sāmānādhikaraṇyena hetu tvāt ātmanaḥ jñasya icchā āśraya tvam abhyupeyam na antaḥkaraṇasya evam ca eka kartṛka tvam jñāna icchā prayatna sukha duḥkha ādīnām samāna āśraya tvam ca tasmāt jñasya eva sukha duḥkha icchā ādayaḥ dharmaḥ na antaḥkaraṇasya iti 
NSV_3.2.36	 nanu astu jñāna icchā ādīnām sāmānādhikaraṇyam parameṣām adhikaraṇam paramāṇu puñjaḥ eva syāt iti śaṅkate tad liṅga tvāt icchā dveṣayoḥ pārthiva ādyeṣu apratiṣedhaḥ pārthiva ādi deheṣu jñāna ādi pratiṣedhaḥ na śakyate kartum kutas icchā dveṣayoḥ ārambha nivṛtti liṅga tvāt tayoḥ ceṣṭā viśeṣa liṅga tvāt ceṣṭāyāḥ ca śarīre pratyakṣa ādi māna siddha tvāt 
NSV_3.2.37	 samādhāna artham pratibandim āha paraśu ādiṣu ārambha nivṛtti darśanāt ārambha nivṛtya ādhāra tvena eva yadi jñāna ādi adhikaraṇa tvam śarīrasya abhyupagamyate tarhi ugha mana nipatana rūpa ārambha nivṛtti darśanāt paraśu ādiṣu api jñāna ādi ādhāra tva prasaṅgaḥ tathā ca pārthiva ādyeṣu apratiṣedhaḥ iti parasya uktam anekāntam iti bhāvaḥ 
NSV_3.2.38	 cetanā cetanayoḥ ceṣṭā niyamam nirūpayati niyamāḥ aniyamau tu tad viśeṣakau niyamaḥ pravṛti ādeḥ janyatā aniyamaḥ tat janyatā atiriktaḥ padārthaḥ tau tad viśeṣakau tad itaretara vyāvartakau tathā ca samavāyena jñāna icchā ādayaḥ cetana dharmāḥ avacchedaka tayā śarīre teṣām janya janaka bhāvaḥ para śu ādau tu yatna viṣaya tayā kriyāḥ iti bhedaḥ 
NSV_3.2.39	 na icchā ādayaḥ manaḥ guṇāḥ iti āha yathā ukta hetu tvāt pāratantryāt sva kṛta abhyāgamāt ca na manasaḥ icchā ādayaḥ iti śeṣaḥ yathā ukta hetu tvāt jñāna icchā ādīnām sāmānādhikaraṇyena hetu hetum at bhāvāt pāratantryāt manasaḥ cetana sahakāri tvāt icchā ādayaḥ na manasaḥ guṇāḥ iti bhāvaḥ atra eva hetu antaram sva kṛta abhyāgamāt iti sva kṛtāt karmaṇaḥ abhyāgamaḥ bhogaḥ manasaḥ kṛtyā ādima tve karmaṇaḥ sva kṛta tva abhāvena jñasya sukha ādi bhogaḥ na syāt tasmāt na manaḥ jñāna icchā ādi āśrayaḥ kintu jñaḥ eva tādṛśaḥ 
NSV_3.2.40–3.2.41	 upasaṃharati pariśeṣāt yathā ukta hetu upapatteḥ ca prasakta pratiṣedhe anyatrā aprasaṅgāt śiṣyamāṇe sampratyayaḥ pariśeṣaḥ tathā ca bhūta indriya manasām pratiṣedhe anyatra aprasaṅgāt śiṣyamāṇe ātmani sa pratyayaḥ jñāna āśraya tva nirdhāraṇam pariśeṣaḥ iti arthaḥ evam darśana sparśanābhyām ekārtha grahaṇāt ityādīnām upapatteḥ upapanna tvāt ātmā icchā ādi āśrayaḥ iti yuktam uktam śiṣya buddhi vaiśadyāya smṛteḥ ātma guṇa tvam viśiṣya āha smaraṇam tu ātmanaḥ jña svābhāvyāt smaraṇam ātmanaḥ eva guṇaḥ kutas jña svābhāvyāt jñāna vatsvābhāvyāt jñāna tva avacchinnava tvam hi ātmanaḥ svabhāvaḥ smṛteḥ ca buddhi santāna dharma tve aham jānāmi ityādi anubhava virādhaḥ 
NSV_3.2.42^1	 smṛti hetūn ām ayaugapadyāt asmaraṇam iti uktam tatra smṛti hetūn āha praṇidhāna nibandha abhyāsa liṅga lakṣaṇa sādṛśya parigraha āśraya āśrita sambandha ānantarya viyoga eka kārya virodha atiśaya prāpti vyavadhāna sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa bhaya arthi tva kriyā rāga dharma adharma nimittebhyaḥ dvandva ante śrūyamāṇasya nimitta śabdasya praṇidhāna ādinā pratyekam anvayaḥ praṇivānam manasaḥ viṣaya antara āsañcāraḥ nibandhanam ekatra kathanam yathā pramāṇena prameya smaraṇam abhyāsaḥ punar punar grahaḥ liṅgam vyāpyam vyāpyena dhūmena dhūma jñānena vyāpakasya agneḥ smaraṇam ānubhavikam lakṣaṇam asādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ yathā jñātam kapi dhvajam arjunasya smārakam sādṛśyam tad bhinna tve sati tad gata bhūyas dharmava tvam yathā candramasam dṛṣṭavataḥ preyasyāḥ smaraṇam parigrahaḥ svīkāraḥ svīkṛta vastunā dātuḥ smaraṇam āśraya āśritau rāja ādi tad parijanau 
NSV_3.2.42^2	 paraspara smārakau sambandhaḥ guru śiṣya bhāva ādiḥ ānantaryam prokṣaṇa avadhāta ādeḥ viyogaḥ dūggamanam tat ca prema āspadānām smārakam eka kāryāḥ antevāsi prabhṛtayaḥ virodhaḥ sahāḥ anavasthānam ahi nakulayoḥ anyatara darśanena anyataram smaryamāṇam anubhūyate atiśayaḥ ādhikayam upanayana dinā saṃskṛte vaṭau ācārya tva smārakaḥ prāpti prāpaṇam dhana āptiḥ dātāram dhanikam smārayati vyavadhānam āvaraṇam yathā svaḍga ādeḥ phoṣa ādiḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ anyatarasya tābhyām prayojakasya vā smaraṇam icchā dveṣau yat viṣayakau tad smārakau bhayam mṛteḥ tad hetoḥ vā smārakam arthi tvam dātuḥ kriyā vyāpāraḥ yathā śākhadeḥ vyāpāraḥ vāyu smārakaḥ rāgaḥ raktiḥ tayā putra ādeḥ smaraṇam dharma adharmabhyām janma antara anubhūta vastu viśeṣa smaraṇam te ete smṛti hetavaḥ 
NSV_3.2.43	 buddheḥ buddhayantarāt vināśaḥ prāk uktaḥ sa ca sva tṛtī ya kṣaṇa vṛtti dhvaṃsa pratiyogitvaḥ eva sambhavati tat ca na sambhavati ekasyāḥ eva buddheḥ viṣaya antara sañcāra viraha ādi satve bahuta rakṣaṇa sthāyi tvāt iti atā āha karma anavasthāyi grahaṇāt anavasthāyinyāḥ śarīra ādi karma dhārāyāḥ pratyakṣa dhārā api vācyā na ca ādya buddheḥ uttara grāhaka tvam viramya vyāpārāḥ abhāvāt pūrva pūrvasya paratas paratas ananubhavāt vināśa siddhau= āśraya nāśa ādeḥ abhāvāt virodhi guṇasya eva na aśaka tvam iti 
NSV_3.2.44–3.2.46	 śaṅkate avyakta grahaṇam anavasthāyi tvāt vidyut sampāte rūpa avyakta grahaṇa vat yadi āśu vena āśinī buddhi sya at tarhi yogyā aśeṣa viśeṣa dharma viśiṣṭa dharmi grāhiṇī na syāt vidyut sampātaka ālīnavastu grahaṇa vat na ca evam tasmāt na tathā iti arthaḥ uttarayati hetu upādānāt pratiṣeddhavyā abhyanujñā vidyut sampāta dṛṣṭāntena pratiṣeddhavyasya buddheḥ āśu vināśi tvam abhyupagatam tathā ca aśaṃtaḥ bādhaḥ samādhāna antaram āha pradīpa arciḥ santati abhivyakta grahaṇa vat tat grahaṇam yathā pradīpa arciṣām santanyamānānām anavasthāyi tve api abhivyakta grahaṇam tathā anyatra api syāt vidyut sampāta sthale yā buddhiḥ utpannā sā sva viṣaye vyaktā eva iti bhāvaḥ 
NSV_3.2.47–3.2.48	 cetanā śarīra guṇaḥ sati śarīre bhāvāt asati śarīre abhāvāt dravye sva guṇa para guṇa upalabdheḥ saṃśayaḥ pārthive candana ādau dravye sva guṇasya rūpa ādeḥ para guṇasya sambandhena āpya śīta sparśa ādeḥ upalabdheḥ evam śarīre api rūpa ādeḥ auṣṇya ādeḥ ca grahaṇāt vipratipattiḥ budhya ādiḥ śarīra guṇaḥ na vā iti siddhāntam āha yāvat śarīra bhāvi tvāt rūpa ādīnām na rūpa ādi hīnam śarīram gṛhyate cetanā hīnam tu gṛhyate yathā uṣṇatā hīnāḥ āpaḥ tasmāt na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā iti tathā ca anumā budhya ādikam na śarīra guṇaḥ ayāvat dravya bhāvi tvāt śabda vat iti 
NSV_3.2.49–3.2.50	 piṭhara pāka vadimatena śaṅkate na pāka ja guṇa antara utpatteḥ dravyasya na atyantam rūpa uparamaḥ bhavati prāktana rūpa vināśe api rūpa antaram pākāt jāyate eva tathā ca vyabhicāraḥ iti bhāvaḥ siddhāntam āha pratidvandvi siddheḥ pāka jānām apratiṣedhaḥ yāvatsu dravyeṣu pūrva guṇa pratiṣedhaḥ tāvatsu pratidvandvinaḥ guṇa antarasya darśanam yathā śyāma nivṛttau rakta ādīnām iti na punar śarīre cetanā viparītam guṇa antaram upalabhyate cetanā mātra uparamaḥ tu atyantam iti 
NSV_3.2.51–3.2.53	 itas ca na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā śarīra avyāpi tvāt śarīra viśeṣa guṇānām iti śeṣaḥ jñāna sukha ādikam tu na śarīra viśeṣa guṇaḥ śarīrāḥ avyāpaka tvāt śarīra vyāpaka tvam ca sarva avayava avacchedena vidyamāna tvam jñāna ādīnām tu hṛdaya rūpa parimita deśa vṛtti tvāt na śarīra guṇa tvam na keśa nakha ādiṣu anupalabdheḥ na rūpa ādīnām api śarīra vyāpaka tvam keśanasu a ādiṣu anupalabdheḥ pariharati tvac paryanta tvāt śarīrasya keśa nakha ādiṣu aprasaṅgaḥ indriya āśraya tvam śarīrasya lakṣaṇam tu akūparyantam hi jaivamanaḥ sukha duḥkha saṃviti āyatanam śarīram tasmāt na keśa nakha ādiṣu cetanā utpadyate artha kāritaḥ tu śarīra upanibandhaḥ keśa ādīnām iti 
NSV_3.2.54–3.2.55	 itas ca na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā śarīra guṇa vaidharmyāt dvividhaḥ śarīra guṇaḥ apratyakṣaḥ ca guru tvam bāhya indriya grāhyaḥ ca rūpa ādiḥ vidha antaram tu cetanā na karaṇa apratyakṣā su saṃvedya tvāt nā atīndriyāḥ manaḥ viṣaya tvāt tasmāt dravya antara guṇaḥ iti codayati na rūpa ādīnām itaretara vaidharmyāt itaretara vidharmāṇaḥ rūpa ādayaḥ na śarīra guṇa tvam jahāti evam rūpa ādi vaidharmye api cetanā śarīra guṇa tvam na hāsyati iti 
NSV_3.2.56	 pariharati aindriyaka tvāt rūpa ādīnām apratiṣedhaḥ apratyakṣa tvāt ca iti yathā itaretara vidharmāṇaḥ na dvaividhyam ativartante tathā cetanā api na dvaividhyam ativarteta yadi śarīra guṇa āsyāt ativartate tu tasmāt na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanāḥ iti bhūta indriya manasaḥ siddhe satya ārambhaḥ dāḍharya arthaḥ iti atra prayogaḥ na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanāḥ nimitta antarāḥ abhāve virodhi guṇa darśane ca satya yāvat dravya bhāvi tvāt aptsu auṣṇya vat iti evam parīkṣitā buddhiḥ 
NSV_3.2.57	 atha manaḥ parīkṣyate tat pratiśarīram ekam anekam vā iti vicāre jñāna ayaugapadyāt ekam manaḥ ayugapad jñānāni bhavanti etad pratyakṣa siddham etat ca manasaḥ eka tvam sādhayati katham yadi bahūni manāṃsi syuḥ pratīndriyam mana ssaṃbandhaḥ iti yugapad aneka artha sannidhāne yugapad jñānāni bhaveyuḥ na tu bhavanti tasmāt viṣaya antareṣu pratyaya paryāyāt ekam manaḥ iti 
NSV_3.2.58–3.2.60	 codayati na yugapad aneka kriyā upalabdheḥ atha khalu adhyāpakaḥ adhīte vrajati kamaṇḍalum dhārayati panthānam paśyati ityādyāḥ kriyāḥ yugapad bhavanti iti prāptam manasaḥ bahu tvam iti pariharati alāta cakra darśana vat tad upalabdhiḥ āśu sañcārāt āśu sañcārāt alāta cakrasya bhramataḥ vidyamānaḥ kramaḥ na gṛhyate iti yugapad kriyāḥ bhavanti iti abhimānaḥ bhavati yathā ukta hetu tvāt ca aṇu aṇu manaḥ ekañcā iti dharma samuccayaḥ yaḥ eva ikatve hetuḥ manasaḥ uktaḥ jñānāḥ ayaugapadyam tena evā aṇu manaḥ avasātavyam iti 
NSV_3.2.61	 manasaḥ khalu bhoḥ sa indriya śarīre vṛttiḥ iti śarīre vicārite manaḥ eva vicāritam bhavati atas punar śarīram vicāryate kim ayam puruṣa karma nimittaḥ śarīra sargaḥ āhosvit bhūtamātra nimittaḥ iti vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ atra idam tatvam pūrva kṛta phalā anubandhāt tad utpattiḥ pūrva śarīre yā pravṛttiḥ vāc buddhi śarīra ambha lakṣaṇā tad pūrva kṛtam tasya phalam tad janitau dharma adharmau tasya phalasyāḥ anubandhaḥ ātma samavetasya avasthānam tena prayuktebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ tasya utpattiḥ śarīrasya na svatantrebhyaḥ iti ayam nyāyaḥ abhidhīyate tad tad puruṣa viśeṣa guṇa prerita bhūta pūrvakam śarīram kāryatve sati puruṣa artha kriyā sāmarthyāt yat puruṣa artha samartham tad puruṣa guṇa viśeṣa prerita bhūta pūrvakam dṛṣṭam yathā ratha ādi iti 
NSV_3.2.62–3.2.63	 atra nāstikaḥ āha bhūtebhyaḥ mūrti upādāna vat tad upādānam yathā karma nirapekṣebhyaḥ nirvṛttāḥ sikata ādi mūrtayaḥ puruṣa artha kāri tvāt upādīyante tathā śarīra sargaḥ api iti na sādhya sama tvāt yathā śarīra utpattiḥ akarma nimittā sādhyā tathā sikata ādīnām api akarma nimitaḥ sargaḥ sādhyaḥ tasmāt asādhanam iti sikata ādīnām api puruṣa karma nimittaḥ eva sargaḥ puruṣa artha kriyā samartha tvāt bhūta ādi vat iti 
NSV_3.2.64	 viṣamaḥ ca ayam upanyāsaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ mūrti upādāna vat iti na utpatti nimitta tvāt mātā pitroḥ na nirbījāḥ imāḥ mūrtayaḥ bīja pūrvikā hi śarīra utpattiḥ mātā pitṛ śabdena lohita retasi bīja bhūte gṛhyete tatra satvasya garbha vāsāḥ anubhavanīyam karma pitroḥ ca putra phala anubhavanīye karmaṇī mātuḥ garbha āśraye śarīra utpattim bhūtebhyaḥ prayojayanti iti ca upapannam bījā anuvidhānam iti 
NSV_3.2.65	 tathā ahārasya utpatti nimitta tvāt iti prakṛtam bhuktam pītam ca āhāraḥ tasya pākāt rasava dravyam nivartyate mātṛ śarīre ca upacīyate bīje ca garbhāśaya sthe tata kalala ādi bhāvena upacīyamānam karma sāpekṣaiḥ bhūtaiḥ pāṇi ādi bhāvam āpadyate yadi punar karma nirapekṣāṇi bhūtāni syuḥ sthālī ādi gatam iva annam pacyeta natu idam asti tasmāt karma sāpekṣāṇi bhūtāni iti 
NSV_3.2.66–3.2.67	 prāptau ca aniyamāt na ca sarvaḥ dampatyoḥ samprayogaḥ garbhādhāna hetuḥ dṛśyate tat api karma sāpekṣa tve liṅgam iti atha manyase śarīram sarva ātmabhiḥ sambadhyate tatra śarīra ādi gataḥ na kaścid niyama hetuḥ asti yena śarīram eva tasya ātmanaḥ vyavatiṣṭheta na ca puruṣa gataḥ kaścid atiśayaḥ dṛśyate yena śarīram ekasya eva upabhoga sādhanam bhavet asti ca niyamaḥ tasmāt vaktavyaḥ niyama hetuḥ atas āha śarīra utpatti nimitta vat saṃyoga utpatti nimittam karma yena eva karmaṇā śarīram utpadyate tat eva śarīram niyamayati iti akarma nimitte tu śarīra sarge yathā ukta doṣaḥ iti 
NSV_3.2.68	 etenā aniyamaḥ pratyuktaḥ yaḥ ayam akarma nimitte śarīra sarge satya niyamaḥ iti ucyate ayam śarīra utpatti nimitta vat saṃyoga utpatti nimittam karma iti anena pratyuktaḥ kaḥ punar ayam niyamaḥ yathā ekasya ātmanaḥ śarīram tathā sarva ātmanām iti upapannaḥ ca tad viyogaḥ karma kṣaya upapatteḥ śarīrasya dve prakṛtī vyaktā avyaktā ca iti tatra avyaktāyā karma samākhyātāyā prakṛteḥ upabhogāt prakṣayaḥ prakṣīṇe ca karmaṇi vidyamānāni bhūtāni na śarīram utpādayanti iti upapannaḥ apavargaḥ karma nirapekṣeṣu śarīra kāraṇeṣu kasya prakṣayāt mokṣamāṇā puruṣāḥ apavṛjyeran bhūta lakṣaṇāyāḥ prakṛteḥ anucchedāt iti 
NSV_3.2.69^1	 punar tad prasaṅgaḥ apavarge tat adṛṣṭa kāritam iti ced atha manyase adṛṣṭa kāri tā śarīra utpattiḥ adṛṣṭa śabdenā adṛśyamānā prakṛtiḥ ucyate sā sarga ādau puruṣa arthena hetunā pravartate pravṛttāḥ mahat ādi bhāvena śarīram utpādayati utpanne tu śarīre adṛṣṭā dṛśyam paśyati dṛśyam ca dvividham viṣayā prakṛti puruṣayoḥ nānātvam ca dṛṣṭe punar tasmin nānātve pradhānam caritārtha tvāt na pravartate iti manyate tatra punar tad prasaṅgaḥ apavarge asya arthaḥ adarśana nimittā ced śarīra utpattiḥ yathā prāk nānātva darśanāt pradhānam puruṣa artham pravartate tathā apavarge api pravarteta 
NSV_3.2.69^2	 na ca evam abhyupagamyate tasmāt na adarśanam sarga kāraṇam caritārtha tā viśeṣaḥ bhaviṣyati iti ca na yuktam carita arthānām api punar punar ārambha darśanāt ādyena śarīreṇa rūpa ādi upalabdheḥ kṛta tve api caritārtham punar dvitīya ādi śarīram hi ārabhyate tena gamyate caritārthānām api punar bhūtānām śarīra ārambhaḥ iti apare tu adṛṣṭam paramāṇu guṇam varṇayanti teṣām api punar punar tad prasaṅgaḥ apavargaḥ iti ukta doṣaḥ samānaḥ paramāṇu guṇasyāḥ adṛṣṭasya sadbhāvāt iti 
NSV_3.2.70	 atha paramāṇu guṇāḥ adṛṣṭa vādinām matam upanyasyati manaḥ karma nimitta tvāt ca saṃyoga ādi anucchedaḥ paramāṇavaḥ sva guṇāt adṛṣṭāt saṃhanyante saṃhatāḥ ca dvayaṇuka ādi krameṇa śarīram utpādayanti tasmin śarīre manaḥ api sva guṇāt adṛṣṭāt upasarpati upasarpaṇa hetoḥ adṛṣṭasya nitya tvāt kim kṛtam apasarpaṇam iti karma āśaya kṣaye karma āśayāt apasarpaṇam iti yuktam prāyaṇam ubhaya vṛttiḥ manaḥ vṛttiḥ adṛṣṭaḥ bhaviṣyati iti na yuktam ekasya jīvana prāyaṇa hetutvā anupapatteḥ 
NSV_3.2.71–3.2.72	 saṃyogāḥ anucchede doṣam āha nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ ca prāyaṇāḥ anupapatteḥ tathā ca prāyaṇasya mṛteḥ anupapatteḥ śarīra ādeḥ nitya tvasya avināśi tvasya ca prasaṅgaḥ asya doṣasya parihāram āha pūrva pakṣimatena aṇu śyāma tā nitya tva vat etat syāt yathā nityasyāḥ aṇoḥ śyāma tvam nityam api agni saṃyogena pratiṣidhyate evam aṇu manasoḥ adṛṣṭam nityam api samyak jñānena pratiṣidhyate iti 
NSV_3.2.73–4.1.2	 etañca na nā akṛtā abhyāgama prasaṅgāt ātmabhiḥ akṛtasya karmaṇaḥ phala upabhoga prasaṅgāt vācā anupapanna pramāṇakasya arthasya abhyupagama prasaṅgāt iti sūtra arthaḥ ātmā śarīram karaṇam arthaḥ buddhiḥ manaḥ tathā tat yathāvastu tatvena tat tathā iha upapāditam manasaḥ anantarā pravṛttiḥ parīkṣitavyā tatra yāvat dharma adharma āśrayam śarīram parīkṣitam sā sarvā pravṛtteḥ parīkṣā iti āha pravṛttiḥ yathā uktā tathā parīkṣitā iti pravṛti anantarāḥ tarhi doṣāḥ parīkṣyantām iti atā āha tathā doṣāḥ uktāḥ iti buddhi samāna āśraya tvāt ātma guṇāḥ saṃsārasya anādi tvādanādinā prabandhena pravartante samyak jñānāt ca mithyājñāna nivṛttau nivartante iti 
NSV_4.1.3	 pravartanā lakṣaṇāḥ doṣāḥ māna īrṣyā asūyā vicikitsā matsara ādayaḥ te kasmāt na upasaṅkhyāyante atra āha tatrairāśyam rāga dveṣa moha arthantara bhāvāt teṣām doṣāṇām trayaḥ rāśayaḥ trayaḥ pakṣāḥ tatra rāgapakṣaḥ kāmaḥ mattsaraḥ spṛhā tṛṣṇā lobhaḥ iti dveṣapakṣaḥ krodhaḥ īrṣyā asūyā drohaḥ amarṣaḥ iti moha pakṣaḥ mithyājñānam vicikitsā mānaḥ madaḥ pramādaḥ iti atra rāgaḥ iti sāmānyam tad viśeṣāḥ kāma ādayaḥ te sāmānyena saṅgrahītāḥ tathā dveṣa sāmānyena krodha ādayaḥ viśeṣāḥ evam mohaḥ iti sāmānyena mithyājñāna ādayaḥ nanu ekam rāga dveṣa mohāḥ lakṣaṇāḥ abhedāt rāga bheda vat iti na rāga dveṣa moha arthantara bhāvāt sati api lakṣaṇasya abhede āntar gaṇikam bhedakam lakṣaṇam asti tad upapatteḥ tri tvam kim punar āntar gaṇikam lakṣaṇam sakti lakṣaṇaḥ rāgaḥ amarṣa lakṣaṇa udveṣaḥ mithyā pratipatti lakṣaṇaḥ mohaḥ etat ca rāga dveṣa mohānām vyavacchedakam lakṣaṇam ātma pratyakṣam iti 
NSV_4.1.4–4.1.5	 atra codayati na eka pratyanīka bhāvāt na artha antaram rāga ādayaḥ eka pratyanīka bhāvāt tatu a jñānam samyak natiḥ ārya prajñā sambodhaḥ iti pratyanīkam trayāṇām atas tat ekam vibhāga vat yathā vibhāgaḥ ekena saṃyogena viruddhyamānaḥ ekaḥ bhavati tathā iti duṣayati vyabhicārāt ahetuḥ eka pratyanīkāḥ pṛthivyām rūpa ādayaḥ eka agni saṃyoga virodhinaḥ na ca eṣām eka tvam iti anekāntar eka yoni tvāt ekam rāga ādayaḥ śabda vat iti api anena eva pratyuktam eka yonayoḥ rūpa ādayaḥ na ca eṣām eka tvam iti sati ca artha antara tve 
NSV_4.1.6–4.1.7	 teṣām mohaḥ pāpīyān na amūḍhasya itara utpatteḥ teṣām mohaḥ pāpaḥ pāpataraḥ vā dvau= abhipretya uktam kasmāt na amūḍhasya itara utpatteḥ tatu a jñānāt tu mohe nivṛtte na rāga dveṣau bhavataḥ iti eka pratyanīka tā na punar eka tvāt iti evañca kṛtvā duḥkha ādīnām uttarottara apāye tad anantara abhāvāt apavargaḥ iti siddhyati prāptaḥ tarhi nimitta naumittika bhāvāt artha antara bhāvaḥ doṣebhyaḥ anyat hi nimittam anyat naimittikam iti doṣasya nimitta tvāt adoṣaḥ mohaḥ iti 
NSV_4.1.9	 pariharati na doṣa lakṣaṇāḥ avarodha amonhasya pravartanā lakṣaṇāḥ doṣāḥ nimitta naimittika upapatteḥ ca tulya jātīyānām apratiṣedhaḥ tulya jātīyānām anekavidhaḥ vikalpaḥ nimittika bhāvaḥ ca yathā buddhiḥ buddhi antarasya nimittam buddhi jātīyā ca iti turya ādayaḥ ca dravyasya nimittam dravya jātīyāḥ nodana abhidhāta saṃyukta saṃyogāḥ saṃskāraḥ ca guṇāḥ iti parīkṣitāḥ 
NSV_4.1.10–4.1.11	 parīkṣitāḥ doṣāḥ doṣān antaram pretyabhāvaḥ tasya asiddhiḥ ātmanaḥ nitya tvāt iti ayam ca siddhārtha anuvādaḥ atha siddhānta sūtram ātma nitya tve pretyabhāva siddhiḥ nityaḥ san= a ātmā praiti pūrva śarīram jahāti mrīyate iti pūrva śarīram ca hitvā bhavati jāyate śarīra antaram upādatte iti tat ca etat punarutpattiḥ pretyabhāvaḥ iti uktam na punar ātmanaḥ janma maraṇe nitya tvāt yasya punar ātmanaḥ utpāta nirodhau tasya kṛta nāśa akṛta āgama doṣāḥ syuḥ iti codayati katham utpattiḥ iti ced kim dharmakāt kāraṇāt idam śarīra indriya mahābhūta ādi vyaktam utpadyate iti 
NSV_4.1.12–4.1.13	 codayati na ghaṭāt ghaṭāḥ aniṣpatteḥ sajātīyāt sajātīyam utpadyate iti matvā ayam pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate pariharati vyaktāt ghaṭa niṣpatteḥ apratiṣedhaḥ na brūmaḥ sarvam sarvasya kāraṇam iti kim tarhi viṣayāt utpadyate vyaktam rūpa ādimat dravyam tat tathābhūtāt eva utpadyate iti tat ca ghaṭe api asti rūpa ādimataḥ eva vyaktāt kapālāt utpadyamāna tvāt iti tat etat tatvam 
NSV_4.1.14–4.1.15	 atas param prāvādukānām darśanāni upanyasya kānicid pratiṣidhyante kānicid abhyanujñāyante tatra tāvat abhāvāt bhāva utpattiḥ na anupamṛdya prādurbhāvāt abhāvāt bhāvaḥ jāyate iti kasyacid darśanam tatra nyāyaḥ nā anupamṛdya prāyurbhāvāt iti na kilā avinaṣṭe bīja ādau kāraṇe kāryam prādurbhavati tasmāt bīja vināśaḥ aṅkura kāraṇam iti vyādhātāt aprayogaḥ upamṛdya prādurbhavati iti prayogaḥ na upapadyate vyāghātāt upamardakasya pūrvam asatve upamardakatvā ayogāt pūrvam satve ca paratas prādurbhāvāḥ ayogāt 
NSV_4.1.16	 punar āśaṅkate na atīta anāgatayoḥ kāraka śabda prayogāt atīte ca anāgate ca avidyamāne kāraka śabdāḥ prayujyante putraḥ janiṣyate janiṣyamāṇam putram abhinandanti abhūt kumbhaḥ bhinnam kumbham anuśocati ajātāḥ putrāḥ pitaram tāpayanti iti bhāktāḥ prayogāḥ dṛśyante kā punar iyam bhaktiḥ ānantarya sāmarthyāt upamṛdya prādurbhāva arthaḥ prādurbhaviṣyan= aṅkuraḥ upamṛdnāti iti bhāktam kartṛ tvam iti 
NSV_4.1.17–4.1.18	 na vinaṣṭebhyaḥ aniṣpatteḥ na bija vināśaḥ aṅkura kāraṇam api tu bīja avayavā pūrva vyūha parityāgena iti sūtra arthaḥ atas na vinaṣṭāt bījāt aṅkuraḥ utpadyate iti krama nirdeśāt apratiṣedhaḥ upamarda prādurbhāvayoḥ paurvāparya niyamaḥ kramaḥ sa khalu hetuḥ abhāvāt bhāva utpatteḥ iti nirdeśaḥ sa ca na pratiṣidhyate iti tasmāt na abhāvāt bhāva utpattiḥ na ca anyat bīja avayavebhyaḥ aṅkurasya kāraṇam asti iti upapādyate bīja upādāna niyamaḥ iti 
NSV_4.1.19–4.1.20	 aparaḥ idānīm āha īśvaraḥ kāraṇam puruṣa karmā aphalya darśanāt puruṣaḥ ayam avaśyam samīhamānaḥ na āpnoti samīhā phalam tena gamyate para adhīnam puruṣasya karma phala ārādhanam iti tasmāt saḥ īśvaraḥ kāraṇam iti na puruṣa karmā abhāve phalāḥ aniṣpatteḥ īśvara śvet kāraṇam antareṇā api puruṣa karma sukha duḥkha upabhogaḥ syāt tatas ca karma vilopaḥ anirmokṣa prasaṅgaḥ ca īśvarasī a ika rūpa tvāt eka rūpā kriyā iti 
NSV_4.1.21^1	 atha īśvara vādinām matena asya parihāram āha tad kārita tvāt ahetuḥ na brūmaḥ karmā anapekṣaḥ īśvaraḥ kāraṇam iti api tu puruṣa karma īśvaraḥ anugṛhṇāti kaḥ anugraha arthaḥ yat yathābhūtam yasya ca yadā paripāka kālaḥ tat tathā tadā ca viniyuktam iti evañca kevalam puruṣa karma phalasya ahetuḥ puruṣa karma kārita tvāt ca kevalam īśvaraḥ api phalasya ahetuḥ atas na yathā ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ tad kārita tvāt iti sarvasya īśvaraḥ nimitta kāraṇam iti uktam bhavati atha manyase siddhe īśvarasya astitve nimitta kāraṇa abhāvaḥ siddhayet tatva siddham tasmāt ayuktam idam iti nyāyate eva tad upapatteḥ yena eva nyāyena īśvarasya kāraṇa tvam siddhayati tena eva astitvam iti na hi avidyamānam kāraṇam iti kaḥ punar iśvarasya kāraṇa tve nyāyaḥ saḥ abhidhīyate pradhāna paramāṇu karmāṇi prāc pravṛtteḥ buddhimat kāraṇa adhiṣṭhitāni pravartante acetana tvāt vātsya ādi vat iti 
NSV_4.1.21^2	 kimartha mayam karoti iti ced svābhāvyāt iti brūmaḥ yathā pṛthivī ādīni bhūtāni dhāraṇa ādi kriyām svābhāvyāt kurvanti tathā eva īśvaraḥ api tat svābhāvyāt pravartate pravṛtti svabhāvakam hi tatvam iti buddhima tvāt eva ca ayam īśvaraḥ ātma antaram tathā hi adharmāḥ ajñāna pramāda hānyā dharma jñāna samādhi sampadā viśiṣṭam ātma antaram īśvaraḥ tadīya buddheḥ ca nitya tvam abhyupagacchāmaḥ katham ucyate nitya jñāna āśrayaḥ īśvaraḥ yugapad aneka kārya utpāgaka tvena pratyartham niyata jñāna tvāt ye tu anitya jñāna āśrayāḥ na te pratyartham niyata jñānāḥ yathā asmad ādayaḥ iti āgamaḥ ca īśvara kāraṇa tā vāde śrūyate ajñaḥ jantuḥ anīśaḥ ayam ātmanaḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ īśvara preritaḥ gacchet svabhram vā svargam eva vā yadā sa devaḥ jāgarti tadā idam ceṣṭate jagat yadā svapiti śānta ātmā tadā sarva nimīlati iti 
NSV_4.1.22	 idānī aparaḥ āha animittaḥ bhāva utpattiḥ kaṇṭaka taikṣṇya ādi darśanāt yathā kaṇṭaka taikṣṇya ādi nirnimittam ca upādāna vat ca tathā śarīra sargaḥ api iti tat idam dṛṣṭānta sūtram kaḥ punar atra nyāyaḥ ucyate animitta racana ādi viśeṣāḥ śarīra ādayaḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣava tvāt kaṇṭaka taikṣṇya ādi vat iti na anupalabhya nimittānām anumānataḥ nimitta upalabdhiḥ katham kaṇṭaka śarīrāni nimittavanti bhavanti saṃsthāna viśeṣava tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat uktam ca atra kim uktam pūrva kṛta phala anubandhāt tad utpattiḥ iti na ca ubhaya pakṣa sampratipannam saṃsthāna viśeṣa vat a nimittam dṛṣṭam iti 
NSV_4.1.23–4.1.24	 apare tu kasyacid nimitta tvam evam varṇayanti iti āha animitta tva at na animittataḥ animittam eva nimittam yatas utpattiḥ tad nimittam iti animitta nimitta tvāt na animittataḥ utattiḥ iti etat ca na nimitta animittayoḥ artha antara bhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ nimitta animittayoḥ artha antara bhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ anyat nimittam anyat ca nimitta pratyākhyānam na pratyākhyānam eva pratyākhyeyam bhavati abhyanujñā pratiṣedhayoḥ eka tva ayogāt 
NSV_4.1.25–4.1.26	 anye manyante sarvam anityam utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvāt kim anityam nāma yasya kadācid bhāvaḥ tat anityam atas ca kādācid kam sarvam anityaḥ utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvāt etat pratikṣipati na anitya tā nitya tvāt sarvam anityam iti bruvāṇaḥ praṣṭavyaḥ kim sarvasyāḥ anitya tā nityāḥ āhosvit anitya iti yadi anityāḥ anitya tāyāḥ abhāvāt sarvam anityam iti vyāhataḥ hetuḥ 
NSV_4.1.27–4.1.28	 atha sva rūpa vādī āha tad anitya tvam agneḥ dāhyam vināśya anuvināśa vat yathā agniḥ dāhyam vināśya anuvinaśyati evam anityatā api sarvam vināśyā anuvinaśyati iti uttaravadi āha nityasya apratyākhyānam yathā upalabdhi vyavasthānāt yatra utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvāt iti ayam hetuḥ upalabhyate tatra tatra hetu sāmarthyāt anitya tvam pratipadyāmahe yatra hetuḥ na asti teṣām anitya tvam katham pratipattavyam iti  
NSV_4.1.29–4.1.31	 sarvam nityam pañcabhūta nitya tvāt bhūtamātram idam sarvam tāni ca nityāni iti bhūta ucchedāḥ anupapatteḥ sarvam nityam iti na utpatti vināśa kāraṇa upalabdheḥ utpatti kāraṇam vināśa kāraṇam ca upalabhyate bhāvānām tat ubhayam nitya tve na syāt iti pūrvavādi āha tad lakṣaṇā avarodhāt apratiṣedhaḥ yat idam utpadyate vinaśyati iti ca manyase na tad bhūta lakṣaṇa hīnam gṛhyate tasmāt bhūta lakṣaṇa avarodhāt sarvam nityam iti sarvam anityam iti brūvāṇaḥ na kaścid jāyate vinaśyati iti pratipadyate tad pratipattau ca hita ahita prāpti parihāraḥ asya parispandaḥ vyarthaḥ āpadyeta sarvasya ca pakṣīkaraṇāt dṛṣṭānta abhāvaḥ vākya upādānam ca vyāhatam 
NSV_4.1.32	 uttaravādi āha na utpatti tad kāraṇa upalabdheḥ bhūta lakṣaṇa avarodhasya anyathā upapattiḥ anena procyate kāraṇa samāna guṇasya utpattiḥ tad kāraṇam ca dṛśyate na ca etat ubhayam nitya viṣayam na ca utpattitaḥ tad kāraṇa upalabdhiḥ śakyā pratyākhyātum na ca āviṣayā kācid upalabdhiḥ upalabdhi sāmarthyāt kāraṇena samāna guṇam kāryam utpadyate iti anumīyate sa kha lu upalabdheḥ viṣayaḥ iti evam ca tad lakṣaṇa avarodha upapattiḥ iti 
NSV_4.1.33^1	 apāsya matam sāṅkhyānām syāyambhuva siddhāntaḥ dūṣyate teṣām ca ayam āśayaḥ trividhaḥ khalu ayam dharmiṇaḥ pariṇāmaḥ dharma lakṣaṇa avasthā rūpaḥ tat yathā suvarṇam dharmi tasya vardhamāna rucaka ādiḥ dharma pariṇāmaḥ lakṣaṇa pariṇāma unaga vādiḥ yadā khalu suvarṇakāraḥ vardhamānakam bhaṅktā rucakam ānayati tadā vardhamānakaḥ vartamāna lakṣaṇam hitvā atīta lakṣaṇam āpadyate rucakaḥ tu anāgatatā lakṣaṇam hitvā vartamāna tām āpadyate vartamāna tām āpannaḥ eva ca rucakaḥ nava purāṇa bhāvam āpadyamānaḥ avasthā pariṇāmavān bhavati nava purāṇa avasthāḥ ca vartamāna lakṣaṇa āśrayāḥ lakṣaṇa pariṇāmaḥ soyam trividhaḥ pariṇāmaḥ dharmiṇaḥ dharma lakṣaṇa avasthāḥ ca dharmiṇaḥ bhinnāḥ ca abhinnāḥ ca dharmiṇā abhinnāḥ santopi dharmāḥ nityāḥ tasmāt bhinnāḥ ca utpatti vināśa viṣayāḥ anityāḥ tathā ca nānāvidheṣu pariṇāmeṣu ekaḥ eva anuvartate 
NSV_4.1.33^2	 evañcāvartamānaḥ nityaḥ eva iti avasthitasya nityasya upādānasya samavāyi kāraṇasya dharma mātram utpadyate naśyati ca evam ca dharma mātram utpatti viṣayaḥ na vastu bhūtaḥ dharmī go ghaṭa ādiḥ abhyupetya idam uditam vastu vaḥ tu dharmāṇām api na utpatti vināśau prāk utpatteḥ arvāk ca vināśāt dharmi rūpeṇa teṣām vartamāna tvāt iti sarva nitya tvam tad avastham eva iti ākṣepa āśayaḥ na vyavasthā anupapatteḥ ayam upajanaḥ iyam nivṛttiḥ iti vyavasthā na upapadyate upajāta nivṛttayoḥ vidyamāna tvāt upajana apāyayoḥ svarūpataḥ kālataḥ vā viśeṣataḥ ca sambandhitaḥ anāgata tvāt itas ca vyavasthā anupapattiḥ iti arthaḥ etat uktam bhavati na tāvat bheda abhedau paraspara parihāra vyavasthita dharmau= ekatra samavetau tasmāt upajana apāya vyavasthāyai dharma lakṣaṇa avasthānām dharmiṇaḥ bhedam icchatā teṣām anitya tvam api abhyupetavyam iti 
NSV_4.1.34–4.1.36	 sarvam pṛthak bhāva lakṣaṇa pṛthaktvāt bhāvasya lakṣaṇam śabdaḥ lakṣyate anena bhāvaḥ sarvaḥ bhāva samākhyā śabdaḥ anekasmin= avayava samūhe rūpa ādi samūhe vartate iti evam anyepi śabdāḥ asya prayogaḥ kumbha śabdaḥ aneka viṣayaḥ eka pada tvāt senā ādi śabda vat iti dūṣayati na aneka lakṣaṇaiḥ eka bhāva niṣpatteḥ aneka lakṣaṇaiḥ iti madhyama pada lopī samāsaḥ anekavidha lakṣaṇaiḥ iti gandha ādibhiḥ ca guṇaiḥ buddhayā ādibhiḥ ca avayavaiḥ sambaddhaḥ ekaḥ bhāvaḥ utpadyate atas śabdāt eka artha avagatau śeṣāḥ anuktaḥ avagamyate iti guṇa vyatiriktaḥ guṇī avayava vyatiriktaḥ ca avayavī iti vibhakta nyāyam etat tad lakṣaṇa vyavasthānāt apratiṣedhaḥ na kaścid ekaḥ bhāvaḥ iti ayam ayuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kasmāt tad lakṣaṇa vyavasthānāt na hi kumbhaḥ iti ukte anekaḥ arthaḥ gamyate gṛhyate punar eka vacana anta tvāt eka arthaḥ iti 
NSV_4.1.37	 atha ayam aparaḥ ekānta vādaḥ sarvam abhāvaḥ bhāveṣu itaretarābhāva siddheḥ yāvat bhāva jātam tat sarvam abhāvaḥ kasmāt bhāveṣu itaretarābhāva siddheḥ asat pratyaya pratiṣedhābhyām bhāva śabda sāmānādhikaraṇyāt sarvam abhāvaḥ anutpanna pradhvasta paṭa vat sarvaḥ bhāva śabdaḥ asat samāna adhikaraṇaḥ pratiṣedha samāna adhikaraṇaḥ ca pradhvasta paṭa vat yathā na asti paṭaḥ iti katham na asti kadā ca na asti iti sthālī ādi ātmanā anutpadyamānaḥ dhvastaḥ ca iti saḥ ayam ghaṭa śabdaḥ asat pratyaya samāna adhikaraṇaḥ ghaṭasya atyanta asa tvam pratipādayati tathā ca sarve bhāvāḥ asat pratyaya samāna adhikaraṇāḥ tasmāt sarvam abhāvaḥ iti 
NSV_4.1.38	 na svabhāva siddheḥ bhāvānām svena bhāvena bhāvāḥ bhavanti iti sūtra arthaḥ kim punar anena sūtreṇa kriyate pūrva sūtra virodha aścodyate svena bhāvena sadbhāvāt bhāvānām na sarvam abhāvaḥ atha kaḥ ca svaḥ bhāvaḥ bhāvānām dravya guṇa karmaṇām sat ādi sāmānyam dravyāṇām kriyāvat iti evamādiḥ viśeṣaḥ sparśa paryantāḥ pṛthivyāḥ iti pratyekam ca anantaḥ bhedaḥ sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyānām ca viśiṣṭāḥ dharmāḥ gṛhyante saḥ ayam abhāvasyam nirupākhya tvāt sampratyāyakaḥ artha bhedaḥ na syāt asti tu ayam tasmāt na sarvam abhāvaḥ 
NSV_4.1.39–4.1.40	 na svabhāva siddhiḥ āpekṣika tvāt na svabhāva siddhiḥ āpekṣika tvāt svena ātmanā na kiñcid siddham atas na svabhāva siddhiḥ āpekṣikī yathā dīrgha hṛsve para apare iti uttaram āha siddhānta vādī vyāhata tvāt ahetuḥ yadi hṛsva apekṣā akṛtam dīrgham hṛsvam anāpekṣikam atha dīrgha apekṣā akṛtam hṛsvam dīrgham anāpekṣikam paraspara apekṣayoḥ ca yat apekṣayetarat jāyate tad anāpekṣikam iti ubhayoḥ abhāvaḥ ekasya abhāvāt iti 
NSV_4.1.41–4.1.42	 atha aime saṅkhyā ekāntāḥ sarvam ekam sat aviśeṣāt sarvam dvedhā nitya anityabhedāt sarvam trividham jñātā jñānam jñeyam iti sarvam caturdhā pramātā pramāṇam prameyam pramitiḥ iti teṣām pratiṣedha sūtram saṅkhyā ekāntā asiddhiḥ kāraṇa anupapati upapattibhyām saṃkhyā ekāntānām asiddhiḥ kāraṇasya pratijñāta artha vyatirekāt sarvam ekam iti pratijñām kṛtvā yadi pratijñeya vyatiriktam sādhanam bruvati ekāntaḥ na sidhyati iti tat ca sādhanam anyat pratijñeyaḥ ca arthaḥ a nyaḥ iti dvaita prasakteḥ evam dvaita ādiṣu api atha pratijñeya vyatiriktam sādhanam na asti evam api ekāntaḥ na sidhyati sādhana abhāvāt na sādhyam iti na kāraṇa avayava bhāvāt kāraṇasya sādhya avayava tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ sādhya avayavaḥ eva sā dhanam evañca sati na sādhya vyatiriktam sādhanam iti uktam bhavati na ca asādhanā siddhiḥ iti 
NSV_4.1.43	 uttaravādi āha niravayava tvāt ahetuḥ sādhya avayavaḥ eva kāraṇam iti ahetuḥ ayam kutas niravayava tvāt pratijñātāta arthasya sarvam ekam iti etasmin pratijñāta arthe na kiñcid apavṛjyate anapa vargeṇa sarvam pakṣīkṛtam iti sarvasya niravayavasya pakṣīkaraṇāt na hetuḥ asti na ca sādhyam hetuḥ bhavitum arhati iti 
NSV_4.1.44	 pretyabhāva anantaram uddiṣṭam phalam tasmin sadyas kāla antare ca phala niṣpatteḥ saṃśayaḥ kācid kriyā sadyaḥphalā yathā pacati dogdhi iti tasyāḥ sadyā phalam odana payasī kācid kāla antara phalā yathā kṛṣati vapati iti tasyāḥ kāla antareṇa phalam na kriyā anantaram sasya adhigamaḥ asti ca iyam kriyā agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ iti tasyāḥ phale sandehaḥ kim iyam sadyaḥphalā uta kāla antara phalā iti  
NSV_4.1.45–4.1.46	 atra nirṇayam āha na sadyas kāla antara upabhogya tvāt svargaḥ phalam śrūyate coditayā ca kriyayā na anarthikayā śakyam bhavitum na ca tāpa ādi kāma ugnihotram juhoti tena gamyate havana ādi lakṣaṇa kriyām apekṣamāṇāt ātma manaḥ saṃyogāt viśuddhena abhisandhinā anugṛhītāt ātmani dharmaḥ utpadyate iti sa kāla antare apratibaddhayamāna śaktiḥ deśa ādi anugṛhītaḥ phalam dadāti tat ca patite tasmin dehe sambhavati deha antara āpannasya atas na sadyas iti kāla antareṇa aniṣpattiḥ hetu vināśāt pradhvastāyām pravṛttau pravṛtti phalam na kāraṇam antareṇa utpattum arhati na khalu vinaṣṭāt kāraṇāt kiñcid utpadyate iti
