NSV_4.1.47	 uttaravādi āha prāk niṣpatteḥ vṛkṣa phala vat tat syāt na brūmaḥ vinaṣṭāt kāraṇāt kāryam utpadyate iti api tu agni hotra havana ādi lakṣaṇayā kriyayā yathā uktena vidhinā dharmaḥ jāyate iti uktam tasmāt phalam iti yathā phala arthinā vṛkṣasya mūla seka ādi karma kriyate tasmin= ca pradhvaste pṛthivī dhātuḥ ap dhātunā saṅgṛhīta āntareṇa tejasā pacyamānaḥ rasa dravyam nirvartayati sa dravya bhūtaḥ rasaḥ vṛkṣa anugataḥ pāka viśiṣṭaḥ vyūha viśeṣeṇa sanniviśamānaḥ parṇa ādi phalam nirvartayati evam pariṣeka ādi karma ca arthavat na ca vinaṣṭāt phala niṣpattiḥ tathā pravṛtyā saṃskāraḥ dharma adharma lakṣaṇaḥ janyate sa jātaḥ nimitta antara anugṛhītaḥ kāla antare phalam niṣpādayati uktam ca etat pūrva kṛta phala anubandhā tad utpattiḥ iti 
NSV_4.1.48	 tat idam na asat na sat na sat asat sat asatoḥ vaidharmyāt iti pūrva pakṣa sūtram prāk niṣpatteḥ niṣpatti dharmakam na asat upādāna niyamāt kasya cit utpattaye kiñcid eva upādeyam iti upādāna niyamāt asadbhāva īsamāne na upapadyate iti na api sat utpatteḥ prāc vidyamānasya utpattiḥ anupapannāḥ na api sat asat sat asatoḥ vaidharmyāt sat iti artha abhyanujñā asat iti artha pratiṣedhaḥ etayoḥ vyāghātaḥ vaidharmyam vyāghātāt avyatireka anupapattiḥ iti 
NSV_4.1.49	 prāk utpatteḥ utpatti dharma kamasat iti addhā kasmāt utpāda vyaya darśanāt vastunaḥ prāc anupalabdhi rūpasya paścāt upalabdhiḥ yāsaḥ asat utpāde sati yujyate vināśaḥ ca upalabdha rūpasya punar anupalabdhiḥ iti na ca etat sarva nitya tva vādinaḥ sambhavati na hi sat pakṣaḥ utpādaḥ na ca vināśaḥ iti utpāda vināśau ca pratyācakṣāṇena lokaḥ heyaḥ 
NSV_4.1.50–4.1.51	 buddhi siddham tu tat asat na ayam satvāt upādāna niyamaḥ api tu sāmarthyāt idam anena śakyam nirvartayitu na idam anena iti evaṃbuddhayā siddham kāryam kṛtvā yat yasya utpattaye samartham tat upādīyate na sarvam sarvasya na sarvasmāt sarvam utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam iti āśraya vyatirekāt vṛkṣa phala utpatti vat iti ahetuḥ yat ca mūla seka ādi karma yat ca parṇa ādi phalam tat ubhayam vṛkṣa āśrayam karma tu iha phalam ca anyatra iti āśraya vyatirekāt vṛkṣa phala utpatti vaditi asiddhaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ 
NSV_4.1.52–4.1.54	 prīteḥ ātma āśraya tvāt apratiṣedhaḥ āśraya vyatirekaḥ asiddhaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ prītiḥ hi ātma pratyakṣa tvāt ātma āśrayāḥ tad āśrayam eva karma dharma saṃjñyakam na putra strī paśu paricchada hiraṇya anna ādi phala nirdeśāt putra ādi phala tvena nirdiśyate grāma kāmaḥ yajeta ityādau na putra ādi ātmani vartate tatra yat uktam prītiḥ phalam iti et ayuktam iti tad sambandhāt phala niṣpatteḥ teṣu phalavat upacāraḥ putra ādi sambandhāt phalam prīti lakṣaṇam niṣpadyate iti putra ādiṣu phalavat upacāraḥ yathā anne prāṇa śabdaḥ annam vai prāṇāḥ iti anna sādhana tvāt prāṇānām evam prīti karaṇa tvāt putra ādau phala upacāraḥ iti 
NSV_4.1.55	 phala anantaram duḥkham uddiṣṭa m uktam ca bādhanā lakṣaṇam duḥkham iti tat kim idam sarva loka sākṣikasya sukhasya pratyākhyānam āhosvit anyaḥ kalpaḥ iti anyaḥ iti āha katham na vai sarva loka sākṣikam sukham śakyam pratyākhyātum ayam tu janma maraṇa prabandha anubhava nimittāt duḥkha nirviṇṇasya duḥkha bhāvanā upadeśaḥ tat idam āha vividha bādhana ayogāt duḥkham eva janma utpattiḥ tatra jāyate iti janma tena śarīra indriya buddhayaḥ upadiśyante tasya janmanaḥ utpattiḥ janma utpatti vividhā tu bādhanā hīnā madhyamā ca utkṛṣṭā ca iti utkṛṣṭāḥ nārakiṇām tiraścām tu madhyamā manuṣyāṇī tu hīnāḥ devānām hīnatarā evam sarvam utpatti sthānam vividha bādhana anuṣaktam paśyataḥ sukhe sukha sādhaneṣu ca duḥkha saṃjñā vyavatiṣṭhate tatas sarva loka viṣayā tṛṣṇā vicchidyate tṛṣṇā prahāṇāt sarvasmāt duḥkhāt pramucyate yathā viṣa yogāt payaḥ viṣam iti buddhayamānaḥ maraṇa duḥkham na prāpnoti iti 
NSV_4.1.56–4.1.57	 na sukhasya api antarāa niṣpatteḥ na tu ayam duḥkha uddeśaḥ sukha pratyākhyānāya kasmāt sukhasya api bādhana antarāaniṣpatteḥ sarva śarīriṇām tat aśakyam pratyākhyātum iti itas ca bādhanā nivṛtteḥ vedayataḥ paryeṣaṇa doṣāt apratiṣedhaḥ paryeṣaṇam prārthanā paryeṣaṇasya doṣaḥ prārthitasya asampattiḥ sampannasya ca nyūna tvam bahu pratyanīkam sampadyate iti asmāt paryeṣaṇa doṣāt nānāvidhaḥ manaḥ santāpaḥ bhavati iti evam vedayataḥ bādhanāyāḥ anivṛttiḥ bādhanā nivṛtteḥ ca duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvanam upadiśyate iti 
NSV_4.1.58	 duḥkha vikalpe sukha abhimānāt ca duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvanā upadeśaḥ yaḥ ca asya sukha artham yatamānasya duḥkha vikalpaḥ bhavati tam sukha aṅga bhūtam sukham iti manyamānaḥ punar tad upādattaḥ punar jāyate iti na saṃsāram ativartate sarvam duḥkham iti tat asyāḥ sukha saṃjñāyāḥ pratikṣepaḥ duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvanam upadiśyate duḥkha anuṣaṅgāt duḥkham janma iti na sukhasya abhāvāt 
NSV_4.1.59	 duḥkha upadeśa anantaram apavargaḥ samprati ākhyāyate ṛṇa kleśa pravṛti anubandhāt apavarga abhāvaḥ ṛṇa anubandhāt jāyamānaḥ vai brāhmaṇaḥ tribhiḥ ṛṇaiḥ ṛṇavān jāyate brahmacaryeṇa ṛṣibhyaḥ yajñena devebhyaḥ prajayā pitṛbhyaḥ iti evam śruti siddhāt kleśa anubandhāt janana maraṇa ādi nimittāt pravṛti anubandhāt vā na apavargaḥ iti anubandhaḥ sarvadā karaṇīyatā iti 
NSV_4.1.60^1	 pradhāna śabdena anupapatteḥ guṇa śabdena anuvādaḥ nindā praśaṃsā upapatteḥ na ayam ṛṇaiḥ iti pradhāna śabdaḥ yatra khalu ekaḥ pratyādeyam dadāti itaraḥ pratideyam gṛhṇāti tatra ayam ṛṇa śabdaḥ pradhānam bhavati anyatra bhāktaḥ saḥ kaḥ upamā arthaḥ asvātantryam yathā ṛṇavān asvatantraḥ evam gṛhasthaḥ yajamānaḥ karmasu paratantraḥ jāyate iti gārhasthya liṅgam ca mantra brāhmaṇam karma abhivadati yat ca mantra brāhmaṇam karma abhivadati tad patnī sambandha ādinā gārhasthya liṅgena upapannam tasmāt gṛhasthaḥ ayām jāyamānaḥ abhidhīyate atha api vihitam vānūdyeta kāmāt vā arthaḥ parikalpyeta vihita anuvacanam nyāyyam iti ṛṇavān iva asvatantraḥ gṛhasthaḥ karmasu pravartate iti upapannam vākyasya sāmarthyam phalasya hi sādhanāni prayatna viṣayaḥ na phalam tāni saṃpannāni phalāya kalpante vihitam ca jāyamānam vidhīyate ca tena yaḥ saṃbaddhyate soyam yajamānaḥ iti pratyakṣa vidhāna abhāvāt iti ced na pratiṣedhasya api pratyakṣa abhidhāna abhāvāt 
NSV_4.1.60^2	 ṛc brāhmaṇam ca apavarga abhidhāyī abhidhīyate ṛcaḥ ca brāhmaṇāni ca ca apavarga abhivādīni bhavanti ṛcaḥ ca tāvat karmabhiḥ mṛtyum ṛṣayaḥ niṣeduḥ prajāvantaḥ draviṇam icchamānāḥ atha apare ṛṣayaḥ manīṣiṇaḥ param karmabhyaḥ amṛta tva mānaśuḥ na karmaṇā na prajayā dhanena tyāgena eke amṛta tva mānaśuḥ pareṇa nākam nihitam gṛhāyām vibhrājate yat yatayaḥ viśanti veda aham etam puruṣam mahāntam āditya varṇam tamasaḥ parastāt tam evam viditvā atimṛtyum eti na anyaḥ panthāḥ vidyate ayanāya atha brāhmaṇāni trayaḥ dharma skandhā yajñaḥ adhyayanam dānam iti prathamaḥ tapaḥ eva dvitīyaḥ brahmacarya ācārya kula vāsī iti tṛtīyaḥ atyantam ātmānam ācārya kule avasādayan sarve eva ete puṇya lokāḥ bhavanti brahma saṃsthaḥ amṛtam eti etam eva pravrājinaḥ lokam abhītsantaḥ pravrajanti iti evam anye ca tatra yat uktam ṛṇa anubandhāt apavarga abhāvaḥ iti etat ayuktam iti ye catvāraḥ pathayaḥ deva yānāḥ iti ca cātu rāśrabhya śruterakauśramya anupapattiḥ 
NSV_4.1.61	 phala arthinaḥ ca idam brāhmaṇam jarā maryam vai etat satram yat agni hotram darśa pūrṇamāsau ca iti katham avagamyate ucyate samāropaṇāt ātmani apratiṣedhaḥ prājāpatyām iṣṭim nirupya tasyām ca sarva vetasam hutvā ātmani agnīn samāropya atha brāhmaṇaḥ pravrajet iti śrūyate tena jānīmaḥ prajā vitta loka eṣaṇābhyaḥ vyutthitasya nivṛtte phala arthi tve samāropaṇa vidhīyate iti evañca brāhmaṇāni saḥ anyat vṛtam upākariṣyamāṇaḥ yā akṣavalkyaḥ maitreyīm iti ha uvāca pravrajiṣyanvā are aham asmāt sthānāt asmi hanta te anayā kātyāyanyā sahāntam karavāṇi iti atha api ukta anuśāsanā asi maitreyi etāvat are khalu amṛta tvam iti ha uktavāḥ yājñavalkayaḥ pravavrājaḥ iti 
NSV_4.1.62	 pātra caya anta anupapatteḥ ca phala abhāvaḥ jarā āmarye karmaṇi aviśeṣeṇa kalpyamāne sarvasya pātra caya antāni karmāṇi iti prasajyate eṣaṇa avyutthānam na śrūyate etat ha sma vai pūrve vidvāṃsaḥ prajām na kāmayante kim prajayā kariṣyāmaḥ yeṣām naḥ ayam ātmā ayam lokaḥ iti te hasma putra eṣaṇāyāḥ ca vitta eṣaṇāyāḥ ca loka eṣaṇāyāḥ ca vyutthāya atha bhikṣā caryam caranti iti eṣaṇābhyaḥ ca vyutthitānām pātra caya antāni karmāṇi na upapadyante iti na aviśeṣeṇa kartuḥ prayojakam phalam bhavati iti cāturāśramya vidhānāt cetihāsa purāṇa dharma śāstreṣu ekāśramya anupapattiḥ tat apramāṇam iti ced na pramāṇena tad prāmāṇyasya abhyanujñānāt viṣaya vyavasthānāt ca tad prāmāṇya upapattiḥ yajñaḥ mantra brāhmaṇa ātmaka veda bhāgasya viṣayaḥ lokam itihāsa purāṇayoḥ loka vyavahāra saṃsthāpanam dharma śāstrasya na ca ekena sarvam pratijñāpyate iti yathā viṣayam etāni pramāṇāni indriya vat iti 
NSV_4.1.63–4.1.65	 yat punar etat kleśa anubandhasya avicchedāt iti suṣuptasya svapna adarśane kleśa abhāvāt apavargaḥ yathā suṣuptasya svapna adarśane kleśa anubandhaḥ vicchidyate tathā muktasya āyāti yat api pravṛti anubandhāt iti na pravṛttiḥ pratisandhānāya hīna kleśasya prakṣīṇeṣu rāga dveṣa moha lakṣaṇeṣu kleśeṣu pravṛttiḥ na pratisandhānāya pratisandhānam tu pūrva janma nivṛttau punarjanma tat ca adṛṣṭa kāritam tasyām prahīṇāyām pūrva janma abhāvaḥ apratisandhānam apavargaḥ atra codayati na kleśa santateḥ svābhāvika tvāt na upapadyate kleśa anubandha vicchedaḥ kasmāt anādiḥ ayam kleśa santatiḥ na ca anādiḥ śakyaḥ ucchettum iti 
NSV_4.1.66–4.1.68	 atra kaścid parihāram āha prāk utpatteḥ abhāva nitya tva vat svābhāvike api anitya tvam yathā anādiḥ prāk utpatteḥ abhāvaḥ utpannena bhāvena nivartyate evam svābhāvikī kleśa santatiḥ anityā iti aparaḥ āha aṇu śyāma tā nitya tva vat vā yathā anādiḥ aṇu śyāma tā atha ca agni saṃyogāt anityā tathā kleśasantatiḥ api iti ayam tu śuddha samādhiḥ na saṅkalpa nimittapyāt ca rāga ādīnām karma nimitta tvāt itaretara nimittāvāt ca iti samuccayaḥ anubhūta viṣaya prārthanā saṅkalpaḥ tasya tatu a jñānāt anutpattiḥ tad anutpattau ca tad kāryāṇām rāga ādīnām atyantam anutpattiḥ iti 
NSV_4.2.1^1	 kim nu khalu bhoḥ yāvantaḥ viṣayāḥ tāvatsu pratyekam tatu a jñānam utpadyate athavā kvacid iti na tāvat pratyekam viṣayāṇām ānantyāt na api kvacid utpadyate tarhi yatra na utpannam tatu a jñānam tatra anivṛttaḥ mohaḥ iti moha śeṣa prasaṅgaḥ atha manyase anya viṣayam tatu a jñānam anya viṣayam moham nivartayati evam ca sati apavargaḥ prāṇi mātre prāpnoti na kaścid prāṇī kasyacid arthasya tatvam na vetti na moha artha aparijñānāt na tatu ajñāna anutpatti mātram mohaḥ api tu mithyājñānam tat ca yasmin viṣaye pravartamānam saṃsāra bījam bhavati sa tatvataḥ jñeyaḥ kim punar tad mithyā jñānam anātmani ātma grahaḥ aham asmi iti mohaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ iti anātmānam khalu aham asmi iti paśyataḥ dṛṣṭiḥ ahaṅkāraḥ iti kim punar tad artha jātam yat viṣayaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ śarīra indriya manaḥ vedanā buddhayaḥ katham tat viṣayaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ saṃsāra bījam bhavati ayam khalu śarīra ādi artha jātam aham asmi iti vyavasitaḥ tad ucchedena ātma ucchedam manyamānaḥ anuccheda tṛṣṇā pariplutaḥ punar tat upādatte tad upādadānaḥ janma maraṇāya yatate 
NSV_4.2.1^2	 tena aviyogāt na atyantam duḥkhāt vimucyate iti yaḥ tu duḥkham duḥkha āyatanam duḥkha anuṣaktam ca sukham sarvam duḥkham iti paśyati sa duḥkham parijānāti parijñānam ca duḥkham prahīṇam bhavati anupādānāt sa viṣān na vat evam doṣān karma ca duḥkha hetuḥ iti paśyati parijñātam ca duḥkham prahīṇam bhavati anupādānāt na ca aprahīṇeṣu doṣeṣu duḥkha prabandha ucchedena śakyam bhavitum iti doṣān jahāti prahīṇeṣu ca doṣeṣu na pravṛttiḥ pratisandhānāya iti uktam pretyabhāva phala duḥkhāni ca jñeyāni vyavasthāpayati karma ca doṣān praheyān apavargaḥ adhigantavyaḥ tasya adhigama upāya ḥ tatva jñānam evam catṛ sṛbhiḥ vidhābhiḥ prameyam vibhaktam āsevamānasya abhyasyataḥ bhāvayataḥ samyak darśanam yathābhūtauvabodhastatva jñānam utpadyate doṣa nimittānām tatu a jñānāt aṅkāra nivṛttiḥ śarīra ādi duḥkhāntam prameya jātam doṣa nimittam tad viṣaya tvāt mithyājñānasya tat idam yat viṣayam tatu a jñānam utpannam tat viṣayam ahaṅkāram nirvartayati samāne viṣaye tayoḥ virodhāt tat ayam śāstra artha saṅgrahaḥ anūdyate nā apūrvam vidhīyate iti 
NSV_4.2.2	 prasaṅkhyān ānupūrvī tu khalu doṣa nimittam rūpa ādayaḥ viṣayāḥ saṅkalpa kṛtāḥ kāmāḥ viṣayāḥ indriya arthāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ gṛhyante te mithyā saṅkalpyamānāḥ rāga dveṣa mohān janayanti kaḥ punar eṣām mithyā saṅkalpaḥ asādhāraṇa pratyaya utpatti nimitta tvena vyavasāyaḥ mama iva ete iti tān asādhāraṇa tayā praticakṣīta na ete mama daiva cora agni dāyāda sādhāraṇāḥ iti evam etasya praticakṣāṇasya yaḥ vyavasāyaḥ tad viṣayaḥ mohaḥ sa nivartate tad nivṛttau adhyātmam śarīra ādīn prasañcakṣīta kim punar prasaṅkhyānam śarīra ādiṣu na ete ātmanaḥ iti vyatireka darśanam pratisaṅkhyānāt adhyātma viṣayohaṅkāraḥ rūpa ādi viṣaya mithyā saṅkalpaḥ nivartate saḥ adhyātmam vijānan bahis ca su vivikta cittaḥ viharan muktaḥ ucyate iti atas kācid saṃjñā bhāvayitavyā kācid heyā iti ucyate na artha nirākaraṇam na artha upādānam kintu yathā vyavasthitaḥ eva viṣaye kiñcid bhāvanīyam kiñcid nirākaraṇīyam iti 
NSV_4.2.3	 tad nimittam tu avayavi abhimānaḥ teṣām doṣāṇām nimittam tu avayavi abhimānaḥ tatra avayavī iti saṃjñā bhāvanīyā strī saṃjñā sa pariṣkārāḥ heyāḥ puruṣasya pariṣkāraḥ bandhanam striyāḥ puruṣa saṃjñā sa pariṣkāra iti pariṣkāraḥ tu nimitta saṃjñā anuvyañjana saṃjñā ca tatra nimitta saṃjñā dantoṣṭham cakṣuḥ nāsam iti anuvyañjana saṃjñā rāgam pravartayati iti praheyāḥ prahāṇam ca asya api keśa māṃsa śoṇita asthi snāyu śirā kapha pitta uccāra ādi saṃjñā tām aśubha saṃjñā iti ācakṣate tām asya bhāvayataḥ kāma rāgaḥ prahīyate sati eva dvividhe viṣaye kācid saṃjñā bhāvanīyā kācid parivarjanīyoti upadiśyate 
NSV_4.2.4	 atha idānīm artham nirākariṣyatā avayavi upapādyate vidyā avidyā dvaividhyāt saṃśayaḥ sat asatoḥ upalambhāt dvividhā vidyā sat asatoḥ anupalambhāt avidyā api dvividhāḥ evam ca avayavī yadi upalabhyate atha na upalabhyate na kathañcana mucyate saṃśayāt iti tatra tāvat uktam na vidyā aviyāt vaividhyam saṃśaya kāraṇam upalabdhi anupalabdhyoḥ pūrva pada viśeṣaṇa tvāt 
NSV_4.2.5–4.2.6	 tad asaṃśayaḥ pūrva hetu prasiddha tvāt tasmin= avayavini na yuktaḥ saṃśayaḥ pūrva uktānāḥ hetūnām apratiṣedhāt ye avayavinaḥ artha antara bhāve hetavaḥ uktāḥ te na śakyāḥ pratiṣeddhum iti atha avayavi nirākaraṇa vādī āha pūrva pakṣiṇā pratibandī rūpeṇa sva mata nirūpaṇam vṛti anupapatteḥ api na saṃśayaḥ saṃśayā anupapattiḥ na asti avayavī iti 
NSV_4.2.7	 tad vibhajate kṛtsna eka deśa avṛtti tvāt avayavānām avayavi abhāvaḥ avayavāḥ avayavini varteran avayavī vā avayaveṣu avayavāḥ avayavini vartamānā kṛtsnena vā varteran eka deśena vā na tāvat avayavini kṛtsne vartante avayavāḥ avayava a= ayavinaḥ parimāṇa bhedāt alpa parimāṇāḥ avayavāḥ mahā parimāṇaḥ avayavī alpa parimāṇeṣu mahā parimāṇasya avyāptiḥ eka dravyaḥ ca avayavaḥ prāpnoti eka avayave vṛtti tvāt na api avayavya eka deśena avayavaḥ vartate na hi asya avayavinaḥ anye eka deśa bhūtāḥ santi iti 
NSV_4.2.8–4.2.9	 atha avayaveṣu eva avayavī vartate teṣu ca avṛtteḥ avayavi abhāvaḥ na tāvat pratyavayavam vartate tayoḥ parimāṇa bhedāt avayavinaḥ ca eka dravya tā prasaṅgāt na api eka deśena sarveṣu anya avayava abhāvāt tat evam na yuktaḥ saṃśayaḥ na asti avayavī iti pṛthak ca avayavebhyaḥ avayavya vṛtteḥ na api avayava vyatirekeṇa anyatra vartate agrahaṇāt nitya tva prasaṅgāt avayava vyatirekeṇa anyatra vartamānaḥ upalabhyeta nityaḥ ca syāt anādhāram dravyam nityam iti 
NSV_4.2.10	 na ca avayavi avayavāḥ na ca atra dharmibhyaḥ avayavebhyaḥ avayavī dharmaḥ pṛthak upalabhyate nitya tva prasaṅgāt iti ca samānam avayavī ca eka deśena avayave vartate iti avayava samūha mātram avayavī prāpnoti ekasmin= ca avayave eka deśena vartamānaḥ avayavī eka avayava upalambhāt eka deśena upalabdhau tat sthānaḥ avayavī gṛhyeta na tu eka tantu darśane paṭa upalabdhiḥ bhavati tat evaṃmukta saṃśayaḥ abhidhīyate na atyavayavī iti yat tāvat avayavāḥ avayavini vartante iti tat na anabhyupagamāt na kāraṇam kārye vartate api tu kāraṇe kāryam iti 
NSV_4.2.11–4.2.13	 yat punar etat avayavi avayaveṣu vartamānaḥ eka deśena vartate kṛtsnena vā vartate iti tat na ekasmin bheda abhāvāt bheda śabda prayoga anupapatteḥ apraśnaḥ kṛtsnam iti eka deśaḥ iti ca bheda viṣayau= etau śabdau na ca etau= ekasmin= upapannau anekasya aśeṣa tā kṛtsna śabda arthaḥ aśeṣasya kasyacid abhidhānam eka deśa śabdasya na ca etat iha upapadyate iti tasmāt na avayavini kṛtsna śabdaḥ na api eka deśa śabdaḥ iti anya avayava abhāva anna eka deśena vartate iti ahetuḥ avayava antara abhāve api avṛtteḥ ahetuḥ avayava antara abhāvāt iti yadi api eka deśaḥ avayava antara bhūtaḥ tathā api avayave avayava antaram varteta na avayavī iti anyaḥ avayavī iti anya avayava abhāve api avṛtteḥ avayavinaḥ na eka deśena vṛttiḥ anya avayava abhāva āditya hetuḥ sarva agrahaṇam avayavya siddheḥ iti vyavasthitaḥ api idam āha keśa samūhe taimirika upalabdhi vat tat upalabdhiḥ yathā ekaikaḥ keśaḥ taimirikeṇa na upalabhyate keśa samūhaḥ tu upalabhyate tathā ekaikaśas aṇuḥ na upalabhyate aṇu samūhaḥ tu upalabhyate tat idam aṇu samūha viṣaya grahaṇam iti 
NSV_4.2.14	 atra brūmaḥ sva viṣaya anatikrameṇa indriyasya paṭu manda bhāvāt viṣaya grahaṇasya tathā abhāvaḥ nā aviṣaye pravṛttiḥ prakṛṣyamāṇam indriyam na sva viṣayam atikrāmati na hi cakṣu prakṛṣyamāṇam rasam gṛhṇāti na aprakṛṣyamāṇam sva viṣayāt pracyavate api tu sva viṣayaḥ eva indriyasya prakarṣa apakarṣa apekṣāṇi paṭu manda bhāvena grahaṇāni bhavanti iti tatra paṭu grahaṇam sāmānya viśeṣa tadvatām grahaṇam iti mandam tu grahaṇam sāmānya mātra ālocanam iti saḥ ayam taimirikaḥ kaścid cakṣuḥ viṣayam keśam na gṛhṇāti keśa samūham ca gṛhṇāti ubhayam api ātaimirikasya cakṣuṣaḥ viṣayaḥ iti paramāṇa vaḥ tu atīndriyāḥ darśana viṣaya tvam na pratipadyante te saṃhatā aindriyakāḥ asaṃhatāḥ atīndriyāḥ iti mahān vyāghātaḥ tasmāt upapadyate avayavī darśana viṣayaḥ iti 
NSV_4.2.15	 avayava avayavi prasaṅgaḥ ca evam āpralayāt yaḥ ca ayam avayavinaḥ avayaveṣu vṛtti vikalpāt abhāvaḥ saḥ avayavasya sva avayaveṣu prasajyamānaḥ niravayavāt vā paramāṇutaḥ nivarteta pralayāt vā ubhayathā ca upalabdhi viṣayasya abhāvaḥ tad abhāvāt upalabdhi abhāvaḥ upalabdhi āśrayaḥ ca ayam vṛtti pratiṣedhaḥ sa tu āśrayam vyādhnan ātma dhātāya kalpate iti 
NSV_4.2.16	 na praayaḥ aṇu sadbhāvāt avayava vibhāgam āśritya vṛtti pratiṣedhāt abhāvaḥ prasajyamānaḥ niravayavāt paramāṇoḥ nivartate na sarva pralayāya kalpate loṣṭasya hi vibhajyamāna avayavasya alpataram uttaram uttaram bhavati sa ca ayam alpatara prasaṅgaḥ yatas nivartate yatas na alpīyaḥ asti tam paramāṇum pracakṣmahe iti tad antaḥ avaya vi bhāgaḥ sa tu nityaḥ 
NSV_4.2.17–4.2.19	 param vā truṭeḥ avayava vibhāgasya anavasthānāt dravyāṇām asaṅkhayeya tvāt truṭi tva nivṛttiḥ iti ākāśa vyatibhedāt tad anupapattiḥ tasya aṇoḥ niravayavasya nitya tva anupapattiḥ kasmāt ākāśena paramāṇuḥ vyatibhinnaḥ vyatibhedāt sa avayavaḥ sāvayava tvāt anitya tvam iti ākāśa asarva gata tvam vā atha etat neṣyate paramāṇoḥ antar na asti ākāśam iti asarva gata tvam prasajyate iti 
NSV_4.2.21–4.2.21	 antar bahis ca kārya dravyasya kāraṇa antara vacanāt akārye tad abhāvaḥ antar iti kāraṇa antaraiḥ pihitam kāraṇam ucyate bahis iti vyavadhāyakam avyavahitam kāraṇam eva ucyate tat etat kārya dravyasya sambhavati na aṇoḥ a kārya tvāt iti yat punar etat ākāśam asarva gatam prasajyeta antar paramāṇunā asambandhāt iti tat na sarva gata tva arthāḥ aparijñānāt na ayam sarva gata arthaḥ yat na asti tena sambandhaḥ iti api tu yat mūrtimat tena sarveṇa mūrtimatā sambandhaḥ iti sarva gata tva arthaḥ na asatā sambandhaḥ na hi paramaṇoḥ madhyam asti tasmāt tena asambandhāt na ākāśam asarva gatam prasajyate śabda saṃyoga vibhavāt ca sarva gatam yadā kadācid utpannāḥ śabdāḥ vibhavanti ākāśe tad āśrayāḥ bhavanti manobhiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ tad kāryaiḥ ca saṃyogāḥ vibhavanti ākāśe na asaṃyuktam ākāśena mūrtam kiñcid dravyam utpadyate tasmāt na asarva gatam ākāśam iti 
NSV_4.2.22–4.2.23	 avyūha avaṣṭambha vibhu tvāni ca ākāśa dharmāḥ sarpatā kriyāvatā dravyeṇa ākāśam na vyūhyate sarpataḥ ca kriyāvataḥ dravyasya kriyā hetum guṇam na pratibadhnāti kasmāt asparśa tvāt yat sparśa vat bhavati tat hayūhyate pratibadhnāti na tu evaṃdharmakam ākāśam tasmāt apratidhāti iti sa bhavān sa avayave sparśavati dravye dṛṣṭam dharmam viparītena āśaṅkitum arhati iti ukta ca atra yadi paramāṇuḥ vibhajyate paramāṇuḥ na syāt kim kāraṇam vibhāge alpatara prasaṅgasya yatas na alpīyaḥ tatra avasthānam iti vināśam ca paramāṇoḥ bhavan kāraṇa vināśāt vā kalpyeta kāraṇa vibhāgāt vā ubhayam ca na asti paramāṇoḥ akārya tvāt iti uktam tasmāt na ākāśa vyatibhedāt anitya tvam iti punar paramāṇu sāvayava tva vādī āha mūrtimatām ca saṃsthāna upapatteḥ avayava sadbhāvaḥ paricchinnānām sparśavatām saṃsthānam tri koṇam catur asram samam parimaṇḍalam iti ucyate yat tat saṃsthānam saḥ avayava sanniveśaḥ parimaṇḍalāḥ ca paramāṇavaḥ tasmāt sāvayavāḥ ghaṭa ādi vat iti 
NSV_4.2.24	 saṃyoga upapatteḥ ca madhye san= aṇuḥ pūrva aparābhyām aṇubhyām saṃyujyate vyavahitaḥ ca bhavati tena aṇunā madhya gatena pūrva bhāgena pūrva aṇunā saṃyujyate apara bhāgena ca aparāṇunā yau tau pūrva aparau bhagau tau= asyā avayavau sarvatas evam saṃyujyamānasa sarvatobhāgāḥ avayavāḥ iti atra ucyate yat tāvat mūrtimatvāt sa avayavāḥ paramāṇavaḥ iti tat na anaikāntika tvāt yaḥ paramāṇoḥ avayavaḥ sa mūrtimān niravayavaḥ ca iti anekāntaḥ paramāṇuḥ sa avayavaḥ iti bruvatā ca kārya viśeṣaḥ paramāṇuḥ iti uktam bhavati kārya viśeṣaḥ paramāṇuḥ ca iti vyāhatam bhavati yat punar etat saṃyoga upapatteḥ ca iti tat na sparśava tvāt madhye san= aṇuḥ pūrva paramāṇu dvaya vyavadhāyakaḥ na sāvayava tvāt 
NSV_4.2.25	 anavasthā kāri tvāt anavasthā anupapatteḥ ca apratiṣedhaḥ yāvat mūrtimat yāvat ca saṃyujyate tat sarvam sāvayavam iti anavasthā kāriṇau= imau hetū sā ca anavasthā na upapadyate satyām anavasthāyām satyau hetū syātām tasmāt apratiṣedhaḥ ayam niravayavasya iti vibhāgasya ca vibhajyamāna hāniḥ na upapadyate tasmāt pralaya anta tā na upapadyate iti anavasthāyām ca pratyadhikaraṇam dravya avayavānām ānantyāt parimāṇa bhedānām guru tvasya ca agrahaṇam samāna parimāṇa tvam ca avayava avayavinoḥ paramāṇu avayava vibhāgāt ūrdhvam 
NSV_4.2.26	 yadi bhavān buddhīḥ āśritya buddhi viṣayāḥ santi iti manyata mithyā buddhayaḥ etāḥ yadi tatva buddhayaḥ syuḥ buddhyā vivecane kriyamāṇe buddhi viṣayāṇām yāthārthyam upalabhyeta buddhayā vivecanāt tu bhāvānām yāthātmya anupalabdhiḥ tantu apakarṣaṇe paṭa sadbhāva anupalabdhi vat tad anupalabdhiḥ yaḥ ete buddhi viṣayāḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ gavā ādayaḥ ca na ete tatva buddhayaḥ kutas buddhyā vivicyamāne bhedaśas grahaṇāt yathā ayam tantuḥ ayam tantuḥ iti buddhayā tantuṣu vivicyamāneṣu na paṭaḥ kaścid asti yaḥ paṭa buddheḥ viṣayaḥ syāt evam aśuṃṣu buddhayā vivicyamāneṣu evam tad avayaveṣu tāvat yāvat paramāṇuḥ paramāṇavaḥ api bhāgaśas vivicyamānāḥ tāvat yāvat pralayaḥ iti tat evam sarvasya asatve gavā ādi buddhayaḥ paṭa ādi buddhayaḥ ca mithyā buddhayaḥ iti 
NSV_4.2.27	 vyāhata tvāt ahetuḥ yadi buddhayā vivecanam bhāvānām sarva bhāva anupapattiḥ iti ayuktam kasmāt vyāghātāt kaḥ vyāghātaḥ saha asambhavaḥ yadi buddhayā vivecanam bhāvānām na sarva bhāva anupapattiḥ atha sarva bhāvānupaparttina buddhyā vivecanam bhāvānām iti sarva bhāvānām anupapattiḥ iti bruvāṇaḥ pramāṇam paryanuyojyaḥ yadi pramāṇam bravīti vyāhatam bhavati atha na bravīti arthaḥ asya na siddhayati pramāṇa abhāvāt atha aprāmāṇikī siddhiḥ sarva bhāva uppattiḥ kasmāt na siddhayati yaḥ ca sarva bhāvānām abhāvaḥ bhāveṣu itaretara apekṣa siddheḥ iti etasmin vāde doṣaḥ uktaḥ saḥ iha api draṣṭavyaḥ iti 
NSV_4.2.28–4.2.29	 yat punar etat yadi vyatirikta ghaṭa ādi dravyam syāt tantuṣu buddhyā vivicyamāneṣu buddhayā pṛthak upalabhyeta iti tatra āha tad āśraya tvāt apṛthak grahaṇam kāraṇa dravya āśritam kārya dravyam na pṛthak upalabhyate yatra āśraya āśrita bhāvaḥ na asti tatra pṛthak grahaṇam pramāṇataḥ ca artha pratipatteḥ buddhayā vivecanāt bhāvānām yāthātmya upalabdhiḥ yat asti yathā ca yatra asti yathā ca tat sarvam pramāṇataḥ upalabhyata tathā vivecanam bhāvānām tena sarva śāstrāṇi sarva karmāṇi sarve ca śarīriṇām vyavahārāḥ upapadyante iti 
NSV_4.2.30–32	 pramāṇa anupapati upapattibhyām na sarva bhāva anupapattiḥ pramāṇa anupapati upapattibhyām yadi sarvam na asti iti pramāṇam upapādyate sarvam na asti iti etat vyāhanyate atha pramāṇam na upapadyata sarvam na asti iti asya kathaṃsiddhiḥ atha pramāṇam antareṇa siddhiḥ sarvam asti iti asya katham na siddhiḥ punar ca prapañca mithyātva vādya āha svapna viṣaya abhimāna vat ayam pramāṇa prameya abhimānaḥ māyā gandharvanagara mṛgatṛṣṇikā vat vā yathā svapne viṣayāḥ na santi atha ca viṣaya abhimānaḥ bhavati evam pramāṇāni prameyāni ca na santi atha ca pramāṇa prameya abhimānaḥ bhavati iti  
NSV_4.2.33–4.2.34	 hetu abhāvāt asiddhiḥ svapna ante viṣaya abhimāna vat pramāṇa prameya abhimānaḥ na punar jāgarita ante viṣaya upalabdhi vat iti atra hetuḥ na asti svapna ante ca asantaḥ viṣayāḥ upalabhyante iti atra api hetu abhāvaḥ atas asiddhiḥ smṛti saṅkalpa vat ca svapna viṣaya abhimānaḥ yathā smṛtiḥ ca saṅkalpaḥ ca pūrva upalabdha viṣayau na tasya pratyākhyānāya kalpete tathā svapne viṣaya grahaṇam pūrva upalabdha viṣayam na tasya pratyākhyānāya kalpate iti 
NSV_4.2.35–4.2.36	 evañca sati mithyā upalabdhi nā śastatva jñānāt svapna viṣaya abhimāna praṇāśa vat pratibodhe sthāṇau puruṣaḥ ayam iti adhyavasāyaḥ mithyā upalabdhiḥ tatva jñānena ca mithyā upalabdhiḥ sa nivartate na arthaḥ sthāṇu puruṣa sāmānya lakṣaṇaḥ yathā svapna upalabdhānām ye adhyavasāyāḥ te jāgrat avasthā upalabdhyā nivartante na arthaḥ viṣaya sāmānya lakṣaṇaḥ iti buddheḥ ca evam nimitta sadbhāva upalambhāt mithyā buddheḥ nimittam asti kim punar tat sāmānya darśanam viśeṣa darśanam avidyamāna viśeṣa adhyāropaḥ iti mithyā rūpam ca mithyā buddhim ca pratipadyamānena tasyāḥ nimittam pratyetavyam nimittam pratipadyamānena arthaḥ abhyupeyaḥ iti 
NSV_4.2.37	 tatva pradhāna bhedācya mithyā buddheḥ dvaividhya upapattiḥ tatvam sthāṇuḥ iti pradhānam puruṣaḥ iti tatva pradhānayoḥ alope mithyā buddhiḥ utpadyate sāmānya grahaṇāt sthāṇau puruṣaḥ iti puruṣe sthāṇuḥ iti buddhiḥ utpadyate yatas atas mithyā buddhiḥ tatra samāne viṣaye mithyā buddhīnām samāveśaḥ sāmānya grahaṇa vyavasthānāt yasya tu nirātmakam nirupākhyam sarvam tasya asamāveśaḥ prasajyate gandha ādau ca prameye gandha ādi buddhayaḥ mithyā abhimatāḥ tatva pradhānayoḥ sāmānya grahaṇasya ca abhāvāt tatva buddhayaḥ eva bhavanti tasmāt ayuktam etat pramāṇa prameya buddhayaḥ mithyā iti 
NSV_4.2.38–4.2.40	 doṣa nimittānām tatu a jñānāt ahaṅkāra nivṛttiḥ iti uktam purastāt atha tatu a jñānam katham utpadyate iti apekṣāyām samādhi viśeṣa abhyāsāt sa tu pratyāhṛtebhyaḥ indriyebhyaḥ manasaḥ dhārakeṇa prayatnena dhāryamāṇasya ātmanā saṃyogaḥ tatva bubhutsā viśiṣṭaḥ samādhi viśeṣaḥ sati hi tasmin indriya artheṣu buddhayaḥ na utpadyante tad abhyāsa vaśāt tu tatvabuddhiḥ utpadyate na artha viśeṣa prāvalyāt na upapadyate samādhi viśeṣa abhyāsaḥ abubhutsamānasya api budhi utpatteḥ yathā stanayitnoḥ śabda prabhṛtiṣu iti kṣudh ādhibhiḥ pravartanāt ca kṣudh pipāsābhyām vyādhibhiḥ ca anicchataḥ api buddhayaḥ utpadyante tasmāt na yuktaḥ samādhi viśeṣaḥ 
NSV_4.2.41	 astu etat samādhim vihāya vyutthānam vyutthāna nimittam samādhi pratyanīkam ca sati tu etasmin pūrva kṛta phala anubandhāt tad utpattiḥ pūrva kṛtaḥ pūrva śarīra abhyastaḥ samādhi viśeṣaḥ tasya phalam dharmaḥ tad kṛtaḥ punar samādhi viśeṣaḥ iti samādhi viśeṣāt ca bāhya viṣaya abhibhavaḥ laukikasya api tāvat samādhi viśeṣa avasthitasya bāhya viṣaya upanipāte buddhayaḥ na utpadyante kim punar yoginaḥ iti 
NSV_4.2.42–4.2.44	 araṇya guhā pulina ādiṣu yogāmyāsa upadeśaḥ apavarge api evam prasaṅgaḥ bāhya viṣaya upanipāte artha jñānāni prādurbhavanti apavargepi evam prasaṅgaḥ yuktaḥ ca apavarge bāhya viṣaya upanipātaḥ vidyate iti buddha yutpāda prasaṅgaḥ  na niṣpanna avaśyambhāvi tvāt karma vaśāt niṣpanne śarīre ceṣṭa indriya artha āśraye nimitta bhāvāt avaśyam bhāvī buddhīnām utpādaḥ na anyathā iti 
NSV_4.2.45–4.2.46	 tad abhāvaḥ ca apavarge tasya śarīra ādi kāraṇasya abhāvaḥ apavargaḥ tasmāt sarva duḥkha vimokṣaḥ apavargaḥ yasmāt sarvam duḥkha bījam ca vicchidyate tasmāt sarveṇa duḥkhena vimuktiḥ apavargaḥ iti yama niyamābhyām ātmanaḥ saṃskāraḥ apavarga sādhanam tad artham yama niyamābhyām ātma saṃskāraḥ yogāt ca adhyātma vidhi upāyaiḥ tasya apavargasya adhigamāya yama niyamābhyām ātma saṃskāraḥ kartavyaḥ ahiṃsā satya asteya brahmacarya aparigrahāḥ yamāḥ śauca santoṣa tapaḥ svādhyāya maheśvara praṇidhānāni niyamāḥ ātma saṃskāraḥ punar adharma hānam dharma upacayaḥ ca yoga śāstrāt ca adhyātma vidhiḥ pratipattavyaḥ sa punar prāṇāyāmaḥ pratyāhāra dhyānam dhāraṇa iti indriya viṣayeṣu ca prasaṅkhyāna abhyāsaḥ rāga dveṣa vighāta arthaḥ upāyaḥ tu yoga ācāra vidhānam iti 
NSV_4.2.47–4.2.48	 jñāna grahaṇa abhyāsaḥ tad vidyaiḥ ca saha saṃvādaḥ jñāna grahaṇa abhyāsā tad vidyaiḥ ca saha saṃvādaḥ jñāna grahaṇam śāstra grahaṇam tat vidyā yatnam upāyam buddhi ante iti taiḥ saha saṃvādaḥ prajñā paripāka artham iti tad vidyaiḥ ca saha saṃvādaḥ iti avibhakta artha vacanam tad vibhajate tam śiṣya guru sabrahmacāri viśiṣṭa śreyaḥ arthibhiḥ anasūyibhiḥ abhyupeyāt etat tu pnigadena eva nīta arbham 
NSV_4.2.49–4.2.50	 yadi ca manyeta pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahaḥ pratikūlaḥ parasya iti tatra āha pratipakṣa hīnam api vā prayojana artham arthi tve tam abhyupeyāt iti vartate paratas prajñām upāditsamānaḥ tatva bubhutsā prakāśena sva pakṣam anavasthāpayan sva darśanam paribodhayet iti anyonya pratyanīkāni ca prāvādukānām darśanāni iti tatvā adhyavasāya saṃrakṣaṇa artham jalpa vitaṇḍe bīja praroha saṃrakṣaṇa artham kaṇṭaka śākhā āvaraṇa vat anutpannatatva jñānānām aprahīṇa doṣāṇām tad artham ghaṭamānānām etat iti 
NSV_4.2.51	 vidyā nirveda ādibhiḥ ca pareṇa avajñāyamānasya tābhyām vigṛhya kathanam tābhyām jalpa vitaṇḍābhyām iti vigṛhya iti vijigīṣayā na tatu abubhutsayā iti vidyā pālana artham ca etat kartavyam na lābha pūjā khyātyartham iti pravṛtti doṣa sambandhaḥ pretyabhāvaḥ prapañcitaḥ phalam duḥkham vimuktiḥ ca caturthe parikīrtitāḥ 
NSV_5.1.1^1	 sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratyavasthānasya vikalpāt jāti bahutvam iti saṃkṣepeṇa uktam tad vistareṇa vibhajate yadi api jāti nigraha sthāna sāmānya lakṣaṇa anantaram prathamaḥ eva adhyāye yuktaḥ viśeṣaḥ lakṣayitum tathā api eṣām bahutara tvāt prameya parīkṣā vilambaḥ mā bhūt iti apekṣitā vā śiṣyaiḥ prameya parīkṣā sā ca saṃśaya ādi parīkṣām vinā na śakyā kartum iti tad parīkṣā kṛtā tasmāt śiṣya anurodhena muniḥ saṃśaya ādi parīkṣā pūrvikām prameya parīkṣām tāvat pravartayā ambabhūva tad anantaram avaśiṣṭam pañcama adhyāye vartayati sādharmya vaidharmya utkarṣa apakarṣa varṇya avarṇya vikalpa sādhya prāpti aprāpti prasaṅga pratidṛṣṭānta an utpatti saṃśaya prakaraṇa hetu arthāpatti viśeṣa upapati upalabdhi anupalabdhi nitya anitya kārya samāḥ kāḥ khalu imāḥ jātayaḥ 
NSV_5.1.1^2	 sthāpana ahetau prayukte caturviṃśati pratiṣedha hetavaḥ tatra jātiḥ nāma sthāpana aheto prayukte yaḥ pratiṣedha samarthaḥ hetuḥ jāteḥ prayoga pratiṣedhāt asat uttara tvāt ca ārambhaḥ na yuktaḥ chala ja ati nigraha sthānānām sva vākye parivarjanam iti hi pratiṣiddhā jātiḥ iti anārambha prayojakasya ukta tvāt uktam jāteḥ ārambha prayojanam svayam ca sukaraḥ prayogaḥ yadā tu vādī parasya sādhanam sādhu iti manyate lābha pūjā khyāti kāmaḥ ca bhavati tadā jātim prayuṅkte kadācid ayam jāti uttareṇa ākulīkṛta buddhiḥ uttaram na pratipadyate tadā nigṛhyeta vādinaḥ ca ekānta jayaḥ atas ekānta parājayāt varam sandehaḥ iti yuktaḥ jāteḥ prayogaḥ iti sādharmyam eva samam vaidharmyam eva samam iti sama arthaḥ prayogaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ iti 
NSV_5.1.2	 lakṣaṇam tu sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām upasaṃhāre tad dharma viparyaya upapatteḥ sādharmya vaidharmya samau sādharmyeṇa upasaṃhāre tad viparīta sādharmyeṇa pratyavasthānam vaidharmyeṇa upasaṃhāre tad viparīta sādharmyeṇa pratyavasthānam vā sādharmya samaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt utpatti dharmakam kumbha ādi anityam dṛṣṭam iti atra yadi anitya ghaṭa sādharmyāt anityaḥ nityena api ākāśena asya sādharmyam amūrta tvam asti iti nityaḥ prāptaḥ iti tasmin= eva hetau ākāśa vaidharmyāt iti ukte yadi nitya ākāśa vaidharmyāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ sādharmyam api ākāśena asti amūrta tvam iti atas nityaḥ prāptaḥ iti evam vaidharmyeṇa ukte hetau tad vaidharmyeṇa pratyavasthānam sādharmyeṇa ukte hetau tad viparīta vaidharmyeṇa pratyavasthānam vaidharmya samaḥ tasmin= eva hetau= ākāśa vaidharmyāt iti ukte yadi nitya ākāśa vaidharmyāt anityaḥ anityena asya ghaṭena vaidharmyam amūrta tvam atas nityaḥ prāptaḥ iti tasmin= eva hetau ghaṭa sādharmyāt iti kṛte yadya nitya ghaṭa sādharmyāt anityaḥ vaidharmyam api amūrta tvam atas nityaḥ prāptaḥ iti 
NSV_5.1.3	 anayoḥ uttaram go tva ādeḥ go siddhi vat tad siddhiḥ gavā aśvasā dharmye satva ādau samāne vaidharmye ca ekaśapha tva ādau sādharmyāt satvāt gauraśvaḥ bhavati na vaidharmyāt ekaśapha tva ādeḥ agauḥ gauḥ bhavati kim kāraṇam ekasya ananvayāt ekasya cāvyāvṛtteḥ yat anvaya vi atireki sādharmyam tasmāt tad dharma vyavasthā go tvam ca tathā tasmāt go tvāt eva jāti viśeṣāt gauḥ siddhayati tathā iha api amūrta tvam ubhaya vyatirekayubhayā anvayi ca tasmāt nitya tvam anitya tvam vā na śakyam pratipattum api tu anvaya vyatireka sampannāt utpatti dharmaka tvāt anitya tvam iti atas yat bravīṣi viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt iti ayam viśeṣaḥ iti 
NSV_5.1.4	 sādhya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ dharmarvi kalpāt ubhaya sādhya tvāt ca utkarṣa apakarṣa varṇa avarṇya vikalpa sādhya samāḥ avidyamāna dharma adhyāropaḥ utkarṣaḥ vidyamāna dharma apacayaḥ apakarṣaḥ varṇyaḥ sādhyaḥ avarṇyaḥ asādhyaḥ vikalpaḥ viśeṣaḥ eteṣām dharmāṇām udbhāvanā arthāḥ prayogāḥ utkarṣa sama ādyāḥ jātayaḥ sādhya sādhana dharmayoḥ tulya tayā pratyavasthānam sādhya samaḥ yathā tasmin= eva hetau ghaṭa sādharmyāt iti kṛte yadi yathā ghaṭaḥ tathā śabdaḥ iti tarhi ghaṭaḥ rūpa ādimān śabdaḥ api evam prasaktaḥ iti utkarṣa samaḥ dṛṣṭānta dharmam sādhye samāropayat utkarṣa samaḥ śabdaḥ arūpaḥ iti ghaṭopi evam prasaktaḥ iti atra sādhye dharma abhāvam dṛṣṭāntāt samāropayati yaḥ saḥ apakarṣa samaḥ ghaṭaḥ anityaḥ iti apavarṇyaḥ śabda upyevam śabdaḥ vāvarṇyaḥ iti ghaṭopi evam iti varṇyāvarṇya samau sati etasmin utpatti dharmaka tve vibhāga ja śabdaḥ na vibhāga jaḥ ghaṭaḥ vibhāga jā vibhāga ja vikalpe ca nitya aniti a vikalpaḥ iti vikalpa samaḥ ghaṭaḥ vā anityaḥ iti atra kaḥ hetuḥ ayam api sādhya vat prajñāpayitavyaḥ iti ubhaya sādhya vat pratyavasthānāt sādhya samaḥ 
NSV_5.1.5	 eteṣām uttaram kiñcid sādharmyāt upasaṃhāra siddheḥ vaidharmyāt apratiṣedhaḥ na brūmaḥ yāvantaḥ ghaṭa dharmāḥ te ghaṭaḥ iva śabde bhavanti iti api tu yasya sādhakaḥ dharmaḥ upapadyate sa tad sādhanam tatra upasaṃhriyate aśeṣa dharma upasaṃhāre tu yathā tathā iti eva na syāt saḥ eva asau= iti syāt tathā iha api iti ayama doṣaḥ yat punar etat vibhāga jā vibhāga ja vikalpa vat nitya anitya vikalpaḥ iti yathā utpatti dharmaka tvam anvayavyatireki na evam vibhāga ja tvam na hi kiñcid vibhāgāt jāyamānam yathā ukta viśeṣaṇam nityam anityam vā dṛṣṭam iti etat anuttaram 
NSV_5.1.6–5.1.7	 sādhya atideśāt ca dṛṣṭānta upapatteḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhyaḥ iti bruvatā na dṛṣṭānta vilakṣaṇam vyajñāyi dṛṣṭāntaḥ hi nāma buddhi sāmya viṣayaḥ evam sādhya atideśāt dṛṣṭānte upapadyamāne sādhya tvam anupapannam iti prāpya sādhyam aprāpya vā hetoḥ prāptyā viśiṣṭa tvāt aprāptyā asādhaka tvāt ca prāpti aprāpti samau tasmin= eva hetau ghaṭa ādi sādharmyāt iti kṛte yadi tāvat ayam hetuḥ sādhyam prāpnoti prāptyā aaviśiṣṭaḥ kaḥ aviśeṣa arthaḥ ubhayoḥ vidyamāna tā na avidyamānaḥ samprāpyate iti hetoḥ sādhana arthaḥ hīyate atha na prāpnoti aprāpteḥ aviśiṣṭa tvāt ahetuḥ bhavati prāptyā pratyavasthānam prāpti samaḥ aprāptyā pratyavasthānam aprāpti samaḥ 
NSV_5.1.8–5.1.9	 anayoḥ uttaram ghaṭa ādi niṣpatti darśanāt pīḍane ca abhicārāt apratiṣedhaḥ mṛd piṇḍa prāpta daṇḍa ādīnām na aviśeṣaḥ na ca sādhya sādhana bhāva nivṛttiḥ na hi mṛd piṇḍa prāpta udaṇḍaḥ sādhana tvam jahāti na api itarat sādhya tvam jahāti dṛṣṭāntasya kāraṇa anapadeśāt pratyavasthānāt ca pratidṛṣṭāntena prasaṅga pratidṛṣṭānta samau yathā asmin= eva hatau ghaṭa ādi sādharmyāditi kṛte ghaṭaḥ eva tāvat anityaḥ iti atra kaḥ hetuḥ iti prasaṅga samaḥ pratidṛṣṭāntena pratyavasthānam pratidṛṣṭānta samaḥ yathā kriyāvān ātmā kriyā hetu guṇa yogāt loṣṭa vat iti ukte pratidṛṣṭāntaḥ upādīyate kriyā hetu guṇa yuktam ākāśam akriyam dṛṣṭam iti kaḥ punar asya ākāśasya kriyā hetuḥ guṇaḥ vāyunā saṃyogaḥ vāyu gata vega ākhya saṃskāra apekṣaḥ vāyu vanaspati saṃyoga vat iti 
NSV_5.1.10	 anyoḥ uttaram pradīpa upādāna prasaṅga vinivṛtti vat tad vinivṛttiḥ idam tāvat ayam pṛṣṭavyaḥ ke pradīpam upādadate kimartham ca etat iti didṛkṣamāṇāḥ dṛśya darśana artham iti atha pradīpam didṛkṣamāṇena dīpa antaram dṛśyate pradīpaḥ atas pradīpa darśana artham pradīpa antara upādānam vyartham iti atha dṛṣṭāntaḥ kim artham ucyate iti aprajñātasya jñāpana artham iti atha dṛṣṭānte kāraṇa apadeśaḥ kimarthaḥ codyate yadi prajñāpana artham prajñātaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ sa khalu laukika parīkṣakāṇām yasmin= arthe buddhi sāmyam sa dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti tad prajñāpana arthaḥ kāraṇa apadeśaḥ nirarthakaḥ iti prasaṅga samasya uttaram 
NSV_5.1.11–5.1.12	 pratidṛṣṭānta hetu tve ca na ahetu dṛṣṭāntaḥ pratidṛṣṭāntam bruvatā na viśeṣa hetuḥ ucyate anena kāraṇena pratidṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhakaḥ na dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti evam pratidṛṣṭāntasya hetu tve na ahetuḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti upapadyate sa ca katham hetuḥ na syāt yadi apratiṣiddhaḥ sādhakaḥ syāt iti prāk anutpatteḥ kāraṇa abhāvāt anutpatti samaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt iti ukte kaścid brūyāt prāk utpatteḥ śabdasya utpatti dharmaka tvam anitya tva kāraṇam na asti tad abhāvāt śabdaḥ anutpatti dharmakaḥ tatas ca nityaḥ iti anutpatyā pratyavasthānam anutpatti samaḥ 
NSV_5.1.13–5.1.14	 asya uttaram tathā abhāvāt utpannasya kāraṇa upapatteḥ na kāraṇa pratiṣedhaḥ utpannaḥ khalu ayam śabdaḥ iti bhavati prāk utpatteḥ śabdaḥ eva na asti utpannasya śabda bhāvāt śabdasya sataḥ prayatna ānantarīyaka tvam anitya tva kāraṇam upapadyate kāraṇa upapatteḥ ayuktaḥ ayam doṣaḥ prāk utpatteḥ kāraṇa abhāvāt iti sāmānya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ aindriyaka tve samāne nitya anitya sādharmyāt saṃśaya samaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti ukte hetau saṃśayena pratyavatiṣṭhate sati prayatna anantarīyaka tve asti eva asya nityena sāmānyena sāmyam aindriyaka tvam asti ca dṛṣṭānte na ghaṭena anityena evam nitya anitya sādharmyāt anivṛttaḥ saṃśayaḥ iti 
NSV_5.1.15	 asya uttaram sādharmyāt saṃśaye na saṃśayaḥ vadhaiḥ myādubhayathā vā saṃśayaḥ a tyanta saṃśaya prasaṅgaḥ nitya tva anabhyupagamāt ca sāmānyasya apratiṣedhaḥ sādharmyāt sādharmya darśanāt saṃśayaḥ vaidharmyāt viśeṣa darśanāt na saṃśayaḥ ubhayathā tu saṃśaye sāmānya viśeṣa darśane sati saṃśaye atyanta saṃśaya prasaṅgaḥ nityam sāmānyam saṃśayam karoti iti tu na pratipadyāmahe sati sāmānye viśeṣa darśanāḥ dvi āvṛtteḥ iti 
NSV_5.1.16	 ubhaya sādharmyāt prakriyā siddheḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ ubhayena nityena anityena ca sādharmyāt pakṣa pratipakṣayoḥ pravṛttiḥ prakriyā anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti ekaḥ pakṣaḥ dvitīyaḥ ca nitya sādharmyāt evam ca sati prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti hetuḥ anitya sādharmyeṇa ucyamānaḥ na prakaraṇam ativartate samānam ca etat nitya sādharmyeṇa ucyamāne hetau tat idam prakaraṇa anativṛtyā pratyavasthānam pakaraṇa samaḥ samānam ca etat vaidharmyepi ubhayarvedharmyāt prakriyā siddheḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ iti 
NSV_5.1.17	 asya uttaram pratipakṣāt prakaraṇa siddheḥ pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ pratipakṣa upapatteḥ ubhaya sādharmyāt prakriyā siddhim bruvatā pratipakṣāt prakriyā siddhiḥ uktā bhavati yadi ubhaya sādharmyam tatra ekataraḥ pratipakṣaḥ evam sati upapannaḥ pratipakṣaḥ bhavati tatas anupapannaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ yadi pratipakṣa upapattiḥ pratiṣedhaḥ na upapadyate atha pratiṣedha upapattiḥ pratipakṣaḥ na upapadyate pratipakṣa upapattiḥ pratiṣedha upapattiḥ ca iti vipratiṣiddham etat tatvānavadhāraṇāt eva prakriyā siddheḥ viparyaye prakaraṇa avasānāt tatvā avadhāraṇe hi avasitam prakaraṇam bhavati iti 
NSV_5.1.18	 traikālya asiddheḥ hetoḥ ahetu samaḥ hetuḥ sādhanam tad sādhyāt pūrvam paścāt saha vā bhavet yadi pūrvam sādhanam asati sādhye kasya sādhanam yadi paścāt asati sādhane kasya idam sādhyam atha yugapad sādhya sāghane dvayoḥ vidyamānayoḥ kim kasya sādhanam kim kasya sādhyam iti hetuḥ ahetunā na viśiṣyate ahetunā sāmyat pratyavasthānam ahetu samaḥ 
NSV_5.1.19	 asya uttaram na hetutaḥ sādhya siddheḥ traikālya asiddhiḥ na traikālya asiddhiḥ kutas hetutaḥ sādhya siddheḥ nirvartanīyasya nivṛttiḥ vijñeyasya vijñānam ubhayam kāraṇataḥ dṛśyate saḥ ayam mahān pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ udāharaṇam iti yat tu uktam asati sādhye kasya sādhanam iti yat ca nivartyate yat ca vijñāpyate tasya iti 
NSV_5.1.20–5.1.21	 pratiṣedha anupapatteḥ ca pratiṣeddhavya apratiṣedhaḥ pratiṣedhāt pūrvam paścāt yugapad vā pratiṣedhaḥ na upapadyate pratiṣedha anupapatteḥ sthāpanā hetuḥ siddhaḥ iti arthāpattitaḥ pratipakṣa siddheḥ arthāpatti samaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti sthāpite pakṣe artha apatyā pratipakṣam sādhayataḥ arthāpatti samaḥ yadi anitya sādharmyāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti arthāt āpadyate nitya sādharmyāt asparśa tvad nityaḥ iti 
NSV_5.1.22	 asya uttaram anuktasya arthāpatteḥ pakṣa hāneḥ upapattiḥ anukta tvāt anaikāntika tvāt ca arthāpatteḥ anupapādya sāmarthyam anuktam arthāt āpadyate iti bruvataḥ pakṣa hāneḥ upapattiḥ anukta tvāt anitya pakṣa siddhau= arthāt āpannam nitya pakṣasya hāniḥ iti anaikāntika tvāt ca arthāpatteḥ ubhaya pakṣa samā ca iyam arthāpattiḥ yadi nitya dhārmyāt asparśa tvāt ākāśa vat ca nityaḥ śabdaḥ arthāt āpannam anitya sādharmyāt prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt anityaḥ iti 
NSV_5.1.23–5.1.24	 eka dharma upapatteḥ aviśeṣe sarva aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt sadbhāva upapatteḥ aviśeṣa samaḥ ekaḥ dharmaḥ prayatna ānantarīyaka tvam śabda ghaṭayoḥ upapadyate iti aviśeṣe ubhayoḥ anitya tve sarvasya aviśeṣaḥ prasajyate sadbhāvasya eka dharma upapatteḥ sarva aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt pratyavasthānam aviśeṣa samaḥ asya uttaram kvacid tad dharma upapateḥ kvacid ca anupapateḥ pratiṣedha abhāvaḥ yathā sādhya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ ekasya dharmasya prayatna ānantarīyaka tvasya upapattau= anitya tvam dharma antaram aviśeṣaḥ evam na sarva bhāvānām sadbhāva upapatti nimittam dharma antaram asti yena aviśeṣaḥ syāt 
NSV_5.1.25–5.1.27	 ubhaya kāraṇa upapatteḥ upapatti samaḥ ubhayasya nitya tvasya anitya tvasya ca kāraṇa upapatyā pratyavasthānam utpatti samaḥ asya uttaram upapatti kāraṇa abhyanujñānāt apratiṣedhaḥ ubhaya kāraṇa upapatteḥ iti bruvatā abhyanujñātam anitya tva kāraṇam iti tathā ca virodhāt uttara pakṣa utthānam na yuktam nirdiṣṭa kāraṇa abhāvepi upalambhāt upalabdhi samaḥ nirdiṣṭasya prayatna ānantarīyaka tvasya anitya tva kāraṇasya abhāve vāyunodanāt vṛkṣa śākhā bhaṅga jasya śabdasya anitya tvam upalabhyate nirdiṣṭasya sādhanasya abhāvepi sādhya dharma upalabdhyā pratyavasthānam upalabdhi samaḥ 
NSV_5.1.28–5.1.29	 asya uttaram karaṇa antarāt api tad dharma upapatteḥ apratiṣedhaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti brūvatā kāraṇatas utpattiḥ abhidhīyate na kāryasya kāraṇa niyamaḥ kriyate iti tad anupalabdeḥ anupalambhāt abhāva siddhau tad viparīta upapatteḥ anupalabdhi samaḥ teṣām āvaraṇa ādīnām anupalabdiḥ na upalabhyate anupalambhāt na asti iti abhāvaḥ asyāḥ sidhyati abhāva siddhau hetu abhāvāt tad viparītam astitvam āvaraṇa ādīnām avadhāryate tad viparīta upapatteḥ yat pratijñātam na prāk ucca raṇāt vidyamānasya śabdasya anupalabdhiḥ iti etat na siddhayati saḥ ayam hetuḥ āvarāṇa ādi anupalabdheḥ iti āvaraṇa ādiṣu ca āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdhau ca samaya anupalabdhvā pratyavasthitaḥ anupalabdhi samaḥ bhavati 
NSV_5.1.30	 anupalambha ātmaka tvāt anupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdhiḥ na asti anupalambhāt iti ayamahetuḥ kutas anupalambha ātmaka tvāt anupalabdheḥ upalambhāva mātra tvāt anupalabdheḥ yat vidyate tad upalabdhi viṣayaḥ na vidyate ca yat tad anupalabdheḥ viṣayaḥ saḥ ayam āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdheḥ anupalambhaḥ upalabdhi abhāve anupalabdhau sva viṣaye pravartamānaḥ na svam viṣayam pratiṣedhati apratiṣiddhā ca āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdhiḥ hetu tvāya kalpate āvaraṇa ādīni tu vidyamāna tvāt upalabdheḥ viṣayāḥ yattāni na upalabhyante tad upalabdheḥ sva viṣaya pratipādikāyāḥ abhāvāt anupalabdheḥ viṣayaḥ gamyate na santi āvaraṇa ādīni śabda agrahaṇa kāraṇāni iti anupalambhāt anupalabdhiḥ siddhayati viṣayaḥ sa tasya iti 
NSV_5.1.31	 jñāna vikalpānām ca bhāva abhāva saṃvedanāt adhyātmam ahetuḥ iti vartate śarīriṇām jñāna vikalpānām bhāva abhāvau saṃvedanīyau asti me saṃśaya jñānam na asti me ityādi sā iyam āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdhiḥ upalabdhi abhāvaḥ sva saṃvedyaḥ na asti me śabdasya āvaraṇa ādi upalabdhiḥ iti na upalabhyante śabdasya agrahaṇa kāraṇāni āvaraṇāni iti tatra yat uktam tad anupalabdheḥ anupalambhāt abhāva siddhiḥ iti etat na upapadyate 
NSV_5.1.32–5.1.33	 sādharmyāt tulya dharma upapatteḥ sarva anitya tva prasaṅgāt anitya samaḥ anityena ghaṭena sādharmyāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti bruvataḥ asti ghaṭena anityena sarva bhāvānām sādharmyam iti sarvasya anitya tvam aniṣṭam sampadyate saḥ ayam anitya tvena pratyavasthānāt anitya samaḥ asya uttaram sādharmyāt asiddheḥ pratiṣedha asiddhiḥ pratiṣedhya sādharmyāt pratijña ādi avayava yuktam vākyam pakṣa nivartakam pratipakṣa lakṣaṇam pratiṣedhaḥ tasya pakṣena pratiṣedhyena sādharmyam pratijña ādi yogaḥ tad yadi anitya sādharmyāt anitya tvasya asiddhiḥ sādharmyāt asiddheḥ pratiṣedhasya api asiddhiḥ pratiṣedhyena sādharmyāt iti 
NSV_5.1.34	 dṛṣṭānte ca sādhya sādhana bhāvena prajñātasya dharmasya hetu tvāt tasya ca ubhayathā bhāvāt na aviśeṣaḥ dṛṣṭānte yaḥ khalu dharmaḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvena prajñāyate sa hetu tvena abhidhīyate saḥ ubhayathā bhavati kenacid samānaḥ kutaścid viśiṣṭaḥ sāmānyāt sādharmyam viśeṣāt vaidharmyam evam sādharmya viśeṣaḥ hetuḥ na aviśeṣeṇa sādharmya mātram vaidharmya mātram vā sādharmya mātram vaidharmya mātram ca āśritya bhavān āha sādharmyāt tulya dharma upapatteḥ sarva anitya tva prasaṅgāt anitya samaḥ iti etat ayuktam iti aviśeṣa sama pratiṣedhe ca yat uktam tat api veditavyam 
NSV_5.1.35	 nityam anitya bhāvāt anitye nitya tva upapatteḥ nitya samaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratijñāyate tad anitya tvam śabde kim nityam anityam vā iti yadi tāvat sarvadā bhavati dharmasya sarvadā bhāvāt dharmiṇaḥ api sarvadā bhāvaḥ iti nityaḥ śabdaḥ atha na sarvadā bhavati tarhi anitya tvasya abhāvāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti evam nitya tvena pratyavasthānāt nitya samaḥ 
NSV_5.1.36	 asya uttaram pratiṣedhye nityam anitya bhāvāt anitye anitya tva upapatteḥ pratiṣedha abhāvaḥ pratiṣedhye śabde nitya manitvasya bhāvāt iti ucyamāne anujñātam śabdasya anitya tvam anitya tva upapatteḥ ca na anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratiṣedhaḥ na upapadyate atha na anujñāyate nityam anitya tvasya bhāvāt iti hetuḥ na bhavati iti hetu abhāvāt pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ iti nitya anitya tva virodhāt ca nitya tvam anitya tvam ca ekasya dharmiṇaḥ dharmau= iti virudhyete na sambhavataḥ tatra yat uktam nityam anitya tvasya bhāvāt nityaḥ eva tat avartamāna artham uktam iti 
NSV_5.1.37–5.1.38	 prayatna kārya aneka tvāt kārya samaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti ukte jātiḥ kārya samā prayujyate prayatna kāryam anekadhā dṛṣṭam iti kiñcid prayatna anantaram vyajyate kiñcid prayatna anantaram utpadyate prayatna anantaram upalabdheḥ hetutva adhyāra upeṇa anaikāntika tā darśanāt kārya samaḥ kārya anya tve prayatna ahetu tvam anupalabdhi kāraṇa upapatteḥ sati kārya anya tve anupalabdhi kāraṇa upapatteḥ prayatnasya ahetu tvam śabdasya abhivyaktau yatra prayatna anantaram abhivyaktiḥ tatra anupalabdhi kāreṇa vyavadhānam upapadyate vyavadhāna apohāt ca prayatna anantara bhāvinaḥ arthasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa abhivyaktiḥ bhavati iti na tu śabdasya anupalabdhi kāraṇam kiñcid asti yasya prayatna anantaram apohāt śabdasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa abhivyaktiḥ bhavati iti tasmāt utpadyate śabdaḥ na abhivyajyate iti 
NSV_5.1.39	 evam tāvat jātayaḥ vyavasthitāḥ idānīm ṣaṭpakṣīm upanyasyan= idam āha pratiṣedhe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ prathama pakṣa vādī uttaram bruvati anena sūtreṇa yadi prayatna ānantarīyaka tvam vyaṅgyepi dṛṣṭam iti anaikantika tvāt ahetuḥ tarhi pratiṣedha upyana ekāntikaḥ kasyacid apratiṣedhāt kasyacid pratiṣedhāt iti arthavā śabdasya anitya tva pakṣe prayatna anantaram utpādaḥ na abhi vyaktiḥ iti viśeṣa hetu abhāvaḥ nitya tva pakṣe api prayatna anantaram abhivyaktiḥ na utpādaḥ iti viśeṣa hetu abhāvaḥ soyam ubhaya pakṣa samaḥ hetu abhāvaḥ iti ubhayam api anaikāntikam iti 
NSV_5.1.40–5.1.41	 sarvatra evam sarvāsu jātiṣu ekā prayuktiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe pratiṣedha doṣa vat doṣaḥ yaḥ ayam pratiṣedhe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ anaikāntika tvam āpādyate saḥ ayam pratiṣedhasya pratiṣedhe api samānaḥ tatra anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti sādhana vādinaḥ sthāpanā prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ prayatna kārya aneka tvāt kārya samaḥ iti dūṣaṇa vādinaḥ pratiṣe hetunā dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tṛtīyaḥ pakṣaḥ vipratiṣedhaḥ etasmin vipratiṣedhe samānam anaikāntika tvam doṣaḥ iti caturthaḥ pakṣaḥ 
NSV_5.1.42	 pratiṣedham sa doṣam abhyupetya pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe samānaḥ doṣa prasaṅgaḥ mata anujñā pratiṣedham dvitīya pakṣam sa doṣam abhyupetya tat uddhāram anuktvā anujñāya pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe tṛtīya pakṣe samānam anaikāntika tvam iti samānam dūṣaṇam prasajataḥ dūṣaṇa vādinaḥ mata anujñā prasajyate iti pañcamaḥ pakṣaḥ 
NSV_5.1.43^1	 sva pakṣa lakṣaṇa apekṣā upapati upasaṃhāre hetu nirdeśe para pakṣa doṣa abhyupagamāt samānaḥ doṣaḥ sthāpanā pakṣe prayatna kārya aneka tvāt iti doṣaḥ sthāpanā hetu vādinaḥ sva pakṣa lakṣaṇaḥ bhavati kasmāt sva pakṣa samuttha tvāt sva pakṣa lakṣaṇam doṣam apekṣamāṇaḥ anuddhṛtya anujñāya pratiṣedhepi samānaḥ doṣaḥ iti upapādyamānam doṣam para pakṣaḥ upasaṃharati ittham vā anaikāntikaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ iti hetum nirdiśati atra sva pakṣa lakṣaṇa apekṣayā upapadyamāna doṣa upasaṃhāre hetu nirdeśe ca sati anena para pakṣa doṣaḥ abhyupagataḥ bhavati katham kṛtvā yaḥ pareṇa prayatna kārya aneka tvāt iti anena anaikāntika doṣaḥ uktaḥ tam anuddhṛtya pratiṣedhepi samānaḥ doṣaḥ iti āha evam sthāpanām sa doṣām abhyupetya pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe api samānam doṣam prasajataḥ para pakṣa abhyupagamāt samānaḥ doṣaḥ bhavati yathā parasya pratiṣedham sa doṣam abhyupetya pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe api tathā asya api sthāpanām sa doṣām abhyupetya pratiṣedhe samānam doṣam prasajataḥ mata anujñā prasajyate iti 
NSV_5.1.43^2–5.2.1	 sa khalu ṣaṣṭhaḥ pakṣaḥ tatra sthāpanāḥ hetu vādinaḥ prathama tṛtīya pañcama pakṣāḥ pratiṣedha hetu vādinaḥ dvitīya caturtha ṣaṣṭha pakṣāḥ teṣām sādhu asādhu tāyām mīmāṃsyamānāyām caturtha ṣaṣṭhayoḥ arthyā aviśeṣāt punar ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ caturtha pakṣe samāna doṣa tvam parasya ucyate pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe pratiṣedha doṣa vat doṣaḥ iti ṣaṣṭhe api para pakṣa doṣa abhyupagamāt samānaḥ doṣaḥ iti samāna doṣa tvam eva ucyate na artha viśeṣaḥ kaścid asti iti tatra pañcama ṣaṣṭhayoḥ punarukta doṣaḥ tṛtīya caturthayoḥ mata anujñā prathama dvitīyayoḥ viśeṣa hetu abhāvaḥ iti ṣaṣ pakṣyām ubhayoḥ asiddhiḥ ayukta vādi tvāt yadā tu anupalabdhi kāraṇa abhāve sati prayatna anantaram upalabdheḥ iti viśeṣa hetuḥ ucyate tadā na ṣaṣ pakṣī pravartate iti etāḥ tu jātayaḥ na tatva vivekam upakurvanti iti bheda mātra m āsām uktam iti vipratipatya vipratipatyoḥ nigraha sthāna bahutvam iti saṃkṣepeṇa uktam tat idānīm vibhajyate nigraha sthānāni parājayavaḥ tūti aparādha adhikaraṇāni dvāviṃśatiḥ teṣām vibhāgaḥ 
NSV_5.2.2	 pratidṛṣṭānta dharma abhyanujñā sva dṛṣṭānte pratijñā hāniḥ pratidṛṣṭāntasya yaḥ dharmaḥ tam yadā sva dṛṣṭānte abhyanujānāti tadā nigṛhītaḥ veditavyaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ aindriyaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti ekaḥ sāmānyam aindriyakam dṛṣṭam nityam kasmāt na tathā śabdaḥ iti dvitīyaḥ yadi sāmānyam aindriyakam nityam ghaṭaḥ api evaḥ tu iti tṛtīyaḥ pakṣaḥ anena kila pratidṛṣṭānta dharmam sva dṛṣṭānte anujānāti tatas ca dṛṣṭāntam jahannigamana antam eva pakṣam jahāti iti pratijñā ahāniḥ iti uccate yat vā dṛṣṭaḥ ca asau ante vyavasthitaḥ ca iti dṛṣṭānta vyutpatyā sva dṛṣṭānta śabdena sva pakṣaḥ eva abhidhīyate pratidṛṣṭānta śabdena pratipakṣaḥ etat uktam bhavati pratipakṣasya yaḥ dharmaḥ tam sva pakṣe abhyanujānāti yathā sāmānyam aindriyakam dṛṣṭam iti śabdopyevam astu iti eṣā pratijñā hāniḥ 
NSV_5.2.3	 pratijñāta artha pratiṣedhe dharma vikalpāt tad artha nirdeśaḥ pratijñāntaram pratijñāta artha pratiṣedhe dharma vikalpāt iti dṛṣṭānta pratidṛṣṭa antayoḥ sādharmya yoge dharma bhedāt sāmānyam aindriyakam sarva gatam asarva gataḥ śabdaḥ iti etasmāt dharma vikalpāt tad artha nirdeśaḥ pratijñāntaram atra anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pūrvā pratijñā asarva gataḥ iti dvitīyā pratijñā pratijñāntaram tat katham nigraha sthānam iti na pratijñāyāḥ sādhanam pratijñāntaram kintu hetu dṛṣṭāntau sādhanam pratijñāyāḥ tat etat asādhana upādānam anarthakam iti 
NSV_5.2.4–5.2.5	 pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ pratijñā virodhaḥ yatra pratijñā hetunā virudhyate hetuḥ ca pratijñayā sa pratijñāvirodhaḥ nāma nigraha sthānam yathā guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam bhedena agrahaṇāt iti pakṣa pratiṣedhe pratijñāta artha apanayanam pratijñāsannyāsaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ endriyaka tvāt iti ukte paraḥ vadet sāmānyam aindriyakam na ca anityam evam śabda upyaindriyakaḥ na ca anityaḥ iti evam pratiṣiddhe pakṣe yadi brūyāt kaḥ punar āha anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti saḥ ayam pratijñāta artha nihnavaḥ pratijñāsannyāsaḥ iti 
NSV_5.2.6^1	 aviśeṣa ukte hetau pratiṣiddhe viśeṣam icchataḥ hetu antaram nidarśanam eka prakṛti idam vyaktam iti pratijñā kasmāt hetoḥ ekaḥ prakṛtīnām vikārāṇām parimāṇāt mṛd pūrvaka ādīnām śarāva ādīnām dṛṣṭam parimāṇam yāvān prakṛte vyūhaḥ bhavati tāvān vikāraḥ iti dṛṣṭam ca prativikāram parimāṇam asti ca idam parimāṇam prativyaktam tad eka prakṛtīnām vikārāṇām parimāṇāt paśyāmaḥ vyaktam idam eka prakṛti iti asya vyabhicāreṇa pratyavasthānam nānā prakṛtīnām eka prakṛtīnām ca vikārāṇām dṛṣṭam parimāṇam iti 
NSV_5.2.6^2	 evam pratyavasthite āha eka pṛkṛti samanvaye sati śarāva ādi vikāraṇām parimāṇa darśanāt sukha duḥkha moha samanvitam hi idam vyaktam parimitam gṛhyate tatra prakṛti antara rūpa samanvaya abhāve sati eka prakṛti tvam iti tat idam aviśeṣa ukte hetau pratiṣiddhe viśeṣam bruvataḥ hetu antaram bhavati sati ca hetu antara vacane sati yadi hetu artha nidarśanaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ upādīyate neda vyaktam eka prakṛti bhavati prakṛti antara upādānāt atha na upādīyate dṛṣṭānte hetu arthesya anidarśitasya sādhaka bhāva anupapatteḥ ānarthakyāt hetoḥ anivṛttam nigraha sthānam iti 
NSV_5.2.7	 prakṛtāt arthāt apratisambaddha artham artha antaram yathā ukta lakṣaṇe pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahe hetutaḥ sādhya siddhau prakṛtāyām brūyāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśa tvāt iti hetuḥ hetuḥ nāma hinoteḥ dhātoḥ tuni pratyaye kṛdanta padam padam ca nāma ākhyāta upasarga nipātāḥ abhidheyasya kriyā antara yogāt viśiṣyamāṇa rūpaḥ śabdaḥ nāma kriyā kāraka samudāyaḥ kāraka saṅghāta viśiṣṭa kriyā kāla yoga abhidhāyi a ākhyātam dhātu artha mātram ca kāla abhidhāna viśiṣṭam prayogeṣu arthāt abhidyamāna rūpāḥ nipātāḥ upasṛjyamānā kriyā avat yotakāḥ upasargaḥ iti evamādi tad artha antaram veditavyam iti 
NSV_5.2.8–5.2.9	 varṇa krama nirdeśa vat nirarthakam yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ kacaṭatapāḥ java gaḍada tvāt jhabhañgaḍa daśa vat iti pavam prakāram nirarthakam abhidhāna abhidheya bhāva anupapattau artha gateḥ abhāvāt varṇāḥ eva krameṇa nirdiśyante iti pariṣad prativādibhyām tris abhihitam api avijñātām avijñāta artham pariṣad prativādibhyām tris abhihitam api na vijñāyate yathā kliṣṭa śabdam apratīta prayogam atidruta uccaritam iti evamādinā kāraṇena tad avijñātam avijñāta artham asāmarthya saṃvaraṇāya prayuktam iti nigraha sthānam iti 
NSV_5.2.10–5.2.13	 paurvāparya ayogāt apratisambaddha artham apārthakam yatra anekasya padasya vākyasya vā paurvāparya yogaḥ na asti iti asambandhāt gṛhyate tat ca samudāya artha abhāvāt apārthakam yathā daśa dāḍimāni paḍa pūpāḥ kuṇḍam ajinam ityādi avayava viparyāsa vacanam aprāpta kālam pratijñā ādīnām avayavānām yathālakṣaṇam artha vaśāt kramaḥ tatra avayava viparyāsena vacanam aprāpta kālam asaṃvaddha artham nigraha sthānam iti hīnam anyatamena api avayavena nyūnam yasmin vākye pratijña ādīnām anyatamaḥ avayavaḥ hīnaḥ bhavati tad vākayam hīnam veditavyam sādhana abhāve sādhya asiddhiḥ iti nigrahaḥ hetu udāharaṇa adhikam adhikam ekena kṛta tvāt anyatarasya ānarthakyam iti tad etat niyama abhyupagame veditavyam iti 
NSV_5.2.14–5.2.15	 śabda arthayoḥ punarvacanam punaruktam anyatra anuvādāt anyatra anuvādāt śabda punaruktam artha punaruktam vā nityaḥ śabdaḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti śabda punaruktam artha punaruktam anityaḥ śabdaḥ nirodha dharmakodhvānaḥ iti anuvāde tu apunaruktam śabda abhyāsāt artha viśeṣa upapatteḥ yathā hetu apadeśāt pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam nigamanam iti arthāt āpannasya sva śabdena punarvacanam punaruktam iti prakṛtam nidarśanam utpatti dharmakam anityam iti uktvā arthāt āpannasya arthasya yaḥ abhidhāyakaḥ śabdaḥ tena sva śabdena brūyāt anutpatti dharmakam nityam iti tat ca punarukta nigraha sthānam bhavati 
NSV_5.2.16–5.2.17	 vijñātasya pariṣada tris abhihitasya api apratyuccāraṇam ananubhāṣaṇam vijñātasya vākya arthasya pariṣadā prativādinā tris abhihitasya yat apratyuccāraṇam tat ananubhāṣaṇam nāma nigraha sthānam iti apratyuccārayan kim āśrayam para pakṣa pratiṣedham brūyāt avijñātam ca ajñānam vijñātasya arthasya pariṣadā prativādinā ca tris abhihitam api yat avijñātam tat ajñānam nāma nigraha sthānam artham khalu ajānan tasya pratiṣedham katham brūyāt iti 
NSV_5.2.18–5.2.19	 uttarasya apratipattiḥ apratibhā para pakṣa pratiṣedhaḥ uttaram śloka pāṭhā ādibhiḥ ajñānam utpādayan yadā tad uttaram na pratipadyate tat apratibhā nāma nigraha sthānam kārya vyāsaṅgāt kathā vicchedaḥ vikṣepaḥ yatra kartavyam kāryam vyāsajya kathām vicchinatti idam me karaṇīyam vidyate paścāt kathayiṣyāmi iti sa vikṣepaḥ nāma nigraha sthānam 
NSV_5.2.20–5.2.21	 sva pakṣe doṣa abhyupagamāt para pakṣe doṣa prasaṅgaḥ mata anujñā yaḥ pareṇa coditam doṣam anuddhṛtya bhavatā upyayam doṣaḥ samānaḥ iti para matam anujānāti sā mata anujñā yathā bhavān= coraḥ iti ukte bhavān api coraḥ iti nigraha sthāna prāptasya anigrahaḥ paryanuyojya upekṣaṇam yaḥ nigraha sthāna prāptam na nigṛhṇāti sa nigṛhītaḥ veditavyaḥ nigraha sthānasya aparijñānāt iti 
NSV_5.2.22–5.2.23	 anigraha sthāne nigraha sthāna abhiyogaḥ niranuyojya anuyogaḥ nigraha sthāna lakṣaṇasya mithyā adhyavasāyāt anigraha sthāne nigṛhītaḥ asi iti param bruvan niranuyojya anuyogāt nigṛhītaḥ veditavyaḥ siddhāntam abhyupetya aniyamāt kathā prasaṅgaḥ apasiddhāntaḥ kasyacid arthasya tathā abhāvam pratijñāya pratijñāta artha viparyayāt aniyamāt kathām prasañjayataḥ apasiddhāntaḥ 
NSV_5.2.24	 hetu abhāsāḥ ca yathā uktā yathā eva vibhaktā lakṣaṇena tathā eva teṣām nigraha sthāna bhāvaḥ iti te khalu ime pramāṇa ādayaḥ padārthāḥ uddiṣṭāḥ prathama sūtre lakṣitāḥ prathame adhyāye parīkṣitāḥ śeṣeṣu iti trividhā tatvasya parisamāptiḥ uktā veditavyā jātīnām sapta pañcānām nigraha sthāna lakṣaṇam śāstrasya ca upasaṃhāraḥ pañcame parikīrtitaḥ
